Chapter 753: Metamorphic Immortal Grass

“Hero Yan, you’ve just broken through, and your foundation is unstable. The most urgent matter now is to find a quiet place to go into seclusion,” Lu Yang advised kindly.

“You’re right, Daoist.” Hero Yan felt immense respect for Lu Yang. With the arrival of Lu Yang’s group, Fangshan Island had gained a fifth-grade spirit vein, and he had successfully passed the lightning tribulation and become a Divine Transfiguration cultivator.

With the help of the fifth-grade spirit vein, his two brothers also had a small chance of cultivating to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

I never expected that kindly informing them about True Lord Horse’s banquet would yield such returns.

Wait, now that I think about it, True Lord Horse’s banquet seemed to have been just this morning.

Hero Yan sorted through the day’s events.

Morning: Attended True Lord Horse’s banquet.

Noon: Invited Lu Yang’s group to Fangshan Island.

Afternoon: Spirit vein anomaly, emergence of immortal grass.

Night: Twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators attacked, and I took the Divine Concentration Pill to become a Divine Transfiguration cultivator.

“What should we do with the Metamorphic Immortal Grass? Do we bring it back or consume it now?” Lu Yang and the others gestured toward the Metamorphic Immortal Grass, considering which option was more beneficial.

“How about plucking a leaf to taste and see how many years of cultivation it boosts?” Li Haoran had heard of the Metamorphic Immortal Grass, but it was his first time seeing it, much less consuming it.

Lu Yang shook his head, turning down Li Haoran’s idea. “The immortal grass is precious. If we pluck a leaf without a proper sealing method, the medicinal properties will leak through the opening, and the gain won’t be worth the loss.

“If we consume all of it, we can indeed quickly increase our cultivation, but we’ll lack some stabilization, which would hinder our future cultivation.”

Generally, the Metamorphic Immortal Grass was consumed by Fusion or Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Reaching Great Perfection in these two cultivation realms didn’t require comprehension but gradual, time-consuming efforts.

“In my opinion, it’s better to bring it back to the sect and ask for Big Senior Sister’s view.”

Everyone nodded; that sounded like a plan.

Lu Yang stored the immortal grass in a wooden box and affixed several talismans.

~~~

When night fell and all was quiet, the wooden box shook incessantly, as if an invisible hand was touching it.

The box opened, and the immortal grass shook its head, then stealthily climbed out of the box.

It looked up at Lu Yang, who was cultivating in the lotus position, and smiled with contempt.

“You want to eat me? Dream on.”

Despite saying this, it remained cautious, gingerly climbing down from the bed. The moment it tried to push open the window, a lamp lit up, illuminating the room.

A chilling voice came from behind the immortal grass.

“As I thought, it is an immortal grass that has gained sentience.”

The Metamorphic Immortal Grass jerked its head around and saw Lu Yang with an uncanny smile.

Whoosh, whoosh, whoosh, whoosh. Four figures appeared in the room, surrounding the Metamorphic Immortal Grass.

“Senior Brother Lu, you guessed it correctly. This is a little herb king.” Tao Yaoye’s searing gaze bore into the Metamorphic Immortal Grass.

“I never expected us to find a little herb king in the East Sea,” Li Haoran marveled. Immortal grasses were rare to begin with, and this one was at the level of a little herb king. Even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would go crazy fighting over it.

“This is my first time seeing a little herb king. Is it tasty?” Man Gu had never been to the herb garden.

Earlier, when they were openly discussing what they should do with the immortal grass, Lu Yang had secretly transmitted an auditory message to the others, informing them about his suspicion that it was a little herb king-level immortal grass.

At night, when the immortal grass heard they were taking it back to the sect, it stopped pretending and exposed itself.

In fact, Lu Yang didn’t suspect it—he had simply heard from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that the immortal grass’s age indicated it was planted in ancient times. Its owner was probably that tyrannical holy son who was a big bully, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had beaten him up.

That holy son also possessed the Metamorphic Immortal Physique. Seeing that he was no match for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he borrowed power from his future self, raising his realm to the Void Refinement Stage.

Then, he got a worse thrashing.

“He probably planted it here in the ancient era. But after I beat him up a few times, his brain got addled, and he forgot where he planted the immortal grass,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy analyzed with conviction, and it actually made some sense.

Lu Yang felt that this Kunlun Holy Son was truly unlucky.

Since the immortal grass had grown from ancient times until now, it was obvious it would have gained sentience and become a demon spirit. These sentient spirit plants inherently yearned for freedom. They spent their entire lives rooted in the soil, unable to run. Once they got the rare opportunity to run, they naturally wanted to roam around and play.

The Metamorphic Immortal Grass usually moved around Fangshan Island via the spirit vein. Otherwise, the legend of a rare treasure in the spirit vein wouldn’t have appeared on Fangshan Island. freewebnovel.com

This time, it resonated with Tao Yaoye, which allowed Lu Yang and the others to discover its existence. Realizing it could be taken away, it played dead during the day to lull them into letting their guard down, planning to escape at night.

Unfortunately, its plan failed.

“Who planted you back then?” Meng Jingzhou asked curiously.

“Human, watch your tone!” The Metamorphic Immortal Grass looked down on short-lived species like humans. Of course, demons were also short-lived species in its eyes.

A ball of pure yang flame burst forth from Meng Jingzhou’s palm, his tone icy. “Should we roast and eat it?”

My barbecue skills aren’t rusty, not to mention that the three great founders of One More Time Barbeque Shop are all here.

Man Gu tactfully whipped out the Man Family’s eighteen-generation ancestral seasoning. If he was lucky, he could even have the first old ancestor of the barbecue Barbarian clan possess him.

Feeling the scorching flame, the Metamorphic Immortal Grass flapped its leaves, trying to extinguish the fire in Meng Jingzhou’s palm, saying with an ingratiating smile, “I was just joking. Why can’t you take a joke?

“Don’t blame me for not saying; I really don’t know who planted me. When I was planted, I wasn’t a little herb king yet.”

Lu Yang nodded. This was the truth. If the Metamorphic Immortal Grass had been a little herb king in the ancient era, the Kunlun Holy Son would have carried the flowerpot with him everywhere, every day.

“Immortal Fairy, is the Kunlun Holy Son still alive? Should we return it to its original owner?” Despite being in the treacherous East Sea, Lu Yang hadn’t lost his conscience.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved dismissively, “No need; he’s already dead. According to ancient rules, this immortal grass should belong to me. But I have no use for this thing, so I’ll give it to you youngsters.”

Lu Yang’s heart skipped a beat. The Battle of the Great Era in ancient times was truly brutal. Even someone as strong as the person with the Metamorphic Immortal Physique died at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s hands. Moreover, judging by her tone, this Kunlun Holy Son wasn’t even considered a formidable opponent.

“That was when I was still a half-immortal. The Kunlun Holy Son—oh, he was already the Holy Lord then—he insisted on fighting me. As usual, he couldn’t beat me, so he kept using his Metamorphic Immortal Physique to borrow power from his future self.”

“And then you beat him to death?”

“Nothing of the sort. He borrowed power from his future self and ended up borrowing until he died.”

Lu Yang was flummoxed, completely unable to understand what had happened.

Seeing Lu Yang so obtuse, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy patiently explained, “His future self was already dead. When he borrowed power from his future self, he also borrowed his death state, causing his present self to die as well.

“See, doesn’t that create a closed loop?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Wait, why is my brain even more confused now?

Immortal Fairy, do you even have any opponents who are normal people?

Chapter 754: A Safe Journey

Lu Yang’s group had surrounded the Metamorphic Immortal Grass. With Meng Jingzhou brandishing Pure Yang True Fire while eyeing it like a tiger watching its prey, it knew it had no chance of escape. It let out a long sigh and resigned itself to its fate.

“Alright, alright, I won’t run.”

Compared to being roasted and eaten now, being taken back and tended to is clearly the path to survival.

“That’s more like it.” Seeing the Metamorphic Immortal Grass behave, Meng Jingzhou clenched his fist, withdrawing the flame.

Man Gu also tactfully put away the barbeque seasoning. He had switched through several old ancestors earlier but hadn’t yet reached the first-generation ancestor of the Barbeque Man family.

“But let’s be clear upfront. You can’t eat me, at least not all of me.” The Metamorphic Immortal Grass stared at the five warily.

“That’s a given.”

Little herb king-level immortal grasses were extremely precious. Who would eat all of it in one go when it could be harvested for a steady supply? The little herb kings in the herb garden were all living well. At most, a few leaves or roots would be plucked from them when needed, never harming the main body.

“Is your promise reliable?” The Metamorphic Immortal Grass looked at Lu Yang suspiciously. During the fight with the Divine Transfiguration cultivators, I had seen clearly that you have the most tricks up your sleeve, kid.

“I swear by the Heaven Mandate Immortal—if I lied just now, may the Heaven Mandate Immortal strike you with heavenly lightning!” Lu Yang raised three fingers and swore to the heavens.

“So ruthless?!”

The Metamorphic Immortal Grass was shocked by Lu Yang’s audacity to make such a deadly oath. It shook its leaves twice, equivalent to it nodding in belief.

“Don't worry, we won’t treat you poorly. Our sect has several little herb kings,” Li Haoran said with a chuckle. As the reincarnation of Creed Leader Qin, he had learned the latter’s art of managing people—to make subordinates obedient, one needed both the stick and the carrot.

He had also learned Creed Leader Qin’s skill of giving carrots that weren’t tangible.

“Junior Sister Tao, since you have a connection with the immortal grass, how about we entrust it to you until we return to the sect?” Lu Yang suggested with a smile.

A little herb king couldn’t be stored in a storage ring; it could only be carried in a box within a bundle. He already had the Everlasting Immortal Fairy chattering in his ear and didn’t want another little herb king added to the mix.

“Thank you for your trust then, Senior Brother Lu.” Tao Yaoye happily accepted the task. Being with a little herb king will certainly broaden my horizons.

Little herb kings hadn’t lived so long for nothing. The Metamorphic Immortal Grass had its own unique method of concealing its aura. Even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator couldn’t detect it with their spiritual consciousness.

~~~

A day later, Hero Yan emerged from seclusion, having consolidated his realm. He was now a bona fide Divine Transfiguration cultivator.

Usually, one would be in high spirits and full of vigor after advancing to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, but Hero Yan wasn’t. He maintained a humble heart.

After all, the feat of Lu Yang’s group of five capturing twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators alive while at the Nascent Soul Stage was still a vivid memory in his mind.

“Hero Yan, are you going to Penglai Island to upgrade your position? Could you take the five of us along?” Lu Yang asked politely.

Hero Yan was an administrator in the East Sea Cultivator Alliance. Now that he had advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, he could apply to be promoted to hall leader.

Having come all the way to the East Sea, we have to visit Penglai Island at least once.

With the map provided by the old horse, they knew how to get to Penglai Island, but they were unfamiliar with the place. It was better to have Hero Yan introduce it to them.

“Of course,” Hero Yan quickly replied.

He gave some instructions to the other two heroes and prepared to set off for Penglai Island.

Penglai Island was very far from Fangshan Island. In the past, Hero Yan needed to stop several times to rest when flying to Penglai Island. But after successfully advancing to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, his dantian had expanded, and his spirit energy was now abundant. He no longer needed to go through such trouble.

~~~

“...Daoists...slow down.” Hero Yan yelled breathlessly as he gazed helplessly at the five flying ahead.

He was sitting on a painting that swayed unsteadily, as if it might plunge into the sea at any moment. He never expected that his spirit energy as a Divine Transfiguration cultivator was less than that of Lu Yang and the others. Having just advanced, he didn’t have any Divine Transfiguration-tier Qi Replenishment Pills on hand.

Lu Yang was standing on his flying sword. As he spun sharply, two trails of water splashed from the sea’s surface and stopped in front of Hero Yan with style.

“Hero Yan, are you alright?”

“S-slow down.”

Seeing Hero Yan was out of energy, the five decided to slow down.

Just then, a hundred-meter-long giant whale surfaced, its blowhole spraying a hundred-zhang water column. Under the sunlight, it displayed a rainbow of colors.

“Why does it feel like we keep seeing this kind of whale along the way?”

“These are whales domesticated by the alliance. Such whales have special bellies that can carry people. They’re expensive; even Qi Training cultivators can’t afford them. I rode one when I was at the Golden Core Stage. As my cultivation improved, the whale’s swimming speed couldn’t keep up with mine, so I stopped riding them.

“This sea route leads to Penglai Island, which is why we keep seeing them.”

Lu Yang nodded. It seems these whales are equivalent to Great Xia’s flying vessels.

“Hero Yan, if you really have no energy left, how about taking a ride inside the whale’s belly?” Man Gu kindly suggested.

Hero Yan nodded feebly. He wasn’t short on money now. It was just that recalling his high spirits at the start of the journey made him feel a bit embarrassed.

~~~

The six of them successfully arrived at Penglai Island. Their journey had been peaceful and uneventful.

Except for when they entered a whale’s belly and coincidentally encountered the whale being hijacked by plundering cultivators who demanded that all passengers hand over their belongings. Later, Lu Yang and the others righteously intervened and discovered a group of armed escorts disguised as ordinary cultivators, responsible for transporting goods. The plundering cultivators’ target was precisely this shipment. They robbed everyone to cover up their true motive.

And except for when the whale accidentally entered a sea vortex and was transported to an unknown secret domain, where a Fusion Stage demon was sealed. It was later discovered that a passenger had long been bewitched by the demon and had deliberately lured everyone into the secret domain as a sacrifice. Fortunately, among the passengers was the only daughter of a Fusion Stage True Lord. She had run away from home and disguised herself as a man, chatting jovially with Lu Yang and the others. When the daughter met with danger, her father came to the rescue, dealt with the demon, and sent everyone and the whale back to their original sea route. The daughter then had to bid farewell to Lu Yang and the others.

And except for when Hero Yan regained his energy and left the whale, only to come across a battle between the Sea Rabbit Tribe and the Clam Tribe during their flight. The war started because the Clam Tribe had lost a supreme treasure, and suspicion fell on the Sea Rabbit Tribe. Lu Yang later discovered that the lost treasure was the same goods the armed escorts from before were transporting. After retrieving the supreme treasure, the war ceased. Through meticulous analysis, Lu Yang deduced that the Clam Tribe Chieftain’s daughter was responsible. According to her confession, she had fallen in love with someone outside, which wasn’t recognized by her tribe. To seek revenge, she stole the clam pearl, inciting the war. The previous group of plundering cultivators had been arranged by her lover.

~~~

“We’ve finally arrived at Penglai Island. The public security in the East Sea is really poor. We encountered so many incidents despite just riding a whale,” Lu Yang grumbled softly.

Meng Jingzhou and the other three nodded in agreement, commenting that the East Sea’s environment was far inferior to Great Xia’s.

Hero Yan looked at the five with a strange expression. I rode whales countless times when I was at the Foundation Establishment and Golden Core Stages and never encountered a single incident.

Is it too late to distance myself from them now?

If all else fails, I can even cripple my own cultivation; the spirit vein can be downgraded too.

Chapter 755: Bounty Notices

As the headquarters of the East Sea Cultivators Alliance and the largest human faction in the East Sea, Penglai Island was truly magnificent. An endless stream of whales docked at the shore, their mouths opening to let groups of cultivators emerge.

The island’s residents were still predominantly mortals, but cultivators were not scarce. Qi Training and Foundation Establishment cultivators could be seen everywhere. Compared to here, Fangshan Island was as different as mud to clouds.

The island lord of Penglai Island was a veteran Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. According to Great Xia’s classification, Penglai Island was considered an S-tier faction, of which there were only nine in all of Great Xia.

Moreover, Penglai Island gathered the vast majority of East Sea cultivators and possessed a profound foundation, making it several times stronger than the S-class sects in Great Xia.

Hero Yan arrived at the alliance headquarters, which was a nine-story pagoda. The pagoda was rustic and simple, having weathered countless years. Each story was carved with talismans, arrays, or diagrams encompassing Great Dao principles, embodying the mysteries of heaven and earth’s laws. Any person standing before the pagoda would appear as small as an ant.

“Daoists, I will enter the alliance to register first. After my business is concluded, I shall take you all on a tour of Penglai Island. Does that work?” Hero Yan asked, cupping his fists. Non-alliance members were not permitted to enter the pagoda.

“No problem, no problem. Attend to your matters first, Hero Yan,” Lu Yang replied cheerfully. They were in no hurry.

Divine Transfiguration cultivators carried some weight in the alliance. After Hero Yan entered the nine-story pagoda and explained his situation, a Divine Transfiguration cultivator soon came out to receive him. Hearing that Hero Yan had passed the lightning tribulation through his own efforts, the cultivator’s words held a bit more respect.

Lu Yang called out to the others. “Let’s go. Hero Yan has his own business to attend to. We’ll explore on our own first.” He reckoned that lacking a local guide probably wouldn’t matter much.

“Take a look, freshly caught Nine-Star Lightning Eel!” Someone yelled as he held up a dark, gleaming eel that was over a meter long. It had four spots on each side and one right in the center of its head—a fairly rare Nine-Star Lightning Eel.

“Old uncle, how much for this Nine-Star Lightning Eel?”

The old uncle chuckled and casually uttered, “Not for sale.”

The person was annoyed. “Then why are you shouting about it?!”

“If I don’t shout, how would you know I caught a Nine-Star Lightning Eel?”

“Ancient pills freshly dug from a secret domain, one hundred thousand spirit stones per bottle!” Someone had several small medicinal bottles in front of him, still covered in mud.

This was a common practice in the cultivation world. Bottles of pills unearthed from secret domains were sold unopened, and buyers had to gamble on whether the pills inside were good or bad. This was also a way to test one’s discernment.

“There are ancient pills here,” Tao Yaoye exclaimed softly, quite surprised.

The Metamorphic Immortal Grass was full of contempt. “What ancient pills? Only the mud is ancient.” As a little herb king that has lived from ancient times until now, I’ve eaten who knows how much dirt in my lifetime. I can tell the era of the mud at a glance, without tasting it.

“Barbeque skewers! Freshly grilled lamb skewers! Eat one to prolong your lifespan, eat two to break through cultivation realms, and eat three to achieve longevity!”

Hearing the familiar hawking, Lu Yang instinctively turned his head and found a One More Time Barbeque Shop by the roadside.

“The barbeque shop has opened here too?” Meng Jingzhou was astonished. The Nine-Netherworlds Creed is really working hard to make money, expanding overseas business all the way to Penglai Island.

Lu Yang shook his head, his expression grave. “Our barbeque doesn’t smell like this, and the fire used isn’t true fire. This is a counterfeit.”

Apart from that, Lu Yang also spotted flying cars without trademarks, unauthorized Dreamlike Bubble Mirages...All were counterfeits.

Great Xia strictly managed copyrights, but the East Sea was not like that. The latter’s principle was that as long as something made money, even money and arson were normal, let alone protecting intellectual property.

It was precisely because of this that pill formulas, arrays, and the like in Great Xia had strict master-disciple lineages. Unauthorized external dissemination meant certain death.

Lu Yang calculated that he had lost at least eight million stones in the East Sea. His heart ached. Eight million! That’s enough to buy Old Meng’s dog life!

Meng Jingzhou glanced sideways at Lu Yang. I keep feeling like this brat is talking badly about me.

Li Haoran comforted him kindly. “The East Sea is like this. You just have to get used to it. Back then, Qin Haoran made a fortune by dealing in counterfeits in the East Sea. That’s where the money for his marriage to Yiren came from.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Why is Shifu’s portrait here?” Lu Yang noticed a poster of the Taciturn Daoist Priest on the announcement board. Looking at the heading, it was a bounty notice.

Taciturn Daoist Priest, Dao-Seeking Sect Leader

Bounty: One billion spirit stones

The bounty was even jointly issued by the seafolk and humans.

“I’d long heard that Shifu fetches a high price on the black market. Now that I’ve seen it today, it truly is the case,” Lu Yang remarked. One billion spirit stones—that’s much more than Old Meng’s eight million.

Aside from the Taciturn Daoist Priest, there were many familiar faces on the wanted posters, such as First Elder, Sixth Elder, Seventh Elder, and Eighth Elder.

Half of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s higher-ups were here. Of course, their bounties couldn’t compare to the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s. The latter firmly secured the top spot, his position unshakable.

Before leaving, Lu Yang had heard Grandpa Ba mention the elders’ stories.

First Elder had valiantly gone in and out of tombs at Penglai, Fangzhang, and Yingzhou multiple times. He even built one on an island in the East Sea. When the three islands discovered the tomb, they all thought it was their own ancient burial site and fought until the contents of their brains nearly spilled out. In the end, Penglai Island won and triumphantly brought the coffin back. They spent a long time comparing it to their genealogy and knelt and bowed to the coffin... and then First Elder pushed open the coffin lid from within and sat up...

Sixth Elder was in the midst of a breakthrough with her Immaculate Immortal Physique at the time, and her Immaculate Field was quite unstable and activated by voice. When she attended a banquet, the host’s speech triggered the Immaculate Field to open. Every time someone spoke, the field opened. From then on, she was blacklisted from banquets.

Seventh Elder and Eighth Elder exploited the fact that Great Xia’s laws didn’t extend to the East Sea and roamed about scamming people, their deception skills growing by the day. Eventually, the East Sea couldn’t tolerate it anymore. After multiple failed attempts to capture them, they asked Great Xia to exercise personal jurisdiction and bring them to justice. However, Great Xia refused to handle the case, citing respect for the East Sea’s sovereignty.

Passers-by noticed the wanted posters and found them nostalgic, recalling past events. “I didn’t think the Taciturn Daoist Priest would still be posted here. It’s been centuries; he hasn’t shown his face in the East Sea for two hundred years, right?”

“Exactly. Remember when the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s bounty was five hundred million spirit stones? He pretended to be captured, and together with the Dao-Seeking Sect’s First Elder, they swindled the bounty money.”

“Since then, his bounty has risen to one billion. And whenever there was news of him, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator would personally lead the capture team.”

“One billion spirit stones! If someone could catch the Taciturn Daoist Priest, they wouldn’t have to worry about cultivation resources for several lifetimes.”

“Catch the Taciturn Daoist Priest? You really can dream. I heard that some cultivators committed crimes under the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s name in the past. After that incident, even plundering cultivators don’t dare to use his name anymore.”

Lu Yang was glad that they were currently using the identity of Five-Elements Sect disciples.

Given the relationship between the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Five-Elements Sect, the Five-Elements Sect likely couldn’t do much even if they minded.

Chapter 756: Stepping Stones

“My shifu is still the reliable one; he’s not on the bounty notices,” Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, and Li Haoran said with smug confidence.

Only Lu Yang’s and Tao Yaoye’s masters were on the wanted posters.

Lu Yang didn’t speak, silently walking around to the back of the announcement board, where the bounties for Third Elder, Fourth Elder, and Fifth Elder were posted, priced slightly lower than those on the front.

“...Our sect has been completely wiped out.” Meng Jingzhou clicked his tongue.

Lu Yang furrowed his brows, berating Meng Jingzhou for his inappropriate choice of words. “What do you mean by ‘our sect?’ The bounty notices are all for the Dao-Seeking Sect. What does that have to do with our Five-Elements Sect?”

Li Haoran nodded repeatedly, finding Lu Yang’s words to make sense.

“Besides, it’s not a complete wipeout. Grandpa Ba doesn’t have a bounty on his head.”

Grandpa Ba hadn’t lied. He was the sole survivor among the Dao-Seeking Sect’s higher-ups.

Witnessing how dangerous the East Sea was, the five verified their cover story again, confirming they were all Five-Elements Sect disciples. Even if they encountered Qiu Jin’an, they would publicly address him as “Sect Leader” first.

Lu Yang felt that given his life-and-death friendship with Qiu Jin’an in Hanshui City, the latter probably wouldn’t mind such a trivial matter.

Before the five moved away from the announcement board, they overheard passers-by discussing other topics.

“The Immortal Appraisal Convention is coming up soon.”

“What Immortal Appraisal Convention? It’s just an event for the Three Islands’ disciples to spread their fame.”

“What else can we do? The Three Islands’ disciples are far superior to us in both cultivation talent and resources. At the same realm, who can defeat them?”

“But they shouldn’t step on the heads of us ordinary cultivators to spread their fame.”

“Just accept fate.”

~~~

“Are so many people on Penglai Island because of that Immortal Appraisal Convention?”

“Probably.”

“Hmm, this magical treasure looks a little interesting.” Li Haoran discovered an exquisitely crafted magical treasure at a blacksmith. It was a metal lotus, and judging by its structure, it should be a covert weapon. Its forging concept was completely different from that in Great Xia, so he decided to purchase it for research.

“How much for this magical treasure?”

“I’m buying this magical treasure.” A voice sounded from behind.

Everyone turned to see a cultivator dressed elegantly, with three wave patterns on his sleeves. The cultivator was handsome and at the Nascent Soul Stage. Behind him stood several attendants, all at the Nascent Soul Stage except for one at the Divine Transfiguration Stage. Among the attendants Lu Yang had encountered, they were considered to have high-level cultivation.

“Who are you?” Li Haoran frowned, finding this person rude.

“So it’s Fellow Daoist Fan Chong. Please excuse me for not coming out to welcome you properly,” the shop owner said with an apologetic smile as he came out.

“Spare the nonsense. I’m buying this iron lotus. I can use it at the convention later. How much does it cost?” The cultivator named Fan Chong didn’t even glance at Li Haoran.

“If it were someone else buying, it’d be 280,000 spirit stones. But since it’s you, it’ll be the cost price—10,000 spirit stones.”

Fan Chong signaled with a look, and an attendant took out ten thousand spirit stones to buy the magical treasure. Even then, the shop owner saw him off with a smile.

After Fan Chong left, the shop owner breathed a sigh of relief and looked at Li Haoran with lingering fear. “Fortunately, you didn’t fight with him over that magical treasure. If you had angered him, you might not be able to leave Penglai Island.”

“Who is he? Is he famous?”

“You’re not locals, are you? Penglai Island disciples are divided into outer, inner, and core, identifiable by the wave patterns on their sleeves. That cultivator just now, Fan Chong, is a core disciple of Penglai Island.

“And Fan Chong is extremely special even among core disciples. He is a disciple of the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest, whose father is the legendary Penglai Island Lord.”

Lu Yang understood. So he’s the grand-disciple of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. No wonder he’s so arrogant.

Quite the entourage, bringing so many Nascent Soul attendants when going out. Look at me, my shifu is Yun Zhi, but I always keep a low profile when traveling.

The shop owner sighed. “If not for his special status, someone would have already seized his Dreamlike Bubble Mirage and flying carriage businesses.”

Lu Yang nodded and said nothing more.

The five left the shop and continued strolling through the streets.

~~~

After half a day, they originally wanted to check out the Immortal Appraisal Convention, but it was organized by the Three Islands; entry was not permitted without an invitation.

Just as Lu Yang and the others were considering whether to employ some tricks to peek at the Immortal Appraisal Convention, a disciple dressed in Penglai Island-style attire blocked their path. The disciple had two wave patterns on his sleeves and deliberately released an oppressive aura of the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

“Who are you?” Lu Yang eyed him warily.

That disciple didn’t answer, coldly staring at the group. In his mind, he mused: Nascent Soul cultivators I haven’t seen before, likely not cultivators from our Three Islands. Just in time; a few are severely injured and won’t recover anytime soon. I’ll use you five to make up the numbers first.

“Hey, you five are in luck. I’ll take you to the Immortal Appraisal Convention later. If you perform well, you might be noticed by our Penglai Island disciples or elders and become attendants.”

The disciple’s attitude was forceful. Without letting Lu Yang and the others say anything, he took them flying toward the core area of Penglai Island.

Lu Yang and the others were merely Nascent Soul cultivators; how could they resist a Divine Transfiguration cultivator?

On the way, through the disciple’s fragmented words, Lu Yang learned his name was Xu Ze and that he was taking them to the Immortal Appraisal Convention. The convention was quite grand and invited various experts, including East Sea cultivators and even Great Xia cultivators.

Although it was called the Immortal Appraisal Convention, its main purpose was to spread the fame of the Three Islands’ disciples. Penglai Island disciples were elites among cultivators, hailed as seeds of the Immortal Dao. They possessed extraordinary combat power, and the best way to prove this was to challenge cultivators at the same level and take on multiple opponents at once.

Unfortunately, Lu Yang’s group belonged to the “multiple” opponents to be challenged, commonly referred to as stepping stones.

Defeating Lu Yang’s group would naturally spread their fame.

The main venue of the Immortal Appraisal Convention was a circular arena stage. There were passages on both sides, one for the Three Island disciples to enter, and the other for ordinary Nascent Soul cultivators.

The Immortal Appraisal Convention had already been underway for a while. As the Three Islands disciples were too heavy-handed in their strikes, over a dozen ordinary cultivators were unable to continue participating. Thus, Penglai Island sent people to capture over a dozen cultivators to fill in temporarily, and Lu Yang’s group was among them.

“I thought there would be immortals or at least half-immortals. But it turns out to be just a bunch of self-proclaimed Immortal Dao seeds participating in the convention.” Lu Yang yawned.

You Three Islands are really daring with your names.

They were waiting in a rest area on one side of the arena. Originally, they wanted to teach these ordinary Nascent Soul cultivators how to fight, but they were very vigilant and unwilling to speak with Lu Yang’s group.

Lu Yang could see that Xu Ze hadn’t been making empty promises by painting pictures of flatbreads. Ordinary cultivators who performed well at the Immortal Appraisal Convention did have a chance to join Penglai Island. This was why they viewed Lu Yang and the others as rivals, resulting in their wariness.

Just as Lu Yang and the others were bored waiting and considering whether to have an internal fight among themselves, it was finally their turn to go on stage.

“Hey, you five, it’s your turn. Hurry up.”

Lu Yang’s group walked through the passage toward the arena and saw their opponent.

They had just encountered him half a day ago.

Fan Chong.

Chapter 757: Rotational Battle of Attrition

“To think it’s Fan Chong, a core disciple, this time. These five Nascent Soul cultivators are out of luck.”

“Fan Chong’s combat talent is quite rare even among core disciples. He has never encountered a match at the same level.”

“Exactly. I heard that although Fan Chong is at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage, he can exchange a hundred blows with a Basic Divine Transfiguration cultivator before losing. Challenging beyond one’s level, especially those at a major realm higher—that’s the caliber of an ancient genius.”

“Hiss, that strong?”

“How could he not be? His shifu is the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest, the only daughter of the Penglai Island Lord. Forget Penglai Island; few in the entire East Sea dare to provoke her.”

“The Immortal Appraisal Convention appraises Immortal Dao seeds. It appears Fan Chong is the most likely candidate to become an Immortal Dao seed in this cohort.”

Lu Yang and the others had excellent hearing. Challenging beyond one’s level? This Fan Chong won’t be easy to deal with.

As the eldest senior brother among the five, Lu Yang analyzed the situation, seeking a way to victory. “In my opinion, although Fan Chong’s combat power is extremely strong, his spirit energy isn’t abundant. As long as we engage him in a battle of attrition by rotating ourselves, we can wear him down eventually!”

“Alright!” Meng Jingzhou was the first to support Lu Yang.

Man Gu was befuddled. Is Fan Chong really as strong as Brother Lu says? Does he have a hidden trump card I couldn’t see?

Or is it a case of 'a lion should use all its strength even when catching a rabbit?’

“So it’s you five.” Fan Chong sneered coldly. He never expected the passers-by he saw in a shop to become his opponents. Seems like we’re really fated.

“All five of you, come at me!” Fan Chong lifted his chin. Given my status, my reputation is already sufficient. What I need now is an overwhelming victory to solidify my image. Only then can I become famous in one go at the Immortal Appraisal Convention and be remembered by the world.

“See? He wants a quick battle. It must be because his power is insufficient,” Lu Yang continued to analyze calmly. “This battle is dangerous. How about this? Since I’m the big senior brother, I’ll go first to scout the path for you.”

Just as Fan Chong was wondering why the five opposite him weren’t fighting him, Lu Yang’s figure transformed into a lightning bolt, speeding over and reaching him in the blink of an eye.

“So fast!” Fan Chong was stunned, instinctively raising his sword to block. He was a sword cultivator.

“Teach you to make flying carriages without my permission!” Lu Yang used his fingers as a sword, bringing two fingers together to release a strand of sword qi.

The sword qi was like a dragon, exceedingly domineering. It collided with Fan Chong’s long sword, producing a metallic clang and forcing Fan Chong several steps back.

If Lu Yang was facing talisman, array, or physique cultivators, he would use the Qingfeng Sword. But since his opponent was a sword cultivator at the same level, Lu Yang didn’t even need to use a real sword.

“Teach you to make flying carriages without paying me royalty fees!” Lu Yang’s resentment surged to the heavens. Eight million stones! I’m not short on money, but seeing my money end up in someone else’s pocket doesn’t make me happy.

“Arhat Fist!” Lu Yang combined fists and sword. Regardless of whether Fan Chong used his sword to block or attack, Lu Yang anticipated his moves in advance. From the start of the fight, Fan Chong never managed to lift his wrist properly.

Simultaneously, his hair fell out in large clumps, dropping onto the ground.

“My hair!” Fan Chong cried out. He always paid particular attention to his appearance. How can I face people like this?

“Whew, he’s really not easy to deal with.” Lu Yang pretended to pant a few times, signaling for Meng Jingzhou to go next.

Meng Jingzhou’s attacks were heavy enough to leave Fan Chong bruised and swollen.

“Even this young master isn’t as ostentatious as you when going out. Just look at you, thinking you’re all that!”

Then came Tao Yaoye, Man Gu, and Li Haoran.

Broadcasting Dreamlike Bubble Mirages without permission was no different from outright robbery. Even with Tao Yaoye’s good temper, fury rose within her.

Man Gu was inspired by Lu Yang’s actions, understanding the principle of using full force even against a weak opponent, just like a lion catching a rabbit. Possessed by his ancestor, he struck with exceptional ferocity.

Li Haoran had an extremely poor impression of Fan Chong and blazed with true fire, but he still held back; otherwise, Fan Chong would have died long ago.

Their rotational battle of attrition plan proceeded smoothly. Fan Chong looked utterly miserable, as if he had been run over by a large truck five times.

“I’ll make you pay!” Fan Chong revealed a vicious expression, and an iron lotus flew out from his sleeve.

The iron lotus bloomed, shooting out eighteen petals, each laced with lethal poison!

Li Haoran’s palms manifested Six Ding Divine Fire and Extreme Calculation True Fire. His jade-like palms caught the iron petals and instantly refined them into his own magical treasure before hurling them back.

Fan Chong let out a blood-curdling scream and fell to the ground, convulsing from the poison.

The invited spectating cultivators were shocked, wondering if they had entered an illusion.

“Who are these five? Each one can overpower Fan Chong!”

“Are they concealing their cultivation realms?”

“No, they’re genuinely at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage!”

“How did five such peerless prodigies suddenly appear?”

“Could it be that Fan Chong isn’t actually that strong? Was it all rumors?”

Fan Chong wailed. “Shifu, kill them! Kill them!”

He showed a venomous expression. Since they’ve made me completely lose face at the Immortal Appraisal Convention, they shouldn’t dream of leaving Penglai Island alive!

Penglai Island is my territory!

“Insulting my disciple like this—do you think our Penglai Island has no one?” A pretty-looking female cultivator on the viewing platform said insipidly, gazing frostily at Li Haoran. Her chest revealed some cleavage, highlighting her tall, alluring figure. Such attire was common in the East Sea and not out of line.

The woman flew down from the platform. It was none other than Fan Chong’s shifu, the only daughter of the Penglai Island Lord, the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest.

At the moment, no one had any lustful thoughts about the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest’s figure. She released her oppressive pressure, displaying the might of a Fusion Stage True Lord.

Even Lu Yang and the other four were enveloped by the oppressive pressure and unable to move.

“Shifu!” Seeing his shifu step forth, Fan Chong seemed to see hope.

The Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest didn’t even glance at him. She extended her slender, fair fingers and lifted Li Haoran, who was rooted to the spot, and scrutinized him.

She smiled seductively and said in a bewitching voice, “You are quite handsome. If you become my male concubine, this matter can be written off.”

A question mark popped out of Meng Jingzhou’s head.

Lu Yang pondered. Openly taking male concubines so brazenly...is this also a distinctive feature of the East Sea?

Might as well since we’ve come all this way. Why not let Junior Brother Li experience it?

Li Haoran looked back in despair, seeking help from Lu Yang and the others, but unfortunately, they were unable to assist.

“Junior Brother Li, just yield to her. We will remember your contribution,” Lu Yang encouraged Li Haoran.

LI Haoran grew even more desperate. I knew you guys couldn’t be relied on.

Just as Li Haoran was considering whether to struggle a bit before yielding to the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest or to be all docile and obedient from the start, another cold voice came from the viewing platform.

“Mystic Spirit, take your dirty hands away.”

Another female figure jumped down from the high platform, releasing an oppressive pressure that dispersed the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest’s. The crowd secretly breathed a sigh of relief.

That woman shielded Li Haoran behind her, watching the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest warily.

“Fellow Daoist Su, this is an internal matter of Penglai Island. This isn’t your place to intervene.”

Fellow Daoist Su’s lips curled into a mocking smile. “Internal matter? This person is my husband. How can I not intervene?”

The one protecting Li Haoran was none other than Su Yiren, who had been invited to observe the Immortal Appraisal Convention.

Chapter 758: The Popular Li Haoran

At the Immortal Appraisal Convention, the robes of the two Fusion Stage True Lords fluttered as they eyed each other frigidly, neither giving in. The auras they released collided on the arena stage, forming two distinctly separate fields.

“Fellow Daoist Su, this person is not even twenty. How could he be your husband? Isn’t your excuse too clumsy?” The Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest stared fixedly at Su Yiren, trying to find a flaw in her reaction.

The Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest was famous for her beauty in the East Sea. As a fellow peerlessly beautiful female cultivator, she felt a natural animosity toward Su Yiren from Great Xia.

Su Yiren replied calmly, “Haoran and I are already engaged. His parents have acknowledged this marriage. How can it be considered an excuse?”

Her words caused an uproar. The crowd present was shocked, but more so envious and jealous.

~~~

“Good heavens, engaged before twenty? How is that possible? Does being handsome really draw so many suitors?”

“I’m so envious. His cultivation isn’t high, yet he’s favored by two Fusion Stage True Lords. If only I had such luck.”

“You don’t say. If I could attach myself to a Fusion Stage True Lord, I wouldn’t need to cultivate for the rest of my life.”

~~~

“Fellow Daoist Su seems to be in fine spirits.”

“Can’t compare to Fellow Daoist Mystic Spirit seducing married men.”

The Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest placed her index finger in her mouth and pulled out a strand of saliva, the other end still clinging to the tip of her extended tongue. She gazed affectionately at Li Haoran. “So what if he’s a married man? Handsome youth, I see your kidney water is abundant. It must be that Fellow Daoist Su is unwilling to give her body to you. Why not submit to me? I can make you ascend to the heavens tonight and provide all your cultivation resources in the future.”

Su Yiren chuckled lightly, not taking the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest seriously. “Heh, do you think degrading yourself can seduce my husband? Milord, between me and Fellow Daoist Mystic Spirit, who do you choose?”

Feeling the weighty gazes of both Su Yiren and the Mystic Spirit Daoist Spirit upon him, Li Haoran’s scalp tingled.

If possible, I don’t want to choose either. But judging by the current situation, I’m afraid choosing neither will make it difficult to leave the Immortal Appraisal Convention alive.

He forcibly pulled out Qin Haoran’s memories and earnestly grasped Su Yiren’s hand. Su Yiren froze, not expecting Li Haoran to act so boldly.

“Yiren, I’ve always liked you.”

Before Su Yiren could say anything, the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest reacted first.

“Fine, fine, fine! Since you refuse to choose me, don’t blame me for using some methods!”

Twelve flying swords hovered behind the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest, their tips pointed outward. They formed a circle and rotated slowly.

These were the twelve Evil-Vanquishing Swords that the Penglai Island Lord had personally refined for the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest, a testament to his fondness for his only daughter.

The Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest’s aptitude was average. Even her current Fusion Stage cultivation was merely a result of the Penglai Island Lord stuffing her with countless pills and elixirs. She could barely reach the Fusion Stage, let alone the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

However, Transcendent Tribulation cultivators had long lifespans, meaning the Penglai Island Lord could protect the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest for a lifetime. This led to her acting wantonly without considering consequences.

If she took a fancy to a male concubine, she would just seize him. Fan Chong’s handsome appearance might have played a part in her decision to take him as a disciple.

Of course, Fan Chong was now bald, bruised and swollen, with multiple burns and severe poisoning—nothing to do with handsomeness.

The twelve Evil-Vanquishing Swords morphed into twelve cyan rays of light that burst forth, slicing through space and forming a sword array that emitted sharp sword cries.

Su Yiren clenched her jade-like hands and threw a punch, stirring up boundless air currents that blew away the twelve Evil-Vanquishing Swords.

The Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest’s expression changed, not expecting Su Yiren to break the sword array in this manner. She wanted to create distance between them, but Su Yiren wouldn’t give her the chance, staying close for melee combat. Su Yiren’s slender and pale body contained terrifying power. Every punch she delivered was enough to cause spatial fluctuations.

Li Haoran’s face turned pallid at this sight. Despite Su Yiren’s delicate appearance, she was actually a physique cultivator.

Lu Yang still had the energy to comment. “Junior Brother Li is so fortunate, having two Fusion Stage True Lords get jealous and vie for his affection.”

Lu Yang waited for a while but didn’t see Meng Jingzhou playing the straight man. He turned and saw Meng Jingzhou gnashing his teeth.

Oh, a Double Nascent Soul expert is also jealous.

Lu Yang was used to seeing Fusion Stage battles, especially high-level ones involving the elders. The fight between Su Yiren and the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest, both Basic Fusion cultivators, was merely a minor scuffle.

Despite Lu Yang feeling this way, it didn’t mean everyone did. Those qualified to be invited to the Immortal Appraisal Convention were all notable figures in the East Sea, accompanied by retainers wherever they went and enjoying refined lifestyles. Even so, most of them had never seen a Fusion Stage True Lord fight in their lives.

A refreshing sea breeze blew past. An old man stood right in the center of the arena and assumed a Taiji stance. He turned both hands and defused Su Yiren’s and the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest’s attacks.

“Fellow Daoists, could you cease hostilities on my account? I think the priority should be to neutralize the poison for Junior Nephew Fan Chong.

The two tacitly stopped attacking and snorted coldly at the same time.

“As I thought, it’s the Wind-Stabilizing Savant who intervened to stop this battle.”

“He is the Wind-Stabilizing Savant, reputed as the number one expert under the Penglai Island Lord. I heard he was defeated by the Taciturn...”

“Shh! Do you want to die? You even dared to say such things!” freewebnovel.com

Su Yiren linked arms with Li Haoran as they returned to the rest area, where Lu Yang and the others were. She adopted a gentle and demure demeanor like a fragile bird, a stark contrast to the combatant she was moments ago.

“Many thanks for your assistance, Senior Su.” Lu Yang cupped his fists in gratitude. Actually, he wanted to call her “younger sister-in-law” but feared Li Haoran would settle scores with him later.

“It was just a trifling effort.” Su Yiren was humble. She believed that given their statuses, Lu Yang and the others certainly had contingencies. “This Immortal Appraisal Convention isn’t very interesting. Let’s leave.”

Under everyone’s envious gaze, Su Yiren led Lu Yang and the other four away.

“Wait, five people, extraordinary combat power... Could it be Fangshan Island...” One of the invited cultivators suddenly thought of something.

“Fellow Daoist, do you know something?” a nearby cultivator asked.

The invited cultivator didn’t hide anything. News about Fangshan Island would reach Penglai Island in days. “Before departing, I heard that a rare treasure had emerged on Fangshan Island. Twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators went to seize it but were stopped by five Intermediate Nascent Soul cultivators.”

The commotion from the battle on Fangshan Island was huge. “One Mengs Into Ten Thousand Mengs,” which created hordes of Meng Jingzhous covering the sky, was especially noticeable.

“Five Intermediate Nascent Soul cultivators stopped twelve Divine Transfiguration cultivators?” that person gasped. How is that possible? Challenging beyond one’s levels is already heaven-defying, yet they could even fight one against many?

The person who was in the know lowered his voice. “Not just stopped—they captured them alive!”

“Captured alive?! Is that even possible?!”

“Of course, it’s possible. It’s said that those five Nascent Soul cultivators employed the Five-Elements Sect’s Five-Elements Combat Tactic during the fight. That’s an untransmitted secret from the Five-Elements Sect, implying that they must be disciples, probably even direct successors of the sect leader!”

“Five-Elements Sect disciples are actually so terrifying.”

Chapter 759: How Did You All Manage to Stir Up So Much Trouble in Half a Day

“The timing is about right. We have another friend waiting for us at the alliance headquarters.”

On the way to the alliance headquarters, Lu Yang chatted casually. “By the way, Senior Su, what brings you here to Penglai Island? Is it to attend this so-called Immortal Appraisal Convention?”

Su Yiren shook her head. “I was just passing through. I’m friends with a princess of the East Sea Dragon Palace. She invited me to attend the Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet. I was worried about potential delays on the journey, so I came to the East Sea in advance. That was when fellow Daoists from Penglai Island invited me to the Immortal Appraisal Convention.

“I see, so that’s how it is.” Lu Yang had surmised that, given Su Yiren’s taste, she wouldn’t have specifically come for such a convention. The five of them fighting among themselves would be more intense than the fights at the Immortal Appraisal Convention.

Lu Yang arrived at a good time. When he reached, Hero Yan had just finished his procedures and walked out of the pagoda.

“Finally settled.” Hero Yan felt a sense of relief wash over him. This alliance is truly black and shady. Not only are the procedures cumbersome, but everything hints at asking for money. It’s finally done after half a day.

“Apologies for keeping you waiting, Daoists. I didn’t expect being promoted to hall leader to be so complicated,” Hero Yan said with an apologetic smile. He then noticed Su Yiren leaning against Li Haoran. “Who is this?”

“It’s like this...” Lu Yang explained concisely. The more he spoke, the paler Hero Yan’s visage became.

Attending the Immortal Appraisal Convention, taking turns beating Fan Chong, being chosen as a male concubine by the Penglai Island Lord’s only daughter, two Fusion cultivators engaging in an all-out brawl, publicly humiliating the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest... and all this happened in just half a day.

How did you all manage to stir up so much trouble in just half a day?

Of all these incidents, he was only qualified to attend the Immortal Appraisal Convention as one of the many spectators.

Suddenly, he realized this unfamiliar female cultivator was a Fusion expert and hurriedly performed a deep bow. “Junior Yan Chuan pays respects to Senior Su.”

“Penglai Island might seek revenge on us in the future. For safety’s sake, Hero Yan, it’s best that you don’t associate with us anymore,” Lu Yang kindly advised. With his current identity as a Five Elements Sect disciple, he couldn’t protect Hero Yan.

Only by bringing out my identity as Young Creed Leader Lu will we stand a chance.

Hero Yan felt that Lu Yang’s words made sense. The experiences he gained from staying with Lu Yang’s group every day were too frightening. As a mere Divine Transfiguration cultivator, I really can’t handle it.

“Then we shall part ways here. Daoists, if you ever come to my Fangshan Island in the future, I will certainly host you.”

“Goodbye.”

Hero Yan and Lu Yang’s group cupped fists solemnly in farewell, then turned and left Penglai Island.

“Just advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage yet without arrogance—that’s a rare mindset,” Su Yiren commented. She had seen several cultivators in the East Sea who had just advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage. They were arrogant beyond bounds, demonstrating poor mental states.

In fact, this was a prevalent problem among East Sea cultivators—emphasizing cultivation but neglecting mental state. This made them prone to falling into qi deviation or encountering bottlenecks.

Li Haoran thought, If you knew what Hero Yan experienced with us, you’d understand why he is without arrogance.

Su Yiren had been to Penglai Island several times and was relatively familiar with it, and Li Haoran had half of Qin Haoran’s memories. Together, they were more than sufficient as guides.

“We are currently on Penglai Island’s main island. It’s divided into inner and outer zones. The inner zone is the core area of Penglai Island, where the Immortal Appraisal Convention and the East Sea Cultivators Alliance headquarters are located.

“Where we are now is the outer zone, the area most densely populated with East Sea cultivators. These shops in the outer zone can definitely be traced back to their origins, belonging to Penglai Island’s various factions like family clans and elders. Due to the Immortal Appraisal Convention, there are more cultivators in the outer zone than usual.

“In the surroundings of the main island are three smaller islands where mortals live. They plant spirit grains, raise silkworms, mine ores...all for the sustenance, clothing, and needs of Penglai Island disciples.”

Li Haoran interjected, “Especially the mining areas; security is extremely tight. In my past life, I tried to steal a few spirit stones and got discovered.”

At the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000-year celebration, Li Haoran had met Su Yiren, informing her he had awakened his past life memories and confessing that Qin Haoran was the Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader.

Su Yiren wasn’t surprised. Qin Haoran had always been mysterious, obviously not like someone engaged in legitimate business. Moreover, Qin Haoran claimed that he would reincarnate, which was a belief of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, indicating he was likely high-ranking in the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

The six found a restaurant and sat down. The East Sea’s high humidity was something low-cultivators couldn’t withstand. Most teas provided in restaurants had dampness-removing effects.

Lu Yang and the others didn’t need dampness removal but didn’t mind ordering a pot for a taste, along with a few plates of local specialties.

Looking at the insects still wriggling on the plate, Lu Yang and the others really couldn’t bring themselves to eat them. The sliced fish, however, tasted excellent and was extremely fresh.

“What a pity. This fish just isn’t old enough; its spirit energy isn’t abundant. If it lived another ten years, the flavor would surely reach another level,” Meng Jingzhou remarked with slight regret. When he fooled around in the imperial capital, he frequented major restaurants and had considerable expertise in food.

“That’s easy to fix.” The Metamorphic Immortal Grass popped up from behind Tao Yaoye. “Ask the shop for a live white crucian carp; it must be alive.”

They were in a private room, so they weren’t afraid of outsiders seeing the Metamorphic Immortal Grass.

Meng Jingzhou called the waiter for a white crucian carp, stressing that it had to be alive and still jumping.

The waiter brought up a wooden basin with a white crucian carp. It was pure as jade and swimming inside. After placing the basin down, he left, but not forgetting to look at the group strangely.

Although our shop prides itself on freshness, this is the first time we’ve encountered patrons who would just bite into a live fish.

The Metamorphic Immortal Grass didn’t care what the waiter thought. It tore off an almost imperceptible bit of its leaf and fed it to the white crucian carp.

Blessed by fortune, the white crucian carp received a fortuitous opportunity, bursting forth with milky white rays. Then the light vanished. It had transformed into a twenty-year-old white crucian carp, brimming with spirit energy.

“Done.” The Metamorphic Immortal Grass had a look of accomplishment.

“Little Herb King?” Su Yiren was astonished. She couldn’t identify the Metamorphic Immortal Grass‘s variety but could discern that it was a little herb king.

“Such a tiny bit made this fish gain twenty years of cultivation?” Meng Jingzhou was shocked. Isn’t this Metamorphic Immortal Grass too heaven-defying?

The most central leaf of the Metamorphic Grass swayed, acting as its head. “How could it be that convenient? It’s because this fish requires very few resources for cultivation.

“If it were you five, this tiny bit of leaf would only increase your cultivation by an extra week.”

Lu Yang used the Qingfeng Sword to slice the white crucian carp into pieces, and everyone took a slice. The taste was indeed several times better than the previous white crucian carp.

Su Yiren had visited the East Sea several times but never eaten a white crucian carp of this level. Finding the Metamorphic Immortal Grass useful, her eyes lit up. Assuming the immortal grass’s ability was to enhance the quality of natural treasures, she took out a small porcelain vial from her storage ring and asked the immortal grass, “This is a treasure I obtained by chance. Could you increase its quality by one level? I have great use for it in the future.”

Meng Jingzhou found this small porcelain vial and its contents extremely familiar.

Isn’t this my essence blood?

Senior Su, what are you trying to do?

Chapter 760: The Legends of the Penglai Island Lord

Accomplished cultivators could deduce information about a blood sample’s owner and use it for schemes, curses, and so on. Hence, before Meng Jingzhou sold his blood, he had completely erased all information contained within his essence blood. No one could trace it back to him, including Su Yiren.

“What is this?” Li Haoran was somewhat perplexed, unsure what Su Yiren was trying to do.

“This is blood I obtained from a black market auction. It cost me one hundred thousand spirit stones.”

Meng Jingzhou’s expression turned strange. When I sold my blood, it was ten thousand spirit stones per drop. Isn’t this price hike way too ridiculous?

To think I lost money despite being a member of the Meng Family—what a disgrace.

“This blood should be the true blood of some pure-blood demon tribe, with effects of enhancing cultivation, boosting yang, and supplementing qi. I figured I’d buy it for my husband. If the immortal grass can elevate this blood’s effects by one level, that would be even better.”

Hearing this, Li Haoran was deeply moved. He didn’t expect Su Yiren to always think of him and look out for him in every way.

Lu Yang also recognized this as Meng Jingzhou’s essence blood. I don’t recall Old Meng’s blood having cultivation-enhancing effects. If Old Meng’s blood has such effects, I’d drink three big bowls first.

Senior Su, have you started speaking blatant lies just to trick Li Haoran into bed?

“No can do. I can only increase the cultivation of living beings. There might be a chance if you find the blood’s owner.” The Metamorphic Immortal Grass dashed Su Yiren’s hopes.

“I see.” Su Yiren’s mood visibly dipped.

Lu Yang surreptitiously glanced at Meng Jingzhou, contemplating whether to tell Su Yiren the truth and give Meng Jingzhou a boost in cultivation. It could count as Old Meng’s fortuitous opportunity.

Meng Jingzhou shook his head rapidly in small motions, rejecting the fortuitous opportunity.

An image surfaced in Meng Jingzhou’s mind:

In the quiet of the night, he lies in bed fast asleep. Su Yiren sneaks into his room in the dark, moonlight illuminating her well-shaped figure.

Meng Jingzhou maintains a firm stance and declares, “I can’t do anything that betrays Junior Brother Li.”

Su Yiren replies, “It’ll just hurt a little; it’ll be quick.”

Meng Jingzhou struggles desperately but is ultimately no match for Su Yiren. Then Su Yiren ties Meng Jingzhou up and starts drawing his blood...

What kind of scenario is that?

Amidst their conversation and laughter, they shared the white crucian carp, leaving only a plate of cleanly picked fish bones.

Pitiful white crucian carp. It had chanced upon a fortuitous opportunity and consumed immortal grass, causing its cultivation to soar, reaching the twenty-year realm no fish of its kind had ever attained. Little did it know this was all a scheme laid by humans. Pierced by an immortal sword, it was carved apart and eaten by human cultivators, with not even an intact corpse remaining.

After enjoying the East Sea delicacies, Lu Yang and the others went downstairs to settle the bill. Lu Yang noticed a statue on the counter depicting a middle-aged man with a goatee.

“Who is this statue supposed to be?” Lu Yang asked casually.

Li Haoran answered, “That’s the Penglai Island Lord, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest. Many legends about him circulate in the East Sea. For example, when fishermen were caught in storms at sea, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest happened to pass by. He casually saved the ship’s crew and told them that they could silently pray with his name for safe travels when going out to fish in the future.

“There’s also a legend that during autumn harvest, when grain farmers had a bountiful harvest, heavy rain suddenly fell, and the Three Mountains Daoist Priest also appeared there. It’s similar to the fishermen legend. I reckon one of these two is the original, and the other evolved through word of mouth.

“Alternatively, another instance is that wherever a plague broke out, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest bestowed sweet dew and heavenly springs to cure diseases and save people.

“Furthermore, there’s the tale that when cultivators got restless due to encountering a bottleneck in cultivation, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest appeared and helped them break through...

“Anyway, there are many such legends, and they have circulated for four or five thousand years. No one knows how much is true. In short, among East Sea cultivators, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest is a belief; every household worships him.

“If one were to say he’s efficacious, he’s definitely not extremely so. Even if he had millions of clones, he couldn’t fulfil everyone’s wishes. Even immortals don’t have that kind of capability.

“But the Three Mountains Daoist Priest has been famous for so long that the belief has become habitual, serving as spiritual solace. Whether it’s efficacious or not is no longer important.

“It’s possible that the Three Mountains Daoist Priest is part of the reason that the three Penglai Islands hold Penglai in the highest esteem.

“I heard the Golden Buddhist Kingdom wanted to spread its teachings to the East Sea but failed due to the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s presence.”

Lu Yang recalled Fan Chong. “As the grand-disciple of the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, Fan Chong relies on his influence to bully others. It feels like the Three Mountains Daoist Priest isn’t as good as the legends say.”

Li Haoran couldn’t explain this either, shaking his head helplessly. “Perhaps the Three Mountains Daoist Priest is in seclusion all year round and doesn’t strictly keep the people below him in check?”

He looked toward Su Yiren, who also shook her head. “I’ve met the Three Mountains Daoist Priest once. He was very considerate in how he treated others. Even when meeting mid- and low-level cultivators, he didn’t appear overly arrogant, much like his image in the folk legends. I also can’t imagine why the Mystic Spirit Daoist Priest and Fan Chong are like that.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly spoke, somewhat puzzled. “What’s with this Three Mountains Daoist Priest? He came up with so many outrageous legends. If he doesn’t have that much ability, he shouldn’t mess around.”

In the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy lay on her water bed, floating on the sea surface, her fish tail flapping with a patter sound.

Lu Yang suddenly remembered that although the current Everlasting Immortal Fairy seemed utterly unreliable, she was also an object of faith in the ancient era. To fulfil her believers’ requests for fertility, she even created the Mother-Child River and the Twins Rivers.

“Immortal Fairy, is there some reason or principle behind this?”

“This immortal doesn’t know much about faith power. Qing He is more knowledgeable in this regard. Qing He told me that as a source of faith, one must control the legends well and absolutely not portray oneself as omnipotent.

“Let’s take this immortal as an example. When believers prayed to me for children, I indeed had the ability to create the Mother-Child River, so I responded to their requests.

“Some believers prayed to me for power. If I wasn’t willing to grant power, I would make it clear face-to-face to avoid believers coming one after another to ask me. That would be very annoying.”

Lu Yang nodded, half-understanding.

“Dear guests, you don’t seem like East Sea cultivators?” The shop owner noticed Lu Yang’s group displaying great interest in the Three Mountains Daoist Priest statue; East Sea cultivators weren’t like this.

Lu Yang nodded. We’re indeed not East Sea cultivators; we’re Five-Elements Sect disciples.

“How about paying respects to the Three Mountains Daoist Priest? It’s very efficacious.” The shop owner appeared extremely devout.

Lu Yang and the others thought about it. Since this could be considered a distinctive feature of the East Sea, paying respects wouldn’t hurt.

Lu Yang pressed his palms together and bowed to the Three Mountains Daoist Priest statue, silently praying with sincere hope that this East Sea legend could protect them. “May our journey in the East Sea be safe and peaceful with no incidents.”

Meng Jingzhou and the rest followed suit, paying their respects.

~~~

Within the inner zone of Penglai Island, at the core area of a nine-grade spirit vein, a man with a goatee was meditating on a putuan cushion.

Suddenly, with a “wah” sound, he spat out blood, his expression startled and bewildered. freewebnovel.com

“What powerful being is paying respects to me?”

Chapter 761: Peerless Mighty Expert

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest calmed his breathing and began calculating with his fingers, attempting to deduce the other party’s origins. Before attaining any result, he was struck by two slaps that left him dizzy and disoriented.

“A peerless mighty expert roaming the mortal world and paying respects to my statue?”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest couldn’t figure out the other party’s methods, but their merely paying respects to him had severely injured him, and his attempt to infer their origins was countered. This indicated that the other party’s status and abilities surpassed his own. freewebnovel.com

“The two slaps weren’t too heavy, meaning the peerless mighty expert holds no malice toward me?”

Peerless mighty experts were capricious. The Three Mountains Daoist Priest could only hope the other party was just passing through the East Sea and wouldn’t linger.

“It appears that the peerless mighty expert also made a wish?”

He was busy spitting blood earlier and didn’t notice what wish that peerless being had made.

That mighty expert must have eyes and hands that reach the heavens, with vast powers and connections. What wish could they possibly need my help with?

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest shook his head, deciding not to dwell on this matter. They’re probably just toying with me.

He had always acted prudently, knowing who he could provoke and who he couldn’t.

“Why was I out of my mind to think of using faith power to cultivate back then?” The Three Mountains Daoist Priest was vexed. If not for that, I wouldn’t be reduced to this state now.

The Wind-Stabilizing Savant stood at the entrance to the ninth-grade spirit vein’s core area. “Island Lord, Great Xia’s Second Imperial Prince, Jiang Zhu, has arrived at Penglai Island and wishes to see you.”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest wiped the blood from the corner of his mouth. I can’t be more troubled right now; how could I be in the mood to see outsiders?

He was about to say no when he suddenly realized the Second Imperial Prince wasn’t from the East Sea. That peerless mighty expert obviously isn’t from the East Sea either; otherwise, they would already have paid respects until I coughed up blood a long time ago and not wait until today.

The biggest variable in the East Sea recently is the Second Imperial Prince’s fleet.

Could that peerless supreme be within the Second Imperial Prince’s fleet, and that just now was a show of force to assert dominance?

The words of refusal were about to roll off his tongue, but he changed them at the last moment. “Then I shall meet him.”

~~~

“Why are you paying respects to some Three Mountains Daoist Priest? You have this immortal, such a big person right here, yet you don’t pay respects to me!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was so upset that she used her fish tail to slap Lu Yang’s face multiple times, splashing water all over his face.

“Can’t this immortal guarantee your safety in the East Sea?”

I, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals, roamed the ancient times unimpeded and was peerless under heaven. The believers who wanted to worship me could fill an entire planet. I never expected Lu Yang to ignore me and pay respects to some unheard-of Three Mountains Daoist Priest instead.

“Immortal Fairy, don’t be angry. It was just for the experience; I wasn’t really paying respects,” Lu Yang repeatedly apologized and explained.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy puffed out her cheeks angrily, crossed her arms, and turned her head away, unwilling to acknowledge Lu Yang.

Lu Yang coaxed her for a long while until she was finally willing to engage with him again, though she still pouted.

“You paying respects to him is useless. As the almighty Second-in-Command of the Everlasting Lineage, you have this immortal backing you—your fate profile is much higher than his.

“Maybe your single act of paying respects made him spit blood.

Lu Yang was startled by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words and said sheepishly, “That can’t be, right? Immortal Fairy, didn’t you also pay respects to the three founding ancestors during the sect celebration?”

“That’s not the same thing. This immortal is a guest elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect, so it’s fine to pay respects to the sect’s founding ancestors. But putting that aside, those three also didn’t use faith power to cultivate.

“How about you try paying respects to the Third-in-Command when you return to the sect? I guarantee he’ll spit blood with every bow of yours.”

Seeing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy speak so convincingly, Lu Yang reckoned it was best to refrain from paying respects to people in the future to avoid causing trouble.

The Third-in-Command is one thing—he has the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit anyway; coughing up a few mouthfuls of blood is fine. But if the Penglai Island Lord spat blood, I can’t afford to compensate.

“Has the Second Imperial Prince’s fleet arrived?” Lu Yang and the others noticed three large, conspicuous ships docked at Penglai Island, with many cultivators heading over to watch the spectacle.

The last time Great Xia’s imperial court came to the East Sea with such fanfare was three hundred years ago, when Yingzhou Island’s new island lord assumed the position.

Lu Yang saw the Second Imperial Prince disembark, accompanied by several attendants who corresponded to the Fusion cultivators in the List of Great Xia Dynasty’s Fusion cultivators bought at the Dao-Seeking Sect’s sect celebration.

The list was full of Shifu’s enemies.

“One of the attendants doesn’t seem to be on the list. Is it a Fusion cultivator secretly groomed by the imperial court or a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator?” Lu Yang thought the latter was more likely.

“Speaking of which, are there any legends about longevity herbs in the East Sea?”

Li Haoran nodded. “Yes, and quite a few at that. For example, legends say that deep within Yingzhou Island’s eighth-grade spirit vein lies a Longevity Immortal Herb, planted by the Evergreen Supreme Lord in ancient times.”

Lu Yang turned back to his mental space to consult the knowledgeable individual. “Who is the Evergreen Supreme Lord?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy dove into the sea to catch bubbles, blowing bubbles while speaking. “A half-immortal who possessed the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit. He even declared he wanted to compete with this immortal for the Dao Fruit position. I knocked him down with two punches; he couldn’t take a beating.”

Li Haoran continued, “For instance, in a corner north of the East Sea, there lies a mysterious island that only appears at high tide, during the transition between the old and new year. The island is filled with lethal dangers, protected by countless ferocious beasts guarding the immortal grass at its center. Consuming the immortal grass allows one to ascend in the day and live forever.

“Also, at the deepest part of the East Sea’s seabed, there’s an extinct volcano. Its crater is piled with embers, and within the embers blooms a fierce red flower. Its species and effects are unknown, and whether it grants longevity is also unclear.

“And there’s...”

Li Haoran narrated over ten legends in one go.

“The East Sea has too many races, making communication and interactions difficult, which resulted in all sorts of bizarre legends. When Qin Haoran came to the East Sea back then, he visited most of the legendary locations.

“They were all fake.”

If there truly were immortal herbs, Qin Haoran would have risked his life to pluck one. It could have solved most of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s debts. He had even considered sneaking into places like the depths of Yingzhou Island’s spirit veins. But that was Yingzhou Island’s lifeblood, and its island lord was a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. He probably could have entered alive but not left alive.

The group relaxed, eating, drinking, and playing for most of the day.

“Be careful, the Waning Moon True Lord is coming this way,” Su Yiren warned.

Right as soon as the words left her mouth, a lanky cultivator stood before Lu Yang and the others. “The Second Imperial Prince requests your presence. Could you grace him with your presence and step over?”

“How does His Highness know we’re here?” Man Gu was surprised. The Second Imperial Prince’s methods are truly impressive. He has just arrived at Penglai Island, yet he already knows our location.

Li Haoran transmitted an auditory message helplessly. “Because Lu Yang used Arhat Fist.”

East Sea cultivators might not know, but which Great Xia cultivator didn’t know Lu Yang’s fists specialized in treating thick hair? The commotion at the Immortal Appraisal Convention was so huge. One simply had to ask around to learn of Lu Yang’s presence.

No matter the case, he is the Second Imperial Prince. Although his status can’t compare to mine, Yun Zhi’s Little Junior Brother, we still have to give him some face.

“Let’s go then.” Lu Yang smiled, curious about the Second Imperial Prince’s intentions.

It wasn’t Lu Yang’s first time meeting the Second Imperial Prince, Jiang Zhu. The latter was the one who came to the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony. But back then, the Second Imperial Prince could only watch helplessly with wide eyes from below, while I, the Young Creed Leader, displayed my divine might on stage.

The Waning Moon True Lord led the group to the most luxurious restaurant in Penglai Island’s outer zone.

Seeing Lu Yang and the others arrive, the Second Imperial Prince smiled and welcomed Lu Yang. “I have long heard of Fellow Daoist Lu Yang’s reputation. Meeting you today, you are indeed extraordinary.”

Lu Yang noticed the table laden with a large spread of dishes.

The Second Imperial Prince thought Lu Yang was fond of delicacies and said modestly, “I just casually ordered a few dishes. I hope you won’t find them wanting, Fellow Daoist Lu Yang.”

Although he said he had casually ordered them, these were actually the restaurant’s signature dishes.

Lu Yang didn’t say anything. I’m a polite person. This entire table of dishes can’t compare to a twenty-year-old white crucian carp. I’ll try my best not to find the Second Imperial Prince’s knowledge wanting.

Chapter 762: Second Imperial Prince

“Young Master Meng, it’s been three years since we last met, hasn’t it? I often hear tales of your exploits from storytellers in the imperial city,” the Second Imperial Prince, Jiang Zhu, remarked.
