Standing tall and upright with a heroic bearing, he patted Meng Jingzhou’s shoulder with a smile, as though he was greeting a good friend he hadn’t seen in ages.

“You two know each other?” Lu Yang asked, then realized his question was redundant. Right, who in the imperial city doesn’t know Meng Jingzhou?

Meng Jingzhou transmitted an auditory message to Lu Yang. “Back when I was doing well in the imperial city, I beat up his younger brother, his biological brother born to the same parents. That’s how we became acquainted.

Oh man! Lu Yang thought, As expected of the imperial city’s tyrannical bully—he even dared to beat an imperial prince.

“I presume these two are the inventor of the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage, Tao Yaoye, and the Ancient Barbarian, Man Gu. And this is...” The Second Imperial Prince paused when his gaze fell upon Li Haoran.

Tao Yaoye and Man Gu frequently undertook missions outside the sect, making it easy for the Second Imperial Prince to gather intelligence on them. However, Li Haoran was an exception. He seldom left the sect, so the Second Imperial Prince didn’t recognize him.

Su Yiren had called him “Haoran” and not his full name at the Immortal Appraisal Convention.

“I am Li Haoran, a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“So it’s Fellow Daoist Li Haoran. I’ve long looked forward to meeting you. And this must be the reclusive cultivator, Fellow Daoist Su Yiren. Please, everyone, have a seat.”

Noticing Su Yiren linking arms with Li Haoran, the Second Imperial Prince recalled the rumors he had heard at the Immortal Appraisal Convention. His gaze toward Li Haoran became slightly peculiar, but his refined upbringing allowed him to conceal his odd expression swiftly.

“May I ask why Your Highness has summoned us?” Having interacted with the Second Imperial Prince before, Meng Jingzhou knew there must be an underlying reason for inviting them over.

“It’s nothing much. It’s just that we are fellow subjects of Great Xia; since we have crossed paths in the East Sea, we can catch up and sample the East Sea delicacies.”

Meng Jingzhou replied inwardly, Like I’ll believe your nonsense. All three of your large ships are full of Great Xia cultivators. Why would you need to come to catch up with us?

Hearing the purpose was so simple, Man Gu buried his head and began eating heartily. Although the flavors can’t compare to the white crucian carp we ate earlier, there’s a better variety. Trying various dishes will help me broaden my horizons.

“I heard Fellow Daoist Lu Yang is a disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, possessing extraordinary spellcraft and swordsmanship that are capable of rivalling that so-called Young Creed Leader Lu, and you’ve even served as acting sect leader twice. Your future is truly boundless. Countless cultivators in the imperial city regard you as a role model!”

Lu Yang replied humbly, “Your Highness is too polite. It’s all due to my own effort and has nothing to do with my shifu.”

The Second Imperial Prince’s eyelid twitched, unsure how to respond.

“I heard Your Highness came to the East Sea to search for the Longevity Immortal Herb. Have you found any leads?”

The Second Imperial Prince smiled. “I just paid a visit to the Penglai Island Lord and heard a few secret tales from him. It’s possible that the Longevity Immortal Herb exists.”

“We are also concerned about His Majesty’s health. If needed, we could assist Your Highness in searching for the immortal herb.”

“I appreciate your kind intentions, Fellow Daoist Lu Yang. However, the environment where such an immortal herb grows is extremely harsh. If anything were to happen to all of you, it would be difficult to explain to the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“It’s fine. We immortal sect disciples have our life-preserving methods. Your Highness need not worry for our safety.”

With things put this way, the Second Imperial Prince could no longer insist that Lu Yang and the others shouldn’t help. “Then I thank you all for your kindness.”

~~~

At the Second Imperial Prince’s invitation, Lu Yang and the others boarded the ship.

“These three ships must have cost a fortune. It seems Your Highness came to the East Sea well-prepared to search for the herb.”

The Second Imperial Prince wore a worried expression and sighed. “My eldest brother claims to have no interest in contending for the throne, but who knows if he’s speaking the truth? And my third brother is also eyeing that position covetously.

“Emperor Father is the backbone of Great Xia. If he falls, it would inevitably trigger a struggle for succession, plunging Great Xia into chaos.

“Although I have no desire to vie for the throne myself, I don’t wish to see brothers turn against each other, which is why I had set sail. If I can track down the Longevity Immortal Herb on this journey to the East Sea and extend Emperor Father’s life, the cost of these three ships will be insignificant.”

“I’ve met the Eldest Imperial Prince twice. He didn’t appear to be interested in the throne.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had first met the Eldest Imperial Prince, Jiang Qun, at the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, where he had used the alias Xia Qun and served as a deputy to the provincial governor.

The second time was during the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration, where the Eldest Imperial Prince had shown up as the representative of Great Xia.

“Some say my eldest brother is biding his time, secretly amassing power. There are even rumors that Emperor Father’s dwindling lifespan is somehow connected to him.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged a glance. It seemed matters in the imperial city were more complicated than they had imagined.

The Second Imperial Prince suddenly realized the conversation had grown heavy and that he had shared too much information that Lu Yang’s group shouldn’t know. Adjusting his mood, he smiled and said, “Alright, that’s enough. Why speak of such matters? The East Sea’s scenery is vast. Why dwell on these troubling affairs?”

The large ship set sail. The azure sky and the profound sea seemed to merge at that moment, forming a seamless, connected tapestry of sky and water. Sunlight scattered across the sea’s surface like shattered gold, sparkling and shimmering, reflecting a resplendent world of light and shadow. Gazing upon it for a while indeed soothed the mind and heart.

However, Lu Yang felt little appreciation for the East Sea’s picturesque scenery. His mind was currently filled with the East Sea’s waters and an immortal-level mermaid frolicking within.

“Might this be Young Friend Lu Yang?” An elderly man appeared silently beside Lu Yang.

Earlier, when Lu Yang had watched the Second Imperial Prince disembark, the attendants surrounding him were all at the Fusion Stage, except for this elderly man he didn’t recognize, leading Lu Yang to suspect he was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Now, he had received confirmation from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that his conjecture was accurate.

“And you are...?”

“This old man is the Cang Mingzi. I once had the fortune to exchange blows with Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi.”

Lu Yang understood. No wonder an almighty Transcendent Tribulation old monster is being so polite to me, addressing me as “young friend.” So it’s because he’s been beaten up by Big Senior Sister.

“Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi has cultivated for less than a thousand years, yet she has already reached a transcendent, sage-like realm. It truly puts these old bones to shame.”

“You jest, Senior Cang Mingzi. Countless people envy your level of cultivation.”

“It’s merely the result of grinding away with time. Not only are you Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi’s junior brother, but you also possess such outstanding talent. You are destined to have a place in the Battle of the Great Era.” Cang Mingzi sighed with emotion upon seeing Lu Yang in the prime of his youth. He then turned and clasped his hands behind his back, shaking his head as he sauntered away.

“What do you say?” Meng Jingzhou asked Lu Yang out of the blue through an auditory message.

Lu Yang sighed and replied with an auditory message, “The Second Imperial Prince is too eager to befriend us. If I’m not mistaken, we may encounter the perils of the sea soon.”

Despite the Second Imperial Prince’s efforts to appear unconcerned about the throne, he had expressed uncertainty about whether his eldest brother would contend for it and mentioned his third brother was also eyeing the position covetously.

The word “also” implied the Second Imperial Prince himself also had his sights set on the throne.

Meanwhile, he and Meng Jingzhou were respectively Yun Zhi’s Little Junior Brother and the Eldest Young Master of the Meng Family. If he could win over the two of them, securing the throne would be as good as nailed in place.

A quick way to deepen friendship was naturally to face danger together and survive a calamity.

“I wonder if he’d still have the guts to try and rope us in if he knows we’re both from the Heavenly Court Creed.”

Chapter 763: Stage a Performance

Just as Lu Yang had predicted, when the large ship sailed onward, the weather abruptly shifted. Lightning flashed and thunder boomed. The ship was lifted a hundred meters into the air before it plummeted, slamming violently against the sea’s surface. If not for the multiple arrays that reinforced the hull, the ship would have already splintered into pieces.

I knew it, Lu Yang mused. He had seen three Fusion cultivators on this ship alone, not counting the number aboard the other two ships. With so many high-level cultivators present, encountering such a terrifying storm was clearly a man-made occurrence. After all, Fusion cultivators wielded partial control over the power of laws. Dispelling a storm at sea was simply a matter of uttering a command.

Su Yiren’s expression turned grave. She shielded Lu Yang and the others, transmitting an auditory message. “Be careful! I attempted to use the power of rules to dispel the storm, but it was ineffective. Someone is deliberately causing trouble from behind the scenes, and they’re at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!”

A hole tore open in the ink-black clouds, and a black silhouette appeared high above, shrouded in wind and rain. Emerald-green eyes, gleaming like amber, lit up with an eerie glow that seemed to come from the depths of the underworld. The oppressive aura was like a prison, unfathomable, unshakable, and unstoppable, weighing down upon the hearts of all present.

“It really is a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator!” Su Yiren broke out in a cold sweat. She hadn’t expected their luck on their journey to be so abysmal as to run into a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

As soon as Tao Yaoye and Man Gu heard it was a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, they grew somewhat flustered. They seldom ventured out with Lu Yang and hadn’t witnessed such grand scenes.

Lu Yang remained unruffled, transmitting an auditory message to the group to explain the situation. “Everyone, don’t panic. This is all part of the Second Imperial Prince’s scheme. To ascend to the throne, he plans to stage a calamity to make us owe him a favor.

“If my guess is correct, Senior Cang Mingzi is conveniently absent from the ship right now. First, the Fusion cultivators will engage the enemy. Then, the Second Imperial Prince will come to reassure us and say we’re on the same boat, calling for unity to tide us over this crisis. To make it convincing, he’ll even injure himself.

“At the critical moment, Senior Cang Mingzi will arrive fashionably late, battle the shadowy figure for three hundred rounds, and ultimately defeat them, forcing them to retreat in disgrace.”

While the group felt a wave of relief, they also seethed with indignation, thinking the Second Imperial Prince had gone too far.

“Form ranks and meet the enemy!” the Second Imperial Prince yelled.

Whoosh, whoosh, whoosh. Three figures flew out from each of the three large ships, all at the Fusion Stage.

The Second Imperial Prince had brought nine Fusion cultivators with him on this trip. These nine were all seasoned veterans. Having anticipated the possibility of conflict in the East Sea, they had practiced many times in advance.

Subtle yet powerful fluctuations of spirit energy rippled out from the array they were setting up—the Nine Heavens Thunder Response Array, engraved with complex and abstruse talismanic scripts. As their fingers traced through the air, rays of light burst forth from their bodies, coalescing into a gigantic nine-sided net. Each of the Fusion cultivators stood at one corner of the net, their hand seals drawing the primordial qi of heaven and earth.

Seeing this, the Second Imperial Prince hurried to Lu Yang’s side and reassured the group. “Fellow Daoists, do not panic. These nine Fusion cultivators have formed the Nine Heavens Thunder Response Array, which can resist a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. Everything will be fine.”

Despite the Second Imperial Prince’s assurances, Lu Yang was only a Nascent Soul after all. Faced with a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s attacks, how could he not feel a sliver of panic?

His voice quivered as he asked, “Where is Senior Cang Mingzi?”

The Second Imperial Prince wore an expression of chagrin. “Just now, he said he spotted a rare fish and went to catch one for a meal. Who could have thought that we’d face an assault by a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator when barely any time has passed?!”

As he spoke, the mysterious Transcendent Tribulation cultivator made their move. An array stabilizing the ship’s hull at its bottom shattered. A towering wave crashed over the deck, sweeping everyone, including the Second Imperial Prince, off their feet and leaving them unable to stand steadily.

“Are you sure everything will be fine?” Meng Jingzhou struggled to grip the ship’s railing, swaying wildly.

The Second Imperial Prince’s expression turned resolute. “Everything will be fine. Even if I must put my life on the line, I will ensure your safety!”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were deeply moved.

The Second Imperial Prince looked up at the figure of the Transcendent Tribulation cultivator in the midst of battle and demanded sternly, “Who exactly are you? I am Jiang Zhu, the Second Imperial Prince of Great Xia! Are you intending on making an enemy of Great Xia?!”

The Transcendent Tribulation shadow emitted a cold laugh and cast a disdainful glance at the Second Imperial Prince, fully displaying the arrogance of someone at such a cultivation realm.

“Long-winded.”

As the Transcendent Tribulation shadow uttered the word, the Second Imperial Prince felt a stifling pressure in his chest and was sent flying backward. He slammed into the cabin wall and spat out two mouthfuls of blood. His hairpin fell loose, and his hair plastered across his face messily. He appeared utterly wretched, a stark contrast to his usual dignified image.

With perfect composure, Lu Yang transmitted an auditory message to the group. “See, what did I tell you? To gain our sympathy, the Second Imperial Prince would definitely get injured. And I must say, his acting is quite convincing.”

“Perhaps his injury is real to avoid exposing the act,” Meng Jingzhou remarked, looking at the blood-spitting prince with admiration. “He’s pulling all the stops for the throne. My impression of him has changed.”

Tao Yaoye and Man Gu gazed at Lu Yang in awe. Up until now, everything that has transpired had unfolded exactly as Senior Brother Lu Yang had predicted.

“How dare you injure others?!”

Cang Mingzi arrived fashionably late. With an angry shout, he deployed his boundless Dharma Manifestation. Muttering archaic incantations, he instantly triggered a resonance from the ocean’s depths. The churning seawater seemed to be pulled by an invisible force, gathering around him. The waters ceased their rampage and obeyed some peculiar law to coalesce into the shape of a colossal humanoid figure.

The two sides clashed in a great battle, each displaying their mighty abilities and overturning the seas, frightening the sea tribes beneath until they trembled.

“Elder Cang, the act has gone on long enough. If you keep fighting, the ship will fall apart.” The Second Imperial Prince secretly transmitted an auditory message to Cang Mingzi. Elder Cang doesn’t know how to hold back; that blow just now injured me quite severely.

The Second Imperial Prince’s plan was exactly as Lu Yang had deduced; even the injury was part of the scheme. He had asked Cang Mingzi to create a clone, which he would battle and ultimately defeat. Furthermore, the clone must not possess any distinguishing features. If it resembled a particular sea tribe, Lu Yang’s group would later clamor to seek trouble with that tribe, and the entire ruse would be exposed.

Given the Dao-Seeking Sect’s strength and Lu Yang’s status, it’s even possible that Yun Zhi and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord—two half-immortals—would join forces to come to the East Sea to settle scores.

This was why they had designed the clone to be a shadowy figure.

Cang Mingzi was stunned, unsure what the Second Imperial Prince was talking about. “The clone isn’t ready yet.”

He had genuinely gone fishing earlier.

A question mark popped out of the Second Imperial Prince’s head. He instantly realized the situation was dire.

Hopy crap, has a real Transcendent Tribulation cultivator shown up?!

“Troublesome.”

While Cang Mingzi was distracted, the Transcendent Tribulation shadow reached out a massive hand covered in talismanic runes, capable of crushing anything it grabbed.

The giant hand ripped through the Nine Heavens Thunder Response Array. Lu Yang and his four companions were snatched away like helpless chicks. Su Yiren tried to save them but was captured alongside them.

After the Transcendent Tribulation shadow captured Lu Yang and the others, the weather returned to normal, and the waves were calm again, as though no battle had taken place.

The Second Imperial Prince collapsed onto the deck, devoid of any relief at having survived a calamity.

“It’s over. Yun Zhi’s Little Junior Brother and the Eldest Young Master of the Meng Family were captured from my ship, and they’re now missing.”

Forget about contending for the throne now; all I pray for now is that the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Meng Family won’t come to my doorstep demanding my life.

~~~

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, is us being captured also part of the plan?” Tao Yaoye asked uncertainly.

They were trapped inside a sphere of water, speeding across the East Sea while clutched by a gigantic claw.

Lu Yang also felt that things were amiss. Could it be that the Second Imperial Prince still wants to stage a “hero saves the heroes” act?

“Immortal Fairy, can you tell the origin of this shadowy figure?”

“Hmm? Isn’t this just a member of the Kunpeng Tribe?” Despite the shadowy figure’s efforts to conceal its race, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw through it at a glance.

Lu Yang, “...”

He didn’t think the Second Imperial Prince had the capability to invite a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the Kunpeng Tribe to stage a performance.

Chapter 764: Black Feather Venerable Lord

The Kunpeng Tribe’s old ancestor moved with extreme speed, so fast that the group couldn’t discern the surrounding scenery at all. The view changed at the speed of lightning. Even a single glance at the outside world would induce dizziness.

Suddenly, they felt a void beneath their feet. The water sphere restraining them vanished, and they all dropped to the ground like dumplings into a pot.

Fortunately, the fall wasn’t from a great height, so no one was injured. They simply tumbled about, their appearances somewhat unseemly.

“Why is the ground so rough?” Man Gu complained as he rubbed his buttocks.

“No, this isn’t ground. It’s a bird nest,” Li Haoran stated solemnly.

Beneath their feet were criss-crossed branches, each as thick as two men, though it was unknown what kind of tree they had been removed from. The nest itself was boundless, stretching a full thousand li. Even if Lu Yang and the others flew with maximum power, it would take them a considerable time to reach its edge.

Li Haoran’s expression turned grim as an ominous rumor came to mind. “I heard that in ancient times, ferocious birds would venture out to capture prey to feed their young. Meanwhile, we talented cultivators who train all year round possess pure spirit energy refined to an unparalleled degree. That makes us prime nourishment, most suitable for feeding fledglings!”

Man Gu was startled. He recalled his tribe’s records, which corroborated Li Haoran’s words. “Our Barbarian Tribe has similar records. Ancient Barbarians would venture out to hunt food to feed their young. The most suitable food in ancient times was the various ferocious beasts, whose pure spirit energy was refined to an unparalleled degree.”

Everyone looked at Man Gu with strange expressions, silently edging away from him.

Sensing the tense atmosphere, Li Haoran hastily added, “But the situation isn’t beyond salvage yet. I’ve also heard that ancient ferocious birds would pit the fledglings against captured cultivators in combat to train their young. Usually, the cultivation levels of the fledgling and the cultivator would match. If we can defeat the fledglings, we may have a chance to escape.”

A gust of black wind swept past, causing the group to shiver with a bone-piercing chill.

They looked up to see the shadowy figure reveal its true form—an enormous Peng bird. Its spread wings spanned a thousand li, and its feathers were as black as ink. The nest was shrouded in its shadow. It then shrank in size, transforming into a human form, with the appearance of a man past middle age. He had narrow, deeply set eyes that gleamed ruthlessly.

It was the Kunpeng Tribe’s old ancestor, the Black Feather Venerable Lord!

“This esteemed one has invited you all here to ask important questions. You must not lie!

“Are you all really disciples of the Five-Elements Sect? How has Shangguan Yu been recently?”

Shangguan Yu, Qiu Jin’an’s mother, was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

The group, “...”

The identity as Five-Elements Sect disciples doesn’t seem as safe as we’d imagined.

Noticing their silence, the Black Feather Venerable Lord frowned slightly. “Are you not Five-Elements Sect disciples? That shouldn’t be. Didn’t you execute the Five-Elements Combat Tactic?

“You don’t know Shangguan Yu? But that’s not right either. I heard she often mingles among young cultivators like you. And you have those wooden tokens for protection; Shangguan Yu must have given them to you.”

The wooden tokens the Black Feather Venerable Lord mentioned were from their previous study exchange at the Five-Elements Sect. Upon seeing the Jianmu Tree, Shangguan Yu had made Lu Yang and the others call her “jiejie.” As a reward, she took a small branch section and crafted it into wooden tokens, gifting them to the group, who still wore those wooden tokens around their necks.

Lu Yang asked cautiously, “Senior...are you very close with Shangguan-jiejie?”

The Black Feather Venerable Lord revealed a smile that said it was a given. “Back when Shangguan Yu and I were still unaccomplished in our cultivation, we met in the East Sea. I was the one who guided her on a tour of the East Sea. Together, we explored secret domains, searched for immortal grasses, overcame hardships, and weathered difficulties. If not for Qiu Duanya’s sweet talk deceiving her heart, we two would have long tied the knot!

“If it weren’t for Qiu Duan’ya, Qiu Jin’an would have been my son!”

Qiu Duan’ya was Qiu Jin’an’s father, the previous sect leader of the Five-Elements Sect.

“What, haven’t you heard her speak of me?” the Black Feather Venerable Lord asked with displeasure upon noticing Lu Yang and the others looking utterly dumbfounded.

He had secretly admired Shangguan Yu for a long time but never dared to go to Great Xia to see her. Hearing that there were Five-Elements Sect disciples in the East Sea, he decided to take action personally, “inviting” Lu Yang and the others back to inquire about her recent situation.

For the sake of his pride, the Black Feather Venerable Lord had concealed his face when “inviting” them, worried about being recognized by outsiders. He saw through their disguises at a glance, but that was inconsequential. Since the five of them could perform the Five-Elements Combat Tactic and possessed the wooden tokens, he believed they were undoubtedly disciples of the Five-Elements Sect.

“Uh, actually, we are disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect,” Lu Yang explained awkwardly, bracing himself.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect? Tang Shengyi’s grand-disciples?”

Seeing the Black Feather Venerable Lord’s expression threatening to shift from sunny to overcast, Lu Yang hurriedly added, “But we have a very good relationship with Shangguan-jiejie. She visited our Dao-Seeking Sect, and I was the one who hosted her.”

Hearing this, the Black Feather Venerable Lord’s expression improved. “Then how has she been recently?”

Lu Yang pondered for a moment and replied, “She seemed quite happy from what I saw.” This was the truth. Among the Transcendent Tribulation cultivators Lu Yang had met, Shangguan Yu was the most lively and cheerful.

“Does she have any plans to remarry?” The Black Feather Venerable Lord asked the most crucial question.

Lu Yang recalled Grandpa Ba’s unrequited longing for Shangguan Yu and figured she likely had no interest in him.

“Probably not.”

The Black Feather Venerable Lord hung his head, thoroughly dejected and disappointed. “So be it. It seems the predestined affinity between us has not yet arrived. What transpired here must not be disclosed to outsiders. Should I learn that this matter has been leaked, you all shall face punishment!”

“Yes,” the group hastily agreed, not daring to refuse.

“However, my Kunpeng Tribe is well-versed in etiquette. Since you have come to our tribe, we must offer proper hospitality.”

Once again, the Black Feather Venerable Lord enveloped the group in a water sphere. Transforming back into a black-winged great Peng bird, he soared out of the nest with a whoosh, diving downward.

North of the East Sea was a forest growing within the waters, the lofty trees reaching the clouds. The Black Feather Venerable Lord’s nest was constructed upon the tallest tree.

Below the nest lay the Kunpeng Tribe’s settlement. The group witnessed a giant Kun, accompanied by churning seawater and surging waves, momentarily breaking free from the sea’s surface and rising like a moving island. Its fish scales shimmered with a peculiar light, gradually dissolving and being replaced by robust feathers as it transformed into a Peng bird, soaring across the sky.

The Black Feather Venerable Lord brought the group to the Kunpeng Tribe’s chieftain.

Upon seeing the old ancestor suddenly bring six people over, the Kunpeng Tribe Chieftain quickly bowed. “Greetings, Old Ancestor.” freewebnovel.com

“These six are esteemed guests of our tribe. You must treat them with the utmost hospitality.”

“Yes yes yes.” The Kunpeng Tribe nodded repeatedly. He always handled matters instructed by the old ancestor to the best of his abilities.

“Chieftain Xiao?” Meng Jingzhou blurted upon seeing the Kunpeng Tribe’s chieftain.

Isn’t this the Chieftain Xiao who visited the Meng Family during the New Year and even gave me lucky yasui money?

Chieftain Xiao was taken aback. Seeing through Meng Jingzhou’s disguise, he appeared even more surprised than Meng Jingzhou. “Eldest Young Master Meng?

“Your Meng Family came directly for the Old Ancestor just to collect a debt?!”

Chapter 765: The Kunpeng Tribe Chieftain’s Untimely Tragedy

“Someone from the Meng Family?” The Black Feather Venerable Lord had a strange expression, not expecting this layer to Meng Jingzhou’s identity.

He was aware of the debt relationship between the Kunpeng Tribe and the Meng Family, but as the old ancestor of the tribe, his status and position meant he would never personally go to the Meng Family to borrow money or pay New Year’s greetings. Such matters were handled by Chieftain Xiao, accompanied by the elders.

The Kunpeng Tribe had its own sea market. In previous years, funds had become tight due to poor management. Borrowing spirit stones from other sea tribes or East Sea cultivators would inevitably place them in a subordinate position in future dealings. That was why they had gone to Great Xia to borrow from the Meng Family.

Naturally, the Black Feather Venerable Lord couldn’t admit he had personally captured the creditors, for it would tarnish his image. “They came to me of their own accord.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Venerable Lord, you live in such a high place. How exactly did we fly up there?

Lu Yang quietly asked Meng Jingzhou. “How many spirit stones does the Kunpeng Tribe owe your family?”

Meng Jingzhou shook his head. “How would I know? I didn’t even know the Kunpeng Tribe had borrowed spirit stones.”

The Black Feather Venerable Lord quietly asked Chieftain Xiao. “How many spirit stones do we owe the Meng Family?”

“We still have six billion spirit stones unpaid.”

“Are we able to repay it?”

Chieftain Xiao gritted his teeth, as if he had made up his mind. “Our spirit stone financials have been tight recently. However, I heard that in Great Xia, Fusion cultivators can work as bodyguards. The current rate is one million spirit stones. If I work as a bodyguard for a year, the debt would almost be cleared.”

“Is there another way?” The Black Feather Venerable Lord frowned. It’d be too shameful to have the tribe chieftain work outside as a bodyguard.

“Yes. The wages for a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator as a bodyguard are even higher.”

The Black Feather Venerable Lord, “...”

Looks like there’s no other choice but for you to become a bodyguard.

“Uh, we’re just passing through the Kunpeng Tribe and taking a casual look around. We’re not here to collect debts,” Meng Jingzhou said. He dared not mention the bird nest incident.

Judging by Chieftain Xiao’s behavior, he likely wasn’t aware of the relationship between Shangguan Yu and the Black Feather Venerable Lord. Otherwise, when he went to Great Xia to visit for the New Year, he would have inquired about Shangguan Yu, and the Black Feather Venerable Lord wouldn’t have needed to personally capture and question them.

“Really?” Chieftain Xiao was overjoyed. He had been prepared to slave away like an ox and a horse for Meng Jingzhou.

“Really.”

In this moment, Meng Jingzhou was no longer a creditor but an honored guest in Chieftain Xiao’s eyes.

“Hurry up and pour tea for Eldest Young Master Meng,” Chieftain Xiao instructed. He looked around; everyone was either a guest or the old ancestor, so he had to pour the tea for Meng Jingzhou himself.

The Black Feather Venerable Lord felt awkward for staying, so he spread his wings and soared back to his old nest.

It was clear Chieftain Xiao was generous. Although the tea leaves weren’t as good as Wudao Enlightenment Tea, they were still top-grade, second only to it.

“Nephew Meng, I heard you’ve joined the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“Yes. These are my junior brothers and sisters.” Meng Jingzhou acted all natural as he counted Lu Yang as his junior brother.

“Her too?” Chieftain Xiao looked in surprise at Su Yiren leaning against Li Haoran’s shoulder. Her age and cultivation don’t make her seem like a disciple.

“No, she is Junior Brother Li’s fiancée.”

Chieftain Xiao secretly drew in a sharp breath, quite envious of Li Haoran. If I had such good luck, I could have become the chieftain three hundred years earlier.

He laughed heartily. “To think the Old Ancestor is so polite even to Dao-Seeking Sect disciples. It appears your name carries considerable weight, Nephew Meng.”

“Why do you say that?” Meng Jingzhou was puzzled. “Is there some story behind it?”

“It seems you’re unaware of the conflict between the Old Ancestor and Senior Tang Shengyi.” This was supposed to be a secret not to be divulged. However, Chieftain Xiao was in high spirits, and the more he looked at Meng Jingzhou, the more he found him pleasing to the eye, so he figured it wouldn’t hurt to talk about it.

“That was four thousand years ago. At the time, the Old Ancestor’s cultivation level was similar to yours. Two cultivators from Great Xia came to train in the East Sea—Senior Tang Shengyi and Senior Shangguan Yu.

“Senior Tang Shengyi was fishing in the East Sea, using fairly precious pills as bait. Discerning the pills’ value, the Old Ancestor transformed into a Kun fish, ate the pills, and immediately fled, absolutely refusing to be hooked. After several such incidents, Senior Tang Shengyi suffered heavy losses. Thus, he used a transformation technique to turn himself into a pill and asked Senior Shangguan Yu to cast him into the water as bait.

“The Old Ancestor was careless and ended up taking the bait, swallowing the pill that was Senior Tang Shengyi.

“Seeing this, Senior Tang Shengyi reverted to his original form and beat the Old Ancestor until he was vomiting and begging for mercy.

“Seeing the bait had been taken, Senior Shangguan Yu yanked the fishing rod hard, reeling in both the Old Ancestor and Senior Tang Shengyi.

“The two fought from the water into the sky, and from the sky back into the water. Senior Tang Shengyi consistently overpowered the Old Ancestor. Back then, the Old Ancestor was a proud prodigy, undefeated in all his battles. Having never received a beating like this before, he was beaten to tears. That was how the matter concluded.

“Senior Shangguan was kind-hearted, comforting the injured Old Ancestor and healing his wounds. She even berated Senior Tang Shengyi for hitting too hard.

“I reckon it was from that time that the Old Ancestor developed feelings for Senior Shangguan. He thought it was a secret, but it’s actually been common knowledge for ages.”

Chieftain Xiao grew more excited as he spoke. He had visited many old seniors to find out what had happened back then. That was how he had pieced together the events.

“When Senior Tang saw the Old Ancestor crying, he even captured it with a recording orb. I once visited your sect and asked Senior Tang for a copy of that recording orb. Truly, I laugh every time I watch it.” Chieftain Xiao slapped his thigh, laughing until tears came out.

Lu Yang thought, Good thing I said earlier that I’m close with Shangguan-jiejie. Otherwise, based on what Grand-Shifu did, the Black Feather Venerable Lord hanging us from the bird nest would be considered lenient.

“And there’s more! Later, they roamed the East Sea, exploring secret domains and searching for immortal herbs. Whenever danger arose, either Senior Tang would throw the Old Ancestor out to block the threat, or the Old Ancestor would throw Senior Tang out to block the threat.

“When it was time to part ways, the Old Ancestor considered whether he should confess to Senior Shangguan. Senior Tang said, ‘Why not let the heavens decide? Pluck a feather and say “don’t confess,” then pluck another and say “confess.” When you pluck the last one, you’ll have your answer.’

“The Old Ancestor asked if it would hurt. Senior Tang said, ‘If you’re afraid of even a little pain like this, how can you speak of loving her?’

“The Old Ancestor clenched his teeth and spent the night plucking feathers until he was finally bare. The final result was ‘confess.’ Then, he went completely naked... Hahahaha! Senior Tang has a recording. I even asked him for a copy.

“Before he could even confess, Senior Shangguan was scared off.

“After Senior Shangguan returned to Great Xia, the Old Ancestor sent her love letters. In his nervousness, he forgot to write his name. The letters described their experiences in the East Sea, so Senior Shangguan thought they were from Senior Tang.”

Meng Jingzhou watched Chieftain Xiao, who was laughing without restraint, and kindly reminded him, “Chieftain Xiao, perhaps you would like to look behind you?”

Chieftain Xiao couldn’t control the smile on his face as he turned to look behind him.

Then, he couldn’t smile anymore. He saw the Black Feather Venerable Lord, his face as black as ink.

The Black Feather Venerable Lord said coldly, “Mingli, I’ve observed your cultivation hasn’t progressed recently. Perhaps you’ve grown lax. Come, let’s step outside and practice.”

Chapter 766: The Beating Was Still Too Lenient

The uproarious laughter of Chieftain Xiao Mingli[1] gradually withered, eventually turning into a hollow, forced chuckle.

The Black Feather Venerable Lord extended a claw and clamped it onto Chieftain Xiao’s shoulder, his gaze as frigid as if he were looking at a corpse.

“O-Old Ancestor... we have guests present. Let’s not make ourselves a spectacle.” Chieftain Xiao used Lu Yang and the others as a shield. freewebnovel.com

Despite usually being conscious about his image, the Black Feather Venerable Lord could no longer be bothered with appearances. He seized Chieftain Xiao by the neck.

Ever eager to learn, Lu Yang was greatly inspired by listening to Chieftain Xiao’s storytelling. He had already taken out a recording orb, hoping to record the final moments of Chieftain Xiao’s life.

Unfortunately, the Black Feather Venerable Lord gave no such opportunity. He directly dragged Chieftain Xiao as he flew off to his nest above.

Soon, a shrill, mournful bird screech echoed above the Kunpeng Tribe. All the Kunpeng tribesmen paused their tasks and looked up at the sky in confusion, unsure where the cry had come from.

Suddenly, the cries ceased.

Chieftain Xiao had died in pursuit of his heart’s desires—a fitting end.

“Ahem ahem, the Old Ancestor is really ruthless. He knocked me out cold in the end.” Chieftain Xiao staggered back moments after the plaintive cries vanished. His face was bruised and swollen, and a golden feather was still embedded in his head. “I wonder how long I was out.”

“Chieftain Xiao, are you alright?” Meng Jingzhou inquired out of courtesy, though he knew the answer. “The Black Feather Venerable Lord was too harsh.”

“Being alive means I’m fine. My luck just wasn’t good this time, and I got caught exposing the Old Ancestor’s secrets. So many people in the tribe know about the Old Ancestor’s embarrassing past; why doesn’t he teach them a lesson?” Chieftain Xiao grumbled indignantly.

“The entire Kunpeng Tribe knows about the Black Feather Venerable Lord’s affairs from his youth?”

“Of course,” Chieftain Xiao asserted confidently. “Whenever I ask whether they know about the Old Ancestor’s affairs, if they say no, I make sure to recount the entire story for them.”

Meng Jingzhou drew a sharp breath, feeling that the Black Feather Venerable Lord’s beating had still been too lenient.

Lu Yang surmised that Chieftain Xiao’s strength likely ranked second within the Kunpeng Tribe. If his ranking were any lower, the Black Feather Venerable Lord likely wouldn’t have left him alive.

Indeed, Lu Yang’s conjecture was correct. Within the Kunpeng Tribe, Chieftain Xiao’s strength was second only to the Black Feather Venerable Lord’s, surpassing even the older generation of kunpeng.

“Originally, I intended to personally show you around the Kunpeng Tribe as a proper host,” Chieftain Xiao said, hissing as he rubbed his face. “But these injuries won’t heal anytime soon. Covering my face while I guide you around would still create a poor impression.”

He transmitted an auditory message to his son. “Xinghai, stop cultivating. Come here.”

Soon, a golden-winged great Peng bird, several dozen zhang tall, descended outside Chieftain Xiao’s home. Seeing his father in human form, he also transformed, revealing himself as a handsome young man with bluish-green eyes and golden hair.

“This is my youngest son, Xiao Xinghai.”[2]

Xiao Xinghai was startled to see his father bruised and swollen. “Dad, what happened to you?”

“It’s nothing. I fell.”

“Fell onto a turtle shell from the Xuanwu Tribe?”

“Shoo shoo shoo! Don’t ask questions you shouldn’t.” Chieftain Xiao fumed, wanting to give the little brat a good spanking. “These six are friends from the Dao-Seeking Sect. They’re around your age. Entertain them on my behalf.”

On the Kunpeng Tribe’s territory, Lu Yang and the others dared not risk offending the Black Feather Venerable Lord by impersonating Five-Elements Sect disciples.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect, one of the Five Great Immortal Sects in Great Xia?” Xiao Xinghai was quite surprised.

Only a week had passed since the Vast Sea Daoist Lord and the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had clashed. News that the Dao-Seeking Sect housed a half-immortal had not yet reached the Kunpeng Tribe, which was located deep in the northern part of the East Sea.

If Xiao Xinghai were aware, he would have been even more surprised.

“Then do you know Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou?”

“I am Lu Yang, and this is my junior brother, Meng Jingzhou.” Lu Yang rushed to be the first to introduce themselves.

“No, that’s not right. You don’t look like the portraits I’ve seen.”

“We’ve altered our appearances because our Dao-Seeking Sect has many enemies in the East Sea.”

Xiao Xinghai recalled that eight of the Dao-Seeking Nine had bounties on their heads and understood Lu Yang’s meaning.

“Then let’s go. I’ll show you around.”

Xiao Xinghai was extremely excited to encounter such famous talents from Great Xia. He transformed back into a golden-winged great Peng bird to carry Lu Yang and the others. His golden feathers resembled glazed gold, shimmering brilliantly under the sunlight.

After sitting on Xiao Xinghai’s back and leaving Chieftain Xiao’s home, the group finally had the chance to behold the living environment of the Kunpeng Tribe.

Vast groves of Xunmu Trees were rooted in the East Sea, standing thousands or even tens of thousands of zhang tall. Half of their trunks were submerged in the sea, while the other half rose above the water. Their dense, interwoven branches formed a canopy that blocked the sunlight overhead, creating a cool and refreshing shade beneath.

The Kunpeng Tribe had two types of dwellings: some hollowed out sections of the Xunmu Trees, while others built enormous bird nests.

Chieftain Xiao’s home belonged to the former.

Due to the massive size of Kunpeng tribesmen, their dwellings were correspondingly huge. Tree hollow entrances were commonly several dozen zhang high. Standing before such an entrance, Lu Yang and the others felt as if they had stumbled into an ancient nation of titans.

From time to time, great Peng birds would fly past them, casting curious glances their way.

“Prepare to enter the sea!” Xiao Xinghai warned loudly. His feathers transformed into golden scales, reminiscent of a legendary golden dragon.

Riding on the back of the golden great Kun, Lu Yang and the others clung tightly to its dorsal fin. Icy seawater surged from all sides, engulfing them. The Water-Repelling Pearls on their chests took effect, neutralizing the water pressure and allowing them to move freely within the sea.

The underwater world presented a living scene entirely different from the surface. Countless great kun swam through the waters, some even larger than Xiao Xinghai, though none possessed scales as flawless as his.

The number of Kun fish was clearly more than that of the great Peng birds.

“Most of our tribesmen enjoy life in the water,” Xiao Xinghai explained.

Aside from the Kun fish, many other nearby sea tribes were also present, coming to the Kunpeng Tribe’s sea market to trade goods.

The market’s scale was comparable to that of Penglai Island’s sea market. In this regard, the Kunpeng lived up to its reputation as one of the Ten Great Races of the East Sea.

This was a place even Qin Haoran and Su Yiren had never visited. Tao Yaoye couldn’t take her eyes off the ineffably beautiful sights, hoping to adapt them to a scene for a future Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.

I fall from the ship, and Senior Brother Lu Yang jumps into the sea. Seeing that I have stopped breathing, he kisses me to breathe life back into me. What a beautiful scene.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, if I fall into the sea, would you save me?”

Lu Yang looked Tao Yaoye up and down in surprise. Seeing her move effortlessly in the water, he couldn’t understand why she would ask such a thing.

“Junior Sister, has water gotten into your brain too?”

“...I meant that I want to film a Dreamlike Bubble Mirage with the East Sea as a backdrop. One of the scenes will be me falling into the sea and you rescuing me.”

Realization dawned upon Lu Yang, and he said excitedly, “So that’s how it is. In that case, Junior Sister, you falling into the sea must be the work of the East Sea Dragon Tribe. After I’ve rescued you, I will battle the East Sea Dragon Tribe for three hundred rounds and rip out their tendons. To take revenge on me, the East Sea Dragon Tribe will threaten to flood Penglai Island. I will then heroically appear and sacrifice myself before the Dragon Tribe.

“Afterward, Big Senior Sister will appear, collect my three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls, and create a lotus root body. I will be reborn through it and wreak havoc upon the Dragon Tribe, returning peace to the East Sea.

“Is that how you want to film it, Junior Sister?”

“...Then what about me?”

Man Gu, listening nearby, was puzzled. “Didn’t you get rescued?”

1. “Mingli” means something like “understands reason.” ☜

2. “Xinghai” literally means stars and sea. ☜

Chapter 767: Gourd Brothers Wreak Havoc in the Sea

“You can film Dreamlike Bubble Mirages? I thought only Fan Chong of Penglai Island could do that!” Xiao Xinghai grew interested in the topic upon overhearing Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye’s conversation.

Lu Yang replied with pride, “What’s Fan Chong? Nothing more than a trivial person. This is my junior sister, Tao Yaoye. She’s not only beautiful but also clever. Dreamlike Bubble Mirages are her invention!”

Tao Yaoye’s cheeks flushed slightly. She pretended she didn’t hear Man Gu’s earlier response.

“As for Fan Chong of Penglai Island, his version is pirated. If someone like him were in our Great Xia, he would have been thrown in prison long ago. Junior Sister Tao is the original creator.”

“So impressive.” Xiao Xinghai’s eyes lit up. “Can you assign me a role then? Either hero or villain works.” Xiao Xinghai had long wished to become a character in a Dreamlike Bubble Mirage. If nothing else, this thing is famous.

Tao Yaoye felt that the Kunpeng Tribe had been quite hospitable. The Black Feather Venerable Lord hadn’t taken his anger out on them, Chieftain Xiao had regaled them with stories of mighty experts, and Xiao Xinghai had transformed into a Peng and a Kun to ferry them around.

“Alright.” It’s just one role anyway.

Lu Yang pondered. “What do you think of the earlier script? How about changing the Dragon Tribe to the Kunpeng Tribe, and you can play the Kunpeng who drags Junior Sister Tao into the water?”

“Sure, sure!” Hearing he would have so much screen time, Xiao Xinghai immediately agreed.

“Then what about me? Can I get a role too?” Meng Jingzhou sidled over to join the fun.

Lu Yang pushed Meng Jingzhou aside with disdain. “The roles are filled. No room for you.”

Meng Jingzhou said enthusiastically, “How is there no room? Didn’t you plan to return your flesh and bones to your parents? I can play your father.”

Li Haoran also leaned in. “Yiran and I are engaged. How about we play the parents?” To play Lu Yang’s father, Li Haoran was willing to sacrifice his dignity by leveraging his looks and act as a kept pretty boy.

“Get lost! How about you two wreak havoc in the sea, and I’ll be your father.”

“Fine, fine, fine, I’ll change roles... But this won’t do. Your script barely has any major roles.” Meng Jingzhou felt that someone of his stature couldn’t possibly play some obscure minor character in a Dreamlike Bubble Mirage. “Think of a way to revise the script.”

“Brother Lu, can you give me a role too?” Man Gu moved closer; he also wanted to be featured in a Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.

Lu Yang felt a headache coming on. How would there be so many important roles in Nezha Wreaks Havoc in the Sea?

Tough.

Suddenly, a flash of inspiration struck Lu Yang, and he thought of a solution. “We can change everyone’s origins. Four gourds grow from an innate vine. The gourds crack open, and four people emerge.

Su Yiren was a reclusive cultivator and unsuitable to appear in a Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.

After all, Su Yiren was experienced, unlike Lu Yang and his blockheaded companions. She could see that Tao Yaoye harbored feelings for Lu Yang.

For Tao Yaoye to construct the scenes for the Dreamlike Bubble Mirages, she needed real-world places and events as templates for modification. If she didn’t witness Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, and Li Haoran fighting a Kunpeng, she couldn’t construct the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.

~~~

Tao Yaoye changed her attire, donning a Penglai Island uniform that highlighted her playful cuteness.

Crack. The first to ripen was a red gourd.

Junior Sister Tao, you have to act more convincingly,” Lu Yang whispered.

Tao Yaoye murmured a barely audible “mmm,” soft as a mosquito’s buzz.

Chapter 768: Four Gourd Brothers

Tao Yaoye’s cheeks burned a fierce scarlet as her mind raced, trying to figure out what she should do next.

What was the arrangement in the script? After being rescued by Senior Brother Lu Yang, how am I supposed to react?

Her nervous gaze fixed on Lu Yang’s eyes, where she detected an almost imperceptible flicker of excitement lurking in their depths.

Could it be that despite his talk about acting more convincingly, Senior Brother Lu Yang is also flustered while carrying me in his arms?

However, for various reasons, Lu Yang hadn’t learned the Dragon Transformation Mantra but had instead learned Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth.

“Meanwhile, look at our Kunpeng Tribe. We don’t even have half a half-immortal. It’s perfectly normal for me to learn the Dragon Tribe’s strengths. If we don’t learn from the strengths of other races, how can we make the Kunpeng Tribe stronger?”

Lu Yang felt that Xiao Xinghai made a rather reasonable point. Judging that he had fought enough with Xiao Xinghai, he consciously allowed himself to be defeated, making way for the next gourd brother to enter the scene.

Little Gourd Lu Yang, shimmering with four kinds of light, made his entrance!

A perfect finale.

After all, it was acting; they wouldn’t really rip out a dragon’s tendon. This was a prop provided by Xiao Xinghai—a sturgeon tendon.

To celebrate the conclusion of the first act, Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu lit a fire, roasting the sturgeon tendon before sharing it with everyone.

“What a great flavor!” Xiao Xinghai exclaimed, his eyes lighting up after taking a bite of the steaming roasted sturgeon tendon. Sea tribes rarely used barbecue as a cooking method.

Considering Yun Zhi wasn’t fond of public appearances, during the script discussions, the group changed her character to the Gourd Immortal who planted the Innate Gourd seeds.

“Alright.” Everyone was on a roll, growing more fervent the more they acted.

Suddenly, Su Yiren pointed at a mass of mist floating above the sea not far away, looking bewildered. “What is that?”

Xiao Xinghai turned to look, and his expression changed dramatically. “Oh no! It’s a Fata Morgana! Run!”

“Fata Morgana?”

Hearing this, Su Yiren summoned her powers, pulling everyone as she ran in the opposite direction. As she ran, she activated the power of rules.

“I hereby establish the rule: [The Mist Shall Disperse]!”

The mist remained completely unaffected.

The mass of mist moved far too quickly. Before Su Yiren could fly a distance away, the mist enveloped them, swallowing them whole.

Chapter 769: Fata Morgana

The Fata Morgana was a mysterious phenomenon that had long circulated in legends of the East Sea. It was said that the Mirage-Clam Tribe was once immensely powerful, ranking among the Ten Great Races of the East Sea. Their most renowned divine ability was the Fata Morgana. Eight thousand years ago, an old ancestor accidentally fell into qi deviation while comprehending a spell and lost control of the Fata Morgana, which swallowed the Mirage-Clam Tribe’s core members.

From then on, the Mirage-Clam Tribe fell from its position as one of the Ten Great Races. The Fata Morgana that went out of control drifted aimlessly through the East Sea, devouring living beings, be they human or seafolk.

Some living beings managed to walk out of the Fata Morgana. They either emerged unscathed or insane and deranged.

Still, more vanished within the Fata Morgana, never to appear again.

According to the recollections of those who came out safely, they encountered the vanished individuals inside the Fata Morgana. However, those people were controlled by illusions and were extremely hostile.

Once, several Transcendent Tribulation demon emperors joined forces, attempting to disperse the Fata Morgana. They ran into the Mirage-Clam old ancestor, who had already gone insane. The old ancestor battled the group until he died from exhaustion. However, even after his death, the Fata Morgana did not dissipate.

Since then, no one had attempted to deal with the Fata Morgana. Instead, it was regarded as a moving calamity that everyone should flee upon sight.

~~~

“What? The life tablet can’t sense Xinghai’s location anymore?!” Chieftain Xiao was recuperating from his injuries when he discovered that Xiao Xinghai’s life tablet had extinguished for no reason. This didn’t signify death but rather that he had moved beyond the life tablet’s detection range.

“Going beyond the life tablet’s range means they’ve entered a fairly high-level secret domain? No, that’s not right. Although Xinghai likes to fool around, he wouldn’t dare to lead guests into a secret domain without a word!

“Could they have been swept into some place... Damn it, it’s the Fata Morgana!” Chieftain Xiao quickly realized.

~~~

“Yo, Chieftain Xiao, why do you have the time to come here today?!” The Mirage-Clam Tribe Chieftain hurried out to greet Chieftain Xiao upon hearing the latter had arrived.

Chieftain Xiao had no leisure for pleasantries with the Mirage-Clam Tribe Chieftain now. His emerald-green eyes icily stared at the Mirage-Clamb Tribe Chieftain, his hooked beak poking the latter’s forehead.

“Let me tell you, my son and my tribe’s esteemed guests are trapped inside that Fata Morgana your tribe created. If anything happens to even one of them, you can expect retaliation!”

The Mirage-Clam Tribe Chieftain turned ashen pale.

“Tell me, how exactly does one escape from the Fata Morgana?!” Chieftain Xiao was prepared to enter the Fata Morgana for a search and rescue operation. Before coming to the Mirage-Clam Tribe, he had already dispatched people to locate the moving mist near their territory, confirming his suspicion.

The Mirage-Clam Tribe Chieftain looked as if he wanted to cry but had no tears. “Chieftain Xiao, that thing isn’t a Fata Morgana at all! If it were, our tribe wouldn’t be completely helpless!”

“It’s not a Fata Morgana?”

“Yes! Eight thousand years ago, an old ancestor discovered a mysterious space. He said if he could comprehend its secrets, he might become a half-immortal. For that purpose, he set up layer upon layer of arrays and entered seclusion.

“Later, no one knows what the old ancestor did, but the mysterious space erupted, becoming a mass of mist. Those arrays proved utterly useless. The old ancestor’s seclusion site was at our tribe’s core area, so when the mysterious space erupted, it devoured the majority of our core members.”

Chieftain Xiao’s expression grew increasingly grave.

~~~

“What do we do now?” Lu Yang’s group was trapped within the Fata Morgana, not daring to move.

They attempted to scout out the place with their spiritual consciousness, only to find that their spiritual consciousness could barely advance an inch here; even Su Yiren at the Fusion Stage was no exception.

Only Man Gu wasn’t knowledgeable about this aspect and was unaware of the Fata Morgana’s terrors. After Xiao Xinghai’s brief explanation, he was also frightened.

“According to the recollections of those who walked out safely, you can leave this place regardless of whether you stay in place or wander aimlessly!” Xiao Xinghai recalled the information. When he mentioned “walked out safely,” he referred to those who hadn’t gone insane.

“So we can leave no matter what we do?” Man Gu asked.

“It’s not that simple. Those who went insane and those who vanished within the Fata Morgana probably all did the same things, so whether we emerge safely is a matter of luck.

“With good luck, nothing will happen, and the Fata Morgana will leave us. With slightly bad luck, you’d get attacked by someone previously trapped here, but after dragging it out for a while, you can still leave. According to records, more than one Fusion cultivator is trapped here. With even worse luck, you could either get killed or be driven insane by the illusions.”

“Immortal Fairy, do you have any solution for this situation?” The Fata Morgana was famous throughout the East Sea. Lu Yang knew this wasn’t a situation he could handle himself; he needed to ask for help.

Transformed into a mermaid, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was lying on the sea and sleeping. Lu Yang’s words roused her, and she woke up reluctantly. “What is it... yawn... What happened?”

“We’re trapped in a Fata Morgana.”

“Fata Morgana? The Mirage-Clam Tribe’s divine ability... yawn... Isn’t that something you can disperse with a breath?

“Wait, this isn’t a Fata Morgana. How could the Mirage-Clamb Tribe have the capability to create something like this?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was well aware of the Mirage-Clamb Tribe’s abilities.

“Then what is this?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned, her tone solemn. “A remnant site of an immortal battle! Both combatants were immortals. This place is filled with traces left by the immortal battle and their Dao Fruits! Tell me, why did you say this was a Fata Morgana earlier?”

Lu Yang recounted all the legends about the Fata Morgana.

“A Fata Morgana created by the Mirage-Clamb Tribe’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivator... That’s definitely a lie.

“It’s more likely that the Mirage-Clamb Tribe’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivator sensed the traces of an immortal battle here and attempted to use this method to comprehend an Incipient Dao Fruit. In the end, he accidentally lost control and caused the residual power of this remnant immortal battleground to erupt and devour him as well.”

“Then whose battlefield was this?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy carefully surveyed the remnant immortal battle site. “I can sense that one of the parties was the Qilin Immortal. His Law of the Jungle Dao Fruit suits every demon race—it’s their inherent nature. Perhaps the Mirage-Clam Tribe’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivator vaguely sensed it too!

“But that’s not right. In my recollection, after the Qilin Immortal became an immortal, he never experienced such a battle!”

Lu Yang also grew nervous, realizing something was amiss. “Is it the battle between the Four Ancient Immortals and the mastermind after you perished, Immortal Fairy?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “Probably not. This battle wasn’t that extreme, but this was absolutely not a friendly spar—it was a fight to the death.”

Lu Yang pondered. How could this be? The Four Ancient Immortals’ enemy should only be the mastermind. Who else could the Qilin Immortal have fought?

Wait, there might actually be someone.

“Immortal Fairy, do you remember that after you perished, there was the Ember Legacy Dynasty? The Ember Legacy is suspected to have produced an immortal who deliberately erased the dynasty’s existence.

“Could the Qilin Immortal’s opponent have been the immortal born during the Ember Legacy Dynasty?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused, “An immortal born during the Ember Legacy Dynasty? That’s indeed possible.”

Chapter 770: You Toss, I Toss

Bang!

In that fleeting moment that the mist dispersed, the group saw their opponent clearly—a crab over three meters tall, holding up two claws. Its body was decayed, and its back was covered in moss. It was unclear how many years it had been dead.

“It’s a Fusion cultivator from the Tyrant Crab Tribe!” Su Yiren recognized its origin and cultivation level.

It wasn’t just the Tyrant Crab. Countless other seafolk and humans surrounded them, all dead yet still moving.

Li Haoran watched the mist warily, various meticulously refined magical treasures hovering around him. Cold sweat beaded on his forehead. “Next time, we should invite a fellow Daoist from the Corpse Driving Sect for a trip to the East Sea.”

The Tyrant Crab Fusion cultivator suddenly raised its claws and flung them forward. The two claws detached and flew out, aimed straight at Su Yiren’s waist, attempting to slice her in half!

“Spirit Pivot Marrow-Cleansing Mantra!” Su Yiren uttered. Her fair skin contained inexhaustible power as she directly met the giant crab’s attack. Despite the crab shell being renowned for its defense, it was dented by her two punches.

Those long-dead seafolk and humans followed the Tyrant Crab Fusion cultivator’s lead in the assault. They came in sundry aggressive forms: a leaping blue whale, a soaring storm petrel demon king, and a towering thousand-year-old turtle demon... Among them were aged monsters and once-peerless geniuses. However, their eras were too distant. Xiao Xinghai had only heard their names and couldn’t match them to their appearances.

“Form the array!” Lu Yang yelled.

The five once again executed the Five-Elements Combat Tactic, interlinking their spirit energy, allowing their combat power to multiply several times over.

“One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!” Lu Yang summoned the Sword-Cleansing Pond. Countless Sword-Cleansing Ponds filled the sky, descending like meteors. Be it seafolk or human, all below the Divine Transfiguration Stage were smashed into pulp. Even Divine Transfiguration cultivators were severely injured, their combat power sharply reduced.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” Meng Jingzhou performed Three Heads Six Arms. His body appeared to be cast from bronze and iron, and his muscles were like intertwined Qiu-Dragons. His fists stirred abounding, majestic momentum, each punch seemingly capable of shaking heaven and earth.

Man Gu swung his ten-thousand-jin heavy hammer, facing a blue whale head-on. Each collision caused violent sea waves, creating enormous whirlpools.

“Thousand Mechanisms Transformation!” Nine different types of magical treasures materialized around Li Haoran: a jade gourd, a precious cauldron, a small hammer, a wooden sword... The nine treasures ignited with true fire, forming a small array that blocked attacks from all sides.

“Metamorphic Immortal Physique!” Faced with jiangshi, the illusions Tao Yaoye was adept at were of little use. She resolutely decided to activate her Metamorphic Immortal Physique. She was shrouded in a milky-white light that transformed into pure white feathers, and her aura surged abruptly.

Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage!

She had borrowed power from her future self, temporarily reaching the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage. The cost was that her future self at the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage would regress to the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage at one point.

Tao Yaoye’s spirit energy grew exponentially like a breached floodgate. Even the four others within the array felt an unending stream of power.

Watching Lu Yang and the others display their mighty abilities, Xiao Xinghai was full of envy.

“Kunpeng Nine Transformations! Dragon Transformation Mantra!” Xiao Xinghai simultaneously performed two mighty abilities, transforming into a golden dragon that was a hundred zhang long and had four claws. The golden dragon sprouted a pair of golden wings, and each flap could stir boundless hurricanes.

“Roar!” Xiao Xinghai clashed with the thousand-year-old turtle demon valiantly. His strong dragon claws carved three deep gashes into the turtle’s shell.

This turtle demon was a famous Divine Transfiguration old devil in the East Sea a thousand years ago. Although it was of mixed blood, it had once defeated a Xuanwu Tribe member of the same level, eliciting a huge uproar at the time.

Meng Jingzhou glanced up at Xiao Xinghai in surprise. This kid’s cultivation does have some substance.

“Don’t get entangled with them. Keep running!” Lu Yang was deeply aware that wasting time here would only lead to their deaths. According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, more Fusion cultivators were continuously converging toward them.

Lu Yang wielded the Qingfeng Sword and Mingyue swords, using sword qi to cleave a path, though it was quickly swallowed by the mist again. Sitting in the Sword-Cleansing Pond, he charged recklessly. “Run this way!”

The group fought their way out through a path of blood.

As they ran, Lu Yang inquired with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Doesn’t the Qilin Immortal have the Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit? How does he have the means to control others?”

“You forgot. Lianyi’s Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit can control others, and the superior version of that is the Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit. A higher Dao Fruit possesses all the abilities of its lower Incipient Dao Fruits.

“However, the relationship between the Everlasting Dao Fruit and the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit doesn’t work like that.

“...The great array has shifted position again. There are quite distinct immortal traces ahead. Those immortal traces encompass fairly dense law comprehensions. Never mind you all, even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator can’t withstand such information overload at a glance and would go insane. That’s how people went mad before. Run east!”

The remnant immortal battleground was riddled with lethal dangers. Few who strayed into it managed to escape. Fortunately, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was here to assist, pointing out a clear path for Lu Yang.

The bloodstained group ran out of the mist, escaping with their lives. They had endured three bloody battles along the way. Although they were injured, they suffered only minor wounds.

“This immortal has already marked that remnant site. After your group settles down, Second-in-Command, you can return here. We’ll study this place carefully.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had long tossed Yun Zhi’s warnings to the back of her mind.

“Alright.”

Coincidentally, Lu Yang had also tossed them.

Chapter 771: Night Investigation of the Remnant Immortal Battleground

“We made it out alive?” Xiao Xinghai was still unable to believe it, his heart still pounding with lingering fear. This is the East Sea’s moving natural disaster. I’ve heard the chance of escaping from the Fata Morgana is less than ten percent, and escaping unscathed is less than one percent.

What secret treasure does Lu Yang possess? Its directions were so effective!

Tao Yaoye’s cultivation realm had fallen back to the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage. Her aura was feeble, and even consuming Qi Replenishment Pills was ineffective.

Seeing Tao Yaoye was so frail she might collapse, Lu Yang hurriedly supported her and asked with concern, “How are you feeling?” He wanted to take out pills to heal Tao Yaoye.

Tao Yaoye shook her head lightly, her voice faint. “This is the aftereffect of using the Metamorphic Immortal Physique. Pills don’t work. I need to convalesce quietly for a few days to recover on my own.”

“Where have we run to?” Meng Jingzhou attempted to find landmarks, but unfortunately, the sea’s surface was empty, save for the drifting mass of mist.

“Wait a moment.” Xiao Xinghai dipped his head into the sea, then lifted it, wiping his face. “Below us is the territory of the Luoyu Tribe. They’re considered a subordinate race to our Kunpeng race. I’m rather familiar with them.”

Just as Xiao Xinghai was about to lead everyone underwater, several hundred-zhang-long kunpeng flew from the distance, shouting with elation.

“Young Lord, you came out safely!”

“Uncle Kun, Uncle Yue, what brings you here?” Xiao Xinghai recognized them as his father’s trusted aides and dropped his guard.

“His Excellency the Tribe Chieftain heard that you and the esteemed guests were swallowed by the Fata Morgana. The Tribe Chieftain was so worried that he went to block the Mirage-Clam Tribe’s door. If he learns that you all have returned safely, who knows how happy he would be.”

Originally, Uncle Kun and Uncle Yue intended to take out healing pills for Lu Yang and the others. But when they saw the various pills that Lu Yang’s group poured from their own bottles, they abandoned the thought. Those pills had pill marks and pill fragrance.

With everyone returning safely, Chieftain Xiao was overjoyed. He hadn’t expected them to leave the Fata Morgana, and with no one insane at that.

“It’s good as long as you’re back, good that you’re back.” Chieftain Xiao arranged accommodations for everyone, letting them rest well.

~~~

Deep into the night, Lu Yang emerged from his meditative state. More accurately, he was deep in cultivation when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy woke him by swishing her tail.

“Go go go! The remnant site hasn’t drifted far yet,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said excitedly.

Although the Kunpeng Tribe didn’t need to sleep, they were accustomed to cultivating at night. Hence, not many were outside now—the perfect opportunity for covert action.

Lu Yang steered the Sword-Cleansing Pond, following the direction indicated by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. He flew out of the Kunpeng Tribe and soon found the aimlessly drifting mist.

If Lu Yang could see the surroundings clearly, he would have known it wasn’t because he didn’t encounter jiangshi, but that they fled in fright the moment they approached him.

“It’s perfectly normal. Although you can see this mist from the outside, this place is actually an isolated pocket dimension, far larger than the mist you see outside.

“No, there’s something over there. Go deeper.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy commanded, and Lu Yang obediently went further in.

“Go right. Yes, it’s here.” Following the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s instruction, Lu Yang crouched and picked up a jade bracelet from the ground.

“This is a Dragon-Pattern Bracelet. It was precisely because it was an immortal artifact that it could survive the battle.

If so, everything makes sense.

Although Little Ling was the strongest half-immortal, she still couldn’t match a full immortal. If the Ember Legacy Dynasty immortal wanted to eliminate her, she would be hard-pressed to resist.

The Qilin Immortal arrived in time, battled the opponent, and destroyed everything.

During the battle, Little Ling’s Dragon-Pattern Bracelet was left here.

“Immortal Fairy, since Senior Ao Ling is also a half-immortal, in order to see you, she would certainly need to use the Play-Dead Technique to endure the long ages, right?

“Correct.”

Lu Yang suddenly recalled something the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had mentioned. The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord had a friend who was killed by an immortal while in slumber because he knew of the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s existence.

How similar the methods are!

Chapter 772: Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit

Lu Yang took out a piece of red cloth and carefully wrapped the Dragon-Pattern Jade Bracelet with it.

This is a bona fide immortal artifact capable of withstanding multiple attacks from an immortal. Even though its energy is now depleted, it’s still immensely valuable.

“But why didn’t the other party make a move against Senior Lianyi? Did they not find her? That’s not right though. Senior Lianyi appeared in the Demon Region, and the entire cultivation world knew, so the opponent certainly was aware. Was there another reason for not taking action?

Maybe we should just ask Big Senior Sister to come and investigate. I can say the Everlasting Immortal Fairy controlled me to come here.

Lu Yang nodded. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had mentioned this before.

Only by emulating nature and returning to simplicity can one maintain eternal strength.

It was already exceedingly hard for a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator to comprehend one Incipient Dao Fruit. Who could be like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, changing Incipient Dao Fruits as she pleased?

“What is ‘Everlasting?’ It is nature. It is eternity. It encompasses both prosperity and decline. Hence, this immortal can both resurrect and self-destruct.” freewebnovel.com

Chapter 773: Rivalry Between Dragon and Phoenix

When Lu Yang visited Tao Yaoye, he brought a recording crystal as promised. The scenes within the recording orb were of immense value.

Weren’t you five supposed to be acting? How did it turn into a real fight while acting?

Perhaps this is a Kunpeng Tribe tradition—the old ancestor beats the chieftain, and the chieftain beats the son. The muscle memory is passed down through generations, Tao Yaoye mused randomly.

The recording orb also emitted Chieftain Xiao’s angry voice.

Fusion cultivator versus Nascent Soul cultivator—unsurprisingly, the battle was one-sided.

The bad news was that Chieftain Xiao had forbidden him from ingesting pills to recover.

This was a [Rule].

This is a theory I haven’t heard before.

Dragon blood wasn’t considered a pill and fell outside the [Rule].

Lu Yang and the other three carried a coffin, flying toward the Dragon Palace’s sea market.

Xiao Xinghai was a prominent prodigy in the East Sea. Carrying him on a stretcher to the Dragon Palace’s sea market would be somewhat embarrassing. Covering him with a coffin lid eliminated the concern of being recognized. The coffin was a magical treasure with the function of blocking spiritual consciousness.

One could call it killing multiple birds with one stone.

The Dragon Palace’s sea market was the largest sea market in the East Sea. It was a gathering place for individuals from all walks of life. Unlike Penglai Island’s sea market, which only humans visited, the Dragon Palace’s sea market had both seafolk and humans.

The Dragon Palace’s sea market was a mixed bag of fish and dragons, with crooks among honest folks. New things happened daily. But people carrying a coffin to tour around the sea market was a first.

“Who passed away?”

“This place is truly huge.” Lu Yang and the others descended, looking down at the Dragon Palace’s sea market. It resembled a colossal dragon adorned with numerous jewels, sleeping on the seabed. No matter how many sea tribes swam over it or how many buildings were built upon it, nothing could disturb this slumbering dragon.

At the end of the sea market stood an old, simple hall—the Dragon Palace, known to everyone in the East Sea.

Even though Lu Yang didn’t feel he was being treated unfairly.

Chapter 774: Coffin

Lu Yang ignored the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s incessant chatter, focusing on carrying the coffin.

“Speaking of which, the quality of this coffin is really quite good. According to Fellow Daoist Xinghai, it can even block the spiritual consciousness of a Fusion cultivator.”

Generally speaking, coffins in the cultivation world had the effect of blocking spiritual consciousness—a sign of respect for the deceased. But to refine a coffin to this level was truly rare.

“I keep feeling the style of this coffin looks familiar.” Lu Yang frowned, then suddenly remembered.

“Isn’t this the coffin First Elder often sleeps in?” When Lu Yang had just learned Close Horizon From Cliff and randomly teleported to a cliff, he had the fortune of barging into a tomb chamber built by First Elder. The coffin style in that chamber was extremely similar to the one Xiao Xinghai was lying in.

“First Elder probably built tombs all over the East Sea, and Fellow Daoist Xinghai found one.” Meng Jingzhou wasn’t surprised at all.

The East Sea was rife with similar legends: some genius would inadvertently enter a tomb, pass the trials left by predecessors, obtain their legacy and magical treasures, and soar to greatness from then on.

It was just that the magical treasure Xiao Xinghai obtained was a coffin.

Lu Yang felt that Meng Jingzhou’s words made sense. After all, wasn’t the Heaven Mandate Immortal buried as a burial object before rising to prominence?

This is all legacy passed down from history.

“According to Fellow Daoist Xinghai, the Dragon Tribe is extravagant, spending lavishly. They wouldn’t sell blood due to a lack of money; they usually sell blood because they have a request. Once the requested task is completed, they would repay with Dragon blood.

“Since Dragon blood is priceless, the difficulty of the requested tasks is also very great. Moreover, some tasks involve the Dragon Tribe’s privacy and aren’t suitable for public disclosure. Hence, such tasks are issued at covert contact points.”

“Is it inappropriate for us to carry a coffin around everywhere?” Man Gu asked. He could clearly feel the surrounding gazes converging on them.

No response.

“Oh right, the coffin blocks spiritual consciousness; auditory messages can’t be transmitted.” Meng Jingzhou recalled that his voice couldn’t get through unless they opened the coffin lid.

“Then we shall decide for Fellow Daoist Xinghai. Let’s find a place to store it... Hmm, ahead is the Luodi Merchant Guild. So they have a branch here too.” Meng Jingzhou smiled. The Luodi Merchant Guild’s business scope is quite broad, extending even to the East Sea.

In this aspect, our Meng Family isn’t lacking either; the East Sea and the Demon Region are also within our business scope.

“Perfect. Merchant guilds have temporary storage services for large items.”

At the sea market’s end, the Dragon Palace.

“A thief doesn’t leave empty-handed, so I respectfully took this coffin away! freewebnovel.com
