The three underlings tried and found it was indeed the case.

“So we put the supreme treasure in this coffin, then secretly transport it out by carrying the coffin?” the underling inquired. As expected of Big Brother! He considers things so thoroughly. No matter what, the Dragon Tribe won’t show such disrespect to the deceased and open a coffin for inspection. Such an outrageous act would surely make people suspect the Dragon Tribe has lost something very important.

The Dragon Tribe loves their face; they won’t do such a thing.

“Yes, but it’s not that simple. Carrying a coffin around the sea market is too ostentatious; it would attract the Dragon Tribe’s attention.”

“So what is your plan, Big Brother?”

“I know someone at the Luodi Merchant Guild; I’ve already made arrangements in advance. We’ll temporarily store the coffin at the merchant guild. After the heat dies down, we’ll retrieve it.

“Also, we need to disguise ourselves.” The big brother fished out four pills from the front of his robes. “These are pills I bought from Great Xia’s black market. They’re produced by a pill-concocting master of the Dao-Seeking Sect. It’s said that eating one can temporarily lower one’s cultivation realm. All four of us are at the Fusion Stage. If the Dragon Tribe investigates, they’ll definitely suspect Fusion cultivators first. That would be dangerous! If we lower our cultivation realms, the Dragon Tribe won’t suspect us!”

“Big Brother is wise!” The three underlings were impressed. Big Brother’s calculations leave nothing to chance; he considers every aspect.

The plan is flawless.

~~~

“Excuse me, may I ask if we can store a coffin here?” Lu Yang and the other three carried the coffin into the Luodi Merchant Guild and inquired politely.

Chapter 775: Good Service Attitude

“Judging by the time, they should be arriving about now,” Steward Liu from the merchant guild murmured.

As a steward, he didn’t need to stand at the front desk, but today was special; he couldn’t afford to be careless.

He had a private arrangement with the Juxuan Island Four Thieves. Although his cultivation was low, his status in the Luodi Merchant Guild and the leverage he held over them meant they wouldn’t dare cross him. It was an equal partnership.

Of course, the Juxuan Island Four Thieves also had leverage over him.

According to the plan, the Juxuan Island Four Thieves were supposed to come to the merchant guild today to store a coffin.

Generally, a merchant guild wouldn’t offer coffin storage services; after all, they weren’t a funeral parlor. Hence, he had been here all day, waiting for the Juxuan Island Four Thieves to arrive so that he could handle it personally.

“Old Liu, the Guildmaster is calling a brief meeting for all stewards and above,” another steward informed Steward Liu.

Steward Liu frowned. He hadn’t expected the guildmaster to call a meeting at such a critical moment. He wanted to refuse but was worried about raising suspicion. The guildmaster disliked anyone skipping meetings.

Troublesome. Looks like I’ll have to resign once I secure the Dragon Tribe’s supreme treasure.

It seems this matter will have to be delegated to a subordinate. But I can’t explicitly instruct them to accept a coffin. That would be far too blatant. Anyone would sense something is wrong right away.

He turned to a delicate-looking girl and instructed, “Su Yu, you must remember, our merchant guild’s mission is to serve the customer. No matter what request a customer makes, we must strive to fulfil it to the best of our ability. Do you understand?”

Su Yu was surprised that the usually cold and aloof Steward Liu was mentoring her. Deeply moved, she quickly replied, “I’ll keep that in mind, Steward Liu.”

Steward Liu nodded. Good, as long as you keep that in mind.

“Old Liu, hurry up!” his friend urged.

“Coming.”

~~~

Less than ten minutes later, the meeting ended. He didn’t ask Su Yu anything but instead made a round of the warehouse.

“There’s no coffin in the warehouse yet. Seems they haven’t arrived.”

Steward Liu went to the front desk and dismissed Su Yu. “Alright, Su Yu, I’ll take over here. You can go rest for now.”

Su Yu is an outsider after all. I can’t let her see the Juxuan Island Four Thieves to avoid introducing unnecessary complications.

Steward Liu stood at the reception. Not two minutes had passed before he saw Lu Yang and the other three carrying a coffin into the merchant guild.

“Excuse me, may I ask if we can store a coffin here?” Meng Jingzhou asked. As he was the most familiar with merchant guilds, he was in charge of handling the interaction.

Strange, I don’t know them, Steward Liu thought. They must have disguised themselves before coming over. Quite cautious, I must say.

He put on a knowing smile, pretending not to recognize the four and treating them as ordinary customers. “Well, of course. Our merchant guild provides all services within its power. Coffin storage? Yes, that’s possible.”

Meng Jingzhou was slightly surprised. I didn’t expect the service attitude at the East Sea branch to be this good. I thought they’d politely refuse us.

He had already been prepared to find an inn and place the coffin there. While inns might not agree either, he could try offering more spirit stones.

If all else failed, they would just have to keep carrying the coffin. He didn’t care about public opinion; it was mainly Man Gu who was shy and had thin skin.

“Dear guests, how many days would you like to store it?”

“Our plan is three days, but it’s not definite. It might be extended depending on the situation. After all, we don’t know how things will go with the Dragon Tribe. How much in spirit stones?” Meng Jingzhou said offhandedly, still unsure how long obtaining the Dragon blood would take.

I see, Steward Liu thought. So even you all don’t know when the heat will die down.

Hearing Meng Jingzhou ask about the price startled Steward Liu. Any spirit stones accepted must be recorded in the accounts. Wait, the Juxuan Island Four Thieves aren’t ignorant of the rules. Could they be hinting through this method that we’re all in this together and that I shouldn’t dream of secretly moving the supreme treasure away?

“Three hundred spirit stones.”

Meng Jingzhou casually took out three mid-grade spirit stones.

“Hey, handle the coffin gently. What’s inside isn’t a dead person,” Lu Yang reminded Steward Liu as he moved the coffin.

Steward Liu wasn’t surprised. He gave a faint smile and moved it with extra care. As if I don’t know the coffin contains the Dragon Tribe’s supreme treasure. That thing is worth more than my life.

After seeing Lu Yang and the others off, someone called for Steward Liu again.

“Old Liu, the Vice Guildmaster says all stewards and above are to meet to discuss and study the spirit of the earlier meeting.”

“Coming! Su Yu, watch the reception.”

“Alright, Steward Liu.”

~~~

A few more minutes passed. The Juxuan Island Four Thieves stealthily entered the merchant guild, carrying a coffin.

“Strange, where’s Old Liu? Didn’t he promise to wait for us here?” The big brother was puzzled. Why is there only a young girl at the reception?

“May I ask what brings you here, dear guests?” Su Yu performed a curtsy.

Could she be someone arranged by Old Liu? The big brother asked skeptically, “We’ve come to store a coffin. Is that possible?”

Su Yu was about to refuse, but then she remembered Steward Liu’s reminder about service attitude and fulfilling customer requests as much as possible. She put on a sweet and natural smile. “Of course, that is possible.”

The big brother thought, So Old Liu did send her here. Otherwise, why would the merchant guild agree so readily?

He must have gotten this young girl to interact with us because he was worried about the Dragon Tribe tracing it to him. Quite cautious, I must say.

“Dear guests, how many days would you like to store it?”

“Store it for three days first; we might extend it later depending on the situation.” The big brother estimated the Dragon Tribe could only search for three or four days. If they keep failing to locate the supreme treasure, they’ll certainly suspect it has already been taken out. The sea market won’t be too dangerous then.

Of course, if the Dragon Tribe is overly suspicious, we can just store it here for a few more days. No big deal; I can wait.

“Alright, that will be three hundred spirit stones in total.” Su Yu smiled politely. I’ll accept three hundred spirit stones upfront; if it exceeds three days, it’ll be an extra hundred per day. This is the rule.

“You’re even charging money?” The big brother was bewildered. How did he instruct her? Charging money for such a secretive operation?

Then he understood. Steward Liu is warning us through this little girl’s words that the agreed-upon benefits must be given in full, not a single bit less.

The big brother whipped out three hundred spirit stones and passed them to the young girl. “We won’t shortchange you.

“By the way, remember to handle it gently. Don’t make too much noise. After all, it’s something that can’t see the light of day.” The big brother reminded Su Yu to be careful. He couldn’t help but feel the girl’s movements were too rough and would easily attract attention.

“Alright.” Su Yu appeared delicate, but she was quite strong. She carried the coffin in the warehouse, handling it carefully. Remembering the Juxuan Island Four Thieves’ words, she took out a black cloth and covered the coffin. “Since it can’t see the light of day, I’ll cover it up.”

After the Juxuan Island Four Thieves walked out of the merchant guild, an underling whispered, “Big Brother, isn’t the effect of these pills too strong? We’re only at the Divine Transfiguration Stage now.” He assumed they would only drop a major realm.

How could the big brother have known that the pills sold on the black market were defective ones discarded by the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Pill Cauldron Peak? Their effects were either not good or too good.

“It’s all within the plan. This way, the Dragon Tribe definitely won’t suspect us.”

~~~

Two hours later, Steward Liu’s meeting concluded, but he didn’t return to the front desk.

Since the coffin is already stored here, today’s task is complete.

“Next will be waiting for the heat to die down. I hope everything goes smoothly,” Steward Liu mumbled to himself.

Chapter 776: Ancestral Dragon Grass

“This should be the place.”

Lu Yang and the other three arrived at a small teahouse. The environment was boisterous, gathering people from all walks of life.

“Waiter, give us a pot of High-Mountain Jasmine Tea.”

“Gotcha.”

According to Xiao Xinghai, this teahouse was a secret location for issuing missions. Ordering a pot of High-Mountain Jasmine Tea, which didn’t actually exist, signified you weren’t a patron but a cultivator here for a mission.

It wasn’t all the time that a Dragon Tribe member waited here for cultivators keen on taking up missions. Sometimes, one had to wait half a day for a Dragon Tribe member to come. With terrible luck, it was possible to wait three days without a Dragon Tribe member showing up.

Lu Yang and the others had decent luck. After drinking two pots of tea, a Dragon Tribe member transmitted an auditory message to them. “Four young friends, come to the room at the far end of the west wing for a discussion.”

The group had to admit that whatever tea the waiter served genuinely tasted decent. After finishing their tea, they arrived at the west wing room to find it empty, save for a Dragon Tribe member wrapped tightly, unwilling to let Lu Yang and the others know his identity. Only two dragon horns that were left uncovered proved he was a dragon. It was a belief of the Dragon Tribe that their horns were a source of pride and must not be concealed.

“You are here to obtain Dragon blood?”

“Yes. Our friend is severely injured and needs Dragon blood to heal.” freewebnovel.com

The black-robed dragon snorted coldly, treating Lu Yang’s words as a sob story. “We are strangers coming together by chance, each taking what we need. No need to explain too much; what you need the blood for is none of my concern.

“I need you to help me find the Ancestral Dragon Grass.”

“Ancestral Dragon Grass? The legendary grass beloved by the Dragon Tribe’s Ancient Ancestor and now on the brink of extinction?” Li Haoran recalled the grass’s origins from Qin Haoran’s memories.

The black-robed dragon glanced at Li Haoran with slight surprise. I didn’t expect young people nowadays to know about the Ancestral Dragon Grass; even among the older generation, few know of it.

“My subordinate disappeared while transporting the Ancestral Dragon Grass, and I have no idea what happened. Perhaps he was harmed by my arch-enemy, or perhaps an accident occurred. Nevertheless, I can faintly sense that the Ancestral Dragon Grass is right in this sea market.

“My identity is special; every move I make may draw the attention of potential enemies. It’s inconvenient for me to search for the Ancestral Dragon Grass personally.

The black-robed dragon flicked out a drop of blood. “This is a drop of my Dragon essence blood. It will react if it gets close to the Ancestral Dragon Grass. Carry this drop of blood with you to search for the grass. If you can find it, Dragon blood won’t be a problem.”

Lu Yang took out a porcelain bottle, placed the Dragon blood inside, and tied the vial to his waist. He could sense terrifying energy from this drop of Dragon blood. This is definitely not from the Divine Transfiguration Stage; even the Void Refinement Stage won’t have such stable fluctuations.

Could this person be at the Fusion Stage?

As far as Lu Yang knew, Fusion Stage dragons were elders of the Dragon Tribe. It seems the Dragon Tribe isn’t a monolithic entity; the elders keep one another in check. Since this is Dragon blood from the Fusion Stage, the benefits would be substantial for Fellow Daoist Xinghai if he could be nourished by it.

The black-robed dragon waved his hand. “This matter is of great importance. You must act in secret. Do not let others, especially the Dragon Tribe, detect your actions!

“And this box here has the effect of blocking spiritual consciousness. If you find the Ancestral Dragon Grass, place it inside this box. That way, others won’t discover what you are carrying.” The black-robed dragon tossed a small wooden box to Lu Yang.

“Alright, go now. Report your progress to me in three days.”

Lu Yang and the others left the teahouse.

Li Haoran pondered. I’ve heard the Old Dragon Emperor reveres the Dragon Tribe’s Ancient Ancestor, and by extension, likes the Ancestral Dragon Grass. Could this black-robed dragon be planning on presenting it as a birthday gift to the Old Dragon Emperor at the upcoming banquet?

As the ruler of the Dragon Palace, the Old Dragon Emperor reigns over the East Sea and possesses innumerable rare treasures. One has to adopt an unconventional approach and be innovative to please him with a birthday gift—something like the Ancestral Dragon Grass.

This explains the emphasis on not letting the Dragon Tribe detect our actions. Which dragon wouldn’t want to present the Ancestral Dragon Grass as a birthday gift to gain the Old Dragon Emperor’s favor?

Li Haoran’s conjecture was correct—it was precisely what the black-robed dragon was thinking. The latter also considered that if there was no progress in three days and the Ancestral Dragon Grass couldn’t be located, he would have to find something else as a birthday gift.

Lu Yang hadn’t heard of any Ancestral Dragon Grass. He asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, but she also said she hadn’t heard of it.

“Its name has probably been changed. It wasn’t called that in our time. As for Little Ling liking grass, when did she like grass... Oh, I remember. There was a period when she pretended to be a refined lady of a noble family and grew flowers and grass, trying to attract the Qilin Immortal’s attention. At that time, the Qilin Immortal often suspected that someone had taken over Little Ling’s body.

“Later, Little Ling saw that this tactic wasn’t working, so she gave up gardening and gifted all those things to this immortal. I saw she had cultivated them well; the plants were all sturdy. I liked them immensely, so I cooked them all into dishes and laid out a grand feast called the ‘Hundred Herb (Grass) Banquet,’ inviting the other four immortals, Little Ling, and Lianyi.

“Subsequently, someone spread a rumor that the Nine-Layers Immortal sampled a hundred herbs and fainted on the way home.

“What nonsense. This immortal clearly saw that the Nine-Layers Immortal was quite happy during the meal, hopping and jumping.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, I’m afraid the Nine-Layers Immortal was hallucinating from all that he ate.

The second layer of the secret domain where Senior Lianyi slumbered contained many rare and exotic plants from ancient times. The Ancestral Dragon Grass should be among them.

However, the Dragon Palace was too far from the Demon Region. By the time they made a round trip, Xiao Xinghai’s injuries would have likely healed on their own.

~~

At an inn.

Although it was called an inn, what it provided weren’t rooms but pocket dimensions for cultivation.

The Juxuan Island Four Thieves rented one such pocket dimension.

“Let’s hide here for a few days. Unless absolutely necessary, don’t leave the pocket dimension for these few days,” the big brother instructed.

The big brother then remembered something. “By the way, Old Four, a Dragon Tribe member stumbled upon us stealing the supreme treasure. After we disposed of the body and got rid of the evidence, we also took the box he was holding. What was inside?”

“We were in a hurry then, so I only opened the box for a brief glance. It was grass, but I don’t know what variety it is.” The fourth brother with the furtive eyes produced a wooden box. Inside lay a grass shaped like a dragon’s claw.

The big brother looked it over from all sides, unable to discern its origins. “What is this? Does anyone recognize it?”

“I don’t.”

“Dragon Claw Grass?”

“Old Three, you know it?”

“Uh, no, I don’t. I just thought it looked like a dragon claw and gave it a random name.”

“...If you don’t know, then keep your mouth shut!”

“Alright.”

“This thing is likely extremely valuable. That Dragon Tribe member was utterly annihilated, yet this box and grass remained intact.”

~~~

The elders searching for the Dragon Tribe’s supreme treasure had their subordinates act first while they convened to analyze the situation. “The Dragon Pearl cannot be placed in a storage ring. The thieves who stole it will definitely seek another way to conceal it.

“Moreover, it would require the effect of blocking spiritual consciousness to guard against our probing.”

Chapter 777: It Was Them!

“Items that block spiritual consciousness are nothing more than cloth and boxes—things extremely common in the sea market. This is the Dragon Palace’s sea market, the most prosperous sea market in the entire East Sea. Using cloth or boxes for wrapping during transactions is perfectly normal.”

Another elder shook his head. “It doesn’t matter. This already narrows the range. The cloth or box containing the Dragon Pearl won’t be too large and will be of a high grade, impossible for even a Fusion cultivator to see through.”

“Cloth or boxes of such level are rare. The Dragon tribesmen we’ve dispatched for the search are minimally at the Divine Transfiguration Stage. A box they can’t see through has a high probability of being the target.”

The theft of the Dragon Pearl was a matter of great importance. The elders mobilized all forces they could to track it down.

“Should we narrow the suspects to Fusion cultivators?”

“No. The culprit is undeniably at the Fusion Stage, but they likely have subordinates. To evade us, the culprit might have a subordinate carry the Dragon Pearl.”

“Of course, we must investigate every Fusion cultivator currently in the sea market, regardless of reputation!”

Another elder slammed the table angrily. “Last time the Dragon Pearl was stolen, it was the work of the Old Taciturn Scoundrel. Which scoundrel is it this time?!”

“Alright, that’s enough. What’s the point of saying this now? The utmost priority is to find the Dragon Pearl as soon as possible, else we’ll face the Palace Leader’s wrath.”

~~~

“Where should we go to find the Ancestral Dragon Grass?” Meng Jingzhou was conflicted. They were completely in the dark about the sea market and had no leads.

“Take it slow; just treat it as touring around the sea market.” Lu Yang was not stressed. “By the way, Junior Brother Li, have you been to the sea market before?”

“No, I haven’t.”

“Alright then.”

Lu Yang and the other three casually strolled around the sea market. They still had three days and were not in a rush.

“Hmm, the dragons have temples too?” Lu Yang passed by a temple teeming with worshippers who were both seafolk and humans coming here to offer incense.

“What temple is this?” Curious, Lu Yang entered the temple but found no statue inside. There was only a memorial tablet inscribed with the words “Great Venerable Dragon Mandate.”

Li Haoran replied, “Don’t you know, Senior Brother Lu? This is the temple of the Great Venerable Dragon Mandate. It’s famous among sea tribes.

“Legends have it that the Great Venerable Dragon Mandate was a supreme powerhouse among ancient dragons, controlling celestial phenomena. Wind, rain, thunder, and lightning shifted with his mood. There are even rumors that the Great Venerable Dragon Mandate was a true dragon stronger than the Dragon Tribe’s Ancient Ancestor.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, I have indeed heard of a Dragon Mandate. He is called the Heaven Mandate Immortal. He cultivated the Dragon Transformation Mantra and could transform into a true dragon, hence the name “Dragon Mandate.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy mentioned this when explaining the Dragon Transformation Mantra.

If I’m not wrong, the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Great Venerable Dragon Mandate should be the same person.

Considering his mind was full of the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s embarrassing dark history, and considering he still had to undergo a lightning tribulation at the Divine Transfiguration Stage, Lu Yang had a guilty conscience. He felt he should offer an incense stick to the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

Lu Yang lit an incense stick and imitated the crowd, making a proper bow.

“Every grievance has its culprit, every debt has its creditor. If you seek revenge, please go find the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Also, please help find Ao Ling and the Ancestral Dragon Grass.”

Seeing Lu Yang burn incense, Meng Jingzhou and the others assumed he was experiencing East Sea culture. They also lit incense sticks and bowed to the Great Venerable Dragon Mandate.

Unfortunately, the Great Venerable Dragon Mandate wasn’t efficacious. A day passed, and despite visiting countless places, they still hadn’t located the Ancestral Dragon Grass.

“Strange, why do I feel like someone’s following us?” Lu Yang frowned. He kept feeling spiritual consciousness scanning the wooden box in his bundle, but upon careful examination, he couldn’t sense anything.

Either I’m imagining things, or the other party has terrifying stealth skills.

“Could the Dragon Tribe have detected our actions? That shouldn’t be,” Lu Yang murmured, utterly perplexed. We haven’t found the Ancestral Dragon Grass yet; why are we already being watched?

In the shadows, two Dragon tribesmen were startled.

“Did he discover us?”

“It can’t be, right? He’s only at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage. We’re at the Apex Divine Transfiguration Stage and specialize in cultivating spiritual consciousness. How could he possibly detect us?”

“Do you think those four have any connection to the missing supreme treasure?” After two days of searching, the Dragon Tribe had secretly identified several suspects, including Lu Yang and his companions, who were deemed suspicious for carrying a wooden box.

“Hey, did you hear what he said? He said, ‘Could the Dragon Tribe have detected our actions?’ It must be them!”

“Don’t get agitated. It might be a coincidence. Let’s observe a bit more.” The steady Dragon Tribe member restrained his companion.

~~~

The second day.

“Big Brother, bad news! The Dragon Tribe has started searching the pocket dimensions!” The third brother hurriedly entered their rented pocket dimension.

They sent one person out daily to scout the situation and check on the progress of the Dragon Tribe’s search. It was the third brother’s turn today.

“Don’t panic. Give the details.”

“The Dragon Tribe has started searching the pocket dimensions one by one! Regardless of cultivation or race, no one should be spared!”

The big brother furrowed his brows. “Even those in seclusion are being searched?” He had planned to use seclusion as a pretext to evade the search.

“It’s useless. Those who entered seclusion within the last three days had the Dragon Tribe barging in. Only those who’ve been in seclusion for over three days aren’t disturbed.”

Entries and exits from pocket dimensions were recorded. Seclusion exceeding three days indicated one hadn’t left, making it impossible for them to have stolen the Dragon Pearl.

“Troublesome.”

“Big Brother, why is it troublesome? The Dragon Pearl isn’t with us. Even if they search, they won’t trace it to us.” The second brother was baffled.

The big brother shook his head. “We have no proof of identification. Normally, that’s not a big deal, but at such a critical period, the Dragon Tribe will definitely list us as suspects. How would we move the coffin then?”

“Then what should we do?”

The big brother gritted his teeth. “Leave the pocket dimension. At worst, we’ll stroll around for these few days. The Dragon Tribe can’t possibly check everyone’s identity on the streets.”

“Alright.”

~~~

The third day.

“It’s so hard to find.” Man Gu sighed. It’s already been three days.

Suddenly, Lu Yang felt the Dragon blood at his waist stir. His eyes locked onto the Juxuan Island Four Thieves passing by, and he sneered. “Found it!”

Clearly, these four aren’t subordinates of the black-robed Dragon Tribe elder. They must have killed and robbed, seizing the Ancestral Dragon Grass. But fearing the black-robed dragon, they dare not sell it.

“Follow them!” Lu Yang secretly transmitted an auditory message.

Meng Jingzhou and the others perked. We’ve finally found it.

“Big Brother, someone’s following us.” The second brother transmitted an auditory message. As the Juxuan Island Four Thieves, tailing and infiltrating were their bread and butter.

“I’ve sensed it too. But don’t worry, they’re only at the Nascent Soul Stage,” the big brother said unhurriedly. “They’re human, so they’re unrelated to the matter of the Dragon Pearl. Let’s lure them to a deserted place and see what they want.”

The Juxuan Island Four Thieves weren’t afraid of Lu Yang’s group. Lu Yang and the others could tell the big brother had discovered them and was intentionally leading them to a deserted place. They weren’t afraid either.

The eight met at a remote, secluded spot at the edge of the sea market.

“I believe I don’t know you four. What do you want?” The big brother stared coldly at Lu Yang and the others.

The closer Lu Yang got, the more he felt the Dragon blood’s restlessness. The Ancestral Dragon Grass must be on them.

“You’ve taken something you shouldn’t have. Are you really not afraid of offending a Dragon Tribe elder?”

Hearing Lu Yang’s words, the big brother relaxed by half. This person said “Dragon Tribe elder” and not “Dragon Tribe,” which implies it’s indeed not related to the Dragon Pearl.

“What thing? I’m not clear.” The big brother shook his head. If I really have anything related to a Dragon Tribe elder, it should be that unidentified grass. But why should I give that thing to four Nascent Soul cultivators? Simply eliminating them would settle everything.

“Not clear? Killing Dragon tribesmen and murdering for wealth, yet you tell me you aren’t clear what thing it is? Fellow Daoist, do you think I’m easily fooled? If that’s the case, should I call the Dragon Tribe elder backing me?”

The big brother’s gaze sharpened. Involving a Dragon Tribe elder might expose the matter of the Dragon Pearl.

I can’t let you all live!

The Juxuan Island Four Thieves acted simultaneously, aiming to eliminate Lu Yang’s group instantly.

Lu Yang drew his sword, and sword qi erupted, carving a deep trench in the ground. His gaze turned deadly. “Do you truly wish to turn this to blows? That is something the Old Dragon Emperor likes. I advise you to hand it over, Fellow Daoist. Then we can go our separate ways peacefully.”

For a moment, both sides reached an impasse.

From the black-robed Dragon Tribe elder’s tone, Lu Yang discerned that the latter didn’t want the matter blown up. If the four of them fought the other four, it would likely be brought to everyone’s attention.

The big brother’s heart jolted with alarm. That sword qi just now was extremely dangerous. The leader is not easy to deal with; he’s a tough nut to crack. I’m afraid a decisive outcome can’t be achieved quickly. There’s no need to fight here over an unidentified grass.

We shouldn’t have taken that grass away in the first place.

Although it was humiliating, he knew how to give and take. He produced the wooden box and tossed it to Lu Yang. “This?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was also curious what this “Ancestral Dragon Grass” was. She scanned it with her immortal consciousness, and realization dawned upon her. “I thought it was something special. When Little Ling started gardening, her skill wasn’t up to par, and she grew a bunch of weeds. Lianyi often mocked her for it. Little Ling was stubborn and insisted she liked growing weeds.

“This Ancestral Dragon Grass is just the weeds from Little Ling’s backyard!”

Lu Yang, “...”

I heard nothing. Senior Ao Ling, please don’t come after me.

With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s confirmation, Lu Yang was sure the box contained the Ancestral Dragon Grass. He directly placed the box inside the box provided by the black-robed Dragon Tribe elder. Double boxes ensured the outside world couldn’t see inside, making it absolutely secure.

In the shadows, the two Dragon tribesmen transmitted auditory messages to each other, somewhat excited.

“Did you hear that? One side tried to pull a double-cross, and the other side’s people came knocking.”

“They obtained the thing by killing a Dragon tribesman, and it’s even something the Old Dragon Emperor likes—it must be the Dragon Pearl! It was them!”

“To think there’s even an elder involved in this!”

Chapter 778: Juxuan Island Four Thieves: Why Is There a Person Inside the Coffin?

The two Dragon Tribe scouts felt their scalps tingle. They had assumed it was a crime committed by outsiders, but it turned out there was a traitor within their ranks, who was even an elder.

To have dared to commit such an outrageous act, this elder’s strength can’t be underestimated.

“What do we do? Should we capture them all now?”

The steady Dragon tribesman looked at his companion in astonishment. “Are you alright? There are eight of them—four Divine Transfiguration cultivators and four Nascent Soul cultivators. Judging by their combat power, those four Nascent Soul cultivators can likely match Divine Transfiguration cultivators. Do you honestly believe we can capture them with just the two of us?”

“Then what do we do?”

“Here’s what. You go notify the elders; I’ll stay here to observe. Once those four Nascent Soul cultivators get the Dragon Pearl, they’ll definitely hand it to the elder behind the theft. We’ll catch them red-handed. That way, we’ll score a meritorious achievement!”

“You’re so clever!” Knowing time was tight, the companion immediately set off to inform the elders.

Lu Yang’s group completed the exchange with the Juxuan Island Four Thieves, successfully obtaining the Ancestral Dragon Grass.

The big brother secretly transmitted an auditory message. “Change of plan. Move quickly!”

The three underlings were baffled. “Did our theft of the Dragon Pearl get exposed?”

The big brother looked at his three underlings in exasperation. If it weren’t for me, you three would have been caught long ago.

“Didn’t you hear those four Nascent Soul cultivators? This grass belongs to a Dragon Tribe elder, and we stole it. Do you think he’d leave us a way out? Once those four Nascent Soul cultivators report this to that Dragon Tribe elder, all four of us will be finished!”

If we’re still at the Fusion Stage, there might be room to maneuver. But four Divine Transfiguration cultivators before a Dragon Tribe elder? I’m afraid we won’t withstand even one smack of his palm!

“Then what do we do?”

The big brother gritted his teeth and made a decision. “We can’t afford to care so much now. Quickly go to the merchant guild and move the Dragon Pearl away.”

On the other hand, Lu Yang’s group decided to go find the black-robed Dragon Tribe elder.

Seeing the two groups split, the steady Dragon tribesman in the shadows didn’t hesitate to follow Lu Yang’s group. As for the Juxuan Island Four Thieves, once the Dragon Tribe elders arrived, even if the four had fled the sea market, the Dragon Tribe could still capture them. This was the confidence of the Dragon Tribe, the East Sea’s overlord!

~~~

The Juxuan Island Four Thieves hurried back to the merchant guild. It was the third day, and Steward Liu was already waiting at the front desk.

The big brother urgently transmitted an auditory message. “Old Liu, quickly retrieve the coffin!”

You changed appearances again?

Three days ago, you four didn’t look like this when storing the coffin. Quite cautious, I must say.

“Alright.”

Steward Liu entered the warehouse. He passed by the coffin Su Yu had covered with a black cloth and retrieved the coffin he had personally stored three days ago.

“Here, be careful.” Steward Liu carried the coffin out.

“Until we meet again.” The Juxuan Island Four Thieves took the coffin and hastily left.

On the way, they even put on mourning expressions, acting as if a dear brother of theirs had died. As great thieves, one needed not only high cultivation and a sharp mind but also good acting skills. People around them believed the coffin contained a dead person. Carrying the coffin, the Juxuan Island Four Thieves cried with snot and tears, successfully deceiving the guards and leaving the sea market.

After swimming about two li from the sea market, the four took out Divine Travel Talismans and affixed them to their legs, speeding forward and distancing themselves from this place of trouble as fast as possible. They changed routes multiple times, sometimes flying and sometimes swimming, before finally arriving at the intended island.

“Whew, we’re safe now.”

The entire journey had been nerve-wracking. They feared that the Dragon Tribe would notice something, which would render all their efforts futile.

“Success! Quickly take out the Dragon Pearl!” The second brother was excited. I can’t believe we actually succeeded! Although there were accidents along the way, Big Brother’s wise decisions turned danger into safety.

The big brother was also excited and pushed open the lid of the coffin. Making eye contact with Xiao Xinghai lying inside, he froze.

He silently closed the lid, then reopened it. Xiao Xinghai was still lying inside.

Xiao Xinghai yawned. “We’ve been out for three days, right? Have you gotten the Dragon blood?

“Did you all change appearances again? Were you afraid of being recognized?” Xiao Xinghai had heard that the Dragon Tribe’s relationship with the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Sect Leader and First Elder was poor. Being cautious can’t go wrong.

The Juxuan Island Four Thieves stared at Xiao Xinghai with shock and disbelief. They were great cultivators over a thousand years old and focused on news of Fusion cultivators. They weren’t familiar with Xiao Xinghai, a young kunpeng who had lived only twenty years and debuted just three years ago.

“Big Brother, what’s going on? Did the Dragon Pearl gain sentience and become a demon spirit?” The fourth brother transmitted an auditory message.

The big brother secretly nodded. “Highly possible. I’ve heard some exquisitely refined half-immortal or immortal artifacts develop intelligence and can take human form.

“And didn’t you hear him? He said ‘been out for three days,’ which indicates he was stolen from the Dragon Palace three days ago. It seems he’s quite happy to be out of the Dragon Palace.

“Not sure. Maybe the Dragon Pearl needs to absorb Dragon blood to unleash its true power?” the second brother speculated.

In any case, they were Fusion experts and had some Dragon blood on hand, just not very fresh.

“Did you want this?” The big brother took out a small jar of Dragon blood from his storage ring, his tone subconsciously respectful.

“Not very fresh, huh?” Xiao Xinghai felt the Dragon Tribe wasn’t honorable, bullying Lu Yang and his companions and even giving them old blood after the mission was completed.

“Please make do with it.” The big brother smiled apologetically.

“Pour it in then.” Xiao Xinghai lay flat in the coffin; he was still severely injured. He sighed. “If not for the rule limitation, I wouldn’t need to rely on absorbing Dragon blood to recover.”

The Four Thieves’ hearts shook. So it’s indeed a sentient Dragon Pearl that has turned into a demon spirit. After taking on human form, its power greatly diminished, needing to absorb Dragon blood to recover.

As for the rule he mentioned, it was likely caused by Transcendent Tribulation cultivators or half-immortals fighting.

The big brother respectfully poured the Dragon blood into the coffin. Xiao Xinghai didn’t care whether his clothes got stained and lay comfortably, absorbing the blood and cultivating the Dragon Transformation Mantra.

Hearing dragon roars echo from within Xiao Xinghai, the Four Thieves grew even more deferential.

The big brother smiled obsequiously by the side and chose his words carefully, afraid of offending this Dragon Pearl demon spirit. “Brother Pearl, what are your plans next?”

Xiao Xinghai was taken aback. “Who’s Brother Pearl? Is that a nickname you gave me?”

“Isn’t your true form the Dragon Pearl? If you don’t like this form of address, we juniors can change it.”

Xiao Xinghai grew even more perplexed. “Have you lost your memories? I’m Xiao Xinghai.”

Xiao Xinghai and the Juxuan Island Four Thieves stared at each other, their expressions utterly befuddled.

Then the Juxuan Island Four Thieves reacted. They flew into a rage, their furious bellows reverberating through the whole island.

“Where’s the Dragon Pearl?!”

Chapter 779: Caught Red-Handed With the Goods

The Juxuan Island Four Thieves fixed their predatory gazes on Xiao Xinghai, killing intent rising.

“Who exactly are you?! Where’s the Dragon Pearl?!”

Xiao Xinghai was even more clueless. What Dragon Pearl? Who are you four? Where am I?

The Juxuan Island Four Thieves grew angrier. They had painstakingly prepared for a hundred years just to steal the Dragon Pearl, only to have it swapped out after the deed.

It must be that Liu fellow’s doing!

Although their cultivation realms had dropped, they were still at the Divine Transfiguration Stage, not to mention that Xiao Xinghai was severely injured and struggled to even stand.

Xiao Xinghai didn’t understand what was happening and had a look of innocence as he let the four attack.

The moment the attacks landed on Xiao Xinghai, one of his hairs suddenly erupted with a gloomy light.

As a peerless prodigy of the Kunpeng Tribe, his cultivation talent could be considered number one in the tribe’s history. How could he not have life-saving items on hand? This hair was one of the Black Feather Venerable Lord’s feathers, which would manifest when Xiao Xinghai was in danger.

“Ah—!”

The Juxuan Island Four Thieves were swept by the black light and stopped breathing.

~~~

Meanwhile, after the Dragon Tribe received the news, they split into two groups to track Lu Yang’s group of four and the Juxuan Island Four Thieves.

The Dragon Tribe elder led a large contingent and flew out of the sea market with great fanfare, inquiring with the nearby schools of fish where the four had gone.

This was his talent—he was born able to communicate with ordinary fish lacking spirit intelligence.

After obtaining information from the schools of fish, they transformed into their true forms. Dozens of true dragons flew over the sea surface, their presence awe-inspiring.

“It’s this island!”

By the time they arrived, they saw Xiao Xinghai lying in the coffin, soaked in blood. He was gasping and extremely frail, unable to stand. The Juxuan Island Four Thieves lay on the ground, blood pooling around them.

The dragons’ hearts shook at this sight. This person fought bloody battles and slew four thieves. He is a hero of the Dragon Tribe!

The dragons descended. Some verified the identities of the four Divine Transfiguration cultivators, while more surrounded Xiao Xinghai, praising his heroic feat.

I was just lying in the coffin. Someone opened it and wanted to kill me, the Old Ancestor’s feather retaliated, and now I’m a hero of the Dragon Tribe?

Where did Lu Yang and the others go?

The black-robed Dragon Tribe elder had long been waiting in the room.

Lu Yang held the wooden box containing the Ancestral Dragon Grass in one hand and carried the coffin on his shoulder.

The black-robed Dragon Tribe elder jolted. He hadn’t expected Lu Yang’s claim about an injured friend needing Dragon blood to be true.

Three days have passed. They helped me find the Ancestral Dragon Grass, but their friend has already died.

People often fantasized that bathing in Dragon blood could resurrect the dead or grant longevity. In reality, how could the Dragon blood possess such heaven-defying effects?

Lu Yang’s group felt the name Ao Ran sounded familiar.

Man Gu had the least things occupying his mind and was the first to remember. Before they set off for the East Sea, Grandpa Ba mentioned he had a friend in the East Sea named Ao Ran, who often liked to seal his cultivation and act out scenes of breaking through on the spot.

“Senior Ao Ran, the four of us are from the Dao-Seeking Sect. I’m Man Gu, and these three are Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Li Haoran!”

“And you still claimed you don’t know them!” Upon hearing Lu Yang’s name, Ao Ye and the other two seemed to recall something. “Lu Yang is that Old Taciturn Scoundrel’s disciple!”

To think that master and disciple took turns stealing the Dragon Pearl! They truly have no regard for our Dragon Palace!

“You three, stop your unreasonable accusations!” Ao Ran shielded Lu Yang’s group, suspecting Ao Ye’s trio was seizing the opportunity to make things difficult for them.

“Unreasonable accusations? Then what’s in that wooden box?!”

As someone who stood straight, Ao Ran wasn’t worried his shadow would be crooked. He opened the box, revealing the dragon-claw-shaped grass. “Ancestral Dragon Grass, a congratulatory gift for the Palace Leader’s grand birthday. What’s the problem?!”

Ao Ye’s trio mumbled inwardly. This isn’t right. Isn’t the Dragon Pearl supposed to be in the wooden box?

Suddenly, they turned their gazes to the most conspicuous object in the room—the coffin.

“What’s inside that coffin?”

Ao Ran angrily opened the coffin. “It’s a person inside the coffin, of course!”

Then everyone saw that secured within the coffin was a crystal-clear, smooth and round pearl that was the size of a palm.

It was precisely the Dragon Pearl.

Absolute silence fell over everyone.

Ao Ran, “...”

“Caught red-handed with the stolen goods—how else do you plan to defend yourself?

“You even wanted to slit your wrist earlier. Were you planning to drip blood and claim ownership?”

First Elder’s coffins were hidden all over the East Sea; finding one wasn’t strange.

Because the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been laughing all this time.

She must have witnessed everything but kept quiet!

Inside his mental space, the mermaid Everlasting Immortal Fairy split her sides laughing until she lacked the strength to swim in the sea. She rolled back and forth on her waterbed, her laughter reverberating through the mental space, completely ignoring Lu Yang’s dark expression.

Lu Yang only regretted that he wasn’t an immortal, unable to teach the Everlasting Immortal Fairy a lesson for enjoying the spectacle without caring about the problem snowballing.

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, have you seen this Dragon Pearl?” Lu Yang had heard Li Haoran mention that it was an ancient object earlier. Since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy also hailed from ancient times, he reckoned she might recognize it.

“What Dragon Pearl? Isn’t this just the bead the Qilin Immortal and the Heaven Mandate Immortal often flicked back and forth while squatting on the ground? Shouldn’t this come in a set?”

“It’s not wrong to say it’s auspicious. Every time I invited them for meals, they’d play a round before eating and keep it on the table during the meal.

“By the way, this thing also has detoxifying functions. I’m just not sure what it’s used for.”

It immediately clicked for Lu Yang. This thing is probably a detoxifying magical treasure. Every mealtime, the Qilin Immortal and the Heaven Mandate Immortal used playing with marbles as a pretext to openly take out the Dragon Pearl.

Though from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s description, the Dragon Pear’s detoxifying effects were minimal.

“But this marble is so big. Wasn’t it cumbersome for the two immortals to play with?” Lu Yang gestured; the pearl was the size of a palm. How did they play?

“Oh, this isn’t its original form. The outer layer is a protective shell. This immortal will show you the pearl’s true appearance.”

Lu Yang wanted to stop her, but then heard a string of obscure ancient words. The Dragon Pearl lying quietly in the coffin developed countless fine cracks.

Crack, crack...

Under everyone’s eyes, the Dragon Pearl split open, revealing the marble’s original appearance—a grayish bead the size of a pill.

“See, it looks like this. It’s a bead refined from an entire star and extremely sturdy.”

The Dragon tribesmen were horrified. Isn’t this Dragon Pearl indestructible? How did it crack just like that?

Lu Yang guiltily lowered his head.

Suddenly, the identity jade tablet at Lu Yang’s waist grew hot, resonating with the grayish bead.

The grayish bead floated out of the coffin. Before Lu Yang could react, he felt a tremendous suction force firmly attaching him to the bead.

Lu Yang realized that the Dragon-Pattern Bracelet within his identity jade tablet and this bead had produced some unknown resonance!

“What the...”

Under everyone’s stunned gazes, the bead carried Lu Yang toward the sky with a whoosh, vanishing without a trace. Its speed was so fast it left everyone in the dust; no one present could catch up.

Ao Li’s huge dragon eyes blinked twice. “Did Lu Yang snatch the Dragon Pearl... or did the Dragon Pearl snatch Lu Yang?”

Ao Li also didn’t know how to handle this situation and hesitantly suggested, “Should we contact the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

Ao Ran looked up at the sky, gazing in the direction Lu Yang and the bead had flown, sighing quietly in his heart.

Old Ba, I really can’t do anything to help.

Chapter 781: Ao Ling

Dao-Seeking Sect, Heaven’s Gate Peak, Discussion Hall.

Yun Zhi convened a routine meeting to discuss recent matters requiring attention. The eight elders attended, while the Vast Sea Daoist Lord observed from the side.

The bead was originally forged from a star. Adding an internal space upon that foundation would have been simple.

In particular, not using the Dragon-Pattern Bracelet to open the space will teleport it randomly, rendering anyone unable to find it, as if it’s guarding against someone.

Is this fairy immortal the Qilin Immortal’s other wife, the Dragon Tribe’s Ancient Ancestor, Ao Ling?

In an instant, an invisible ripple spread from her fingertip, enveloping Ao Ling. The soul that had been shattered into millions of pieces gathered and connected, restoring Ao Ling’s original form.

Life and death, destruction and rebirth—the Dao of nature was undeniably revealed at this moment. The principles it encompassed were far beyond Lu Yang’s current comprehension.

Chapter 782: The Reason the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Couldn’t Be Resurrected

“My husband also said that if anyone could wake me up from the Play-Dead Technique, it could only be you, Jiejie.

“Where’s my husband? He said he would bring you over to wake me. Where is he?” Ao Ling looked around, searching for the Qilin Immortal, only to find herself lying in a small pavilion surrounded by a vast, boundless lake.

“Strange, where is this? I clearly remember falling asleep in my cave abode.” Her eyes flickered with confusion. This is different from what Hubby had described. “Jiejie, what is going on?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also didn’t know what was going on.

Lu Yang, who had remained quiet, suddenly asked, “Senior Ao Ling, could you recount what happened before you slumbered?”

“This is...” Ao Ling only then noticed a young Nascent Soul cultivator beside the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Lu Yang, the Second-in-Command of our Everlasting Lineage,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy introduced in a tone that demonstrated her high regard for him. “It was he who resurrected me.”

“Ah?” Ao Ling grew even more bewildered. This was also beyond her expectations. freewebnovel.com

She lowered her head pensively, organizing her memories. “My experiences before slumbering—let me think where I should start. Right, from the day the immortal battle began.

“At that time, Lianyi was cultivating, and Hubby was guarding over her cultivation. I was reading when suddenly, my mind went black, and a piercing pain drilled into my chest. It felt like I had lost something forever.

“Then I heard my husband roar angrily, manifest his Qilin true form, and stride across the skies. Wherever he passed, innumerable stars shattered into dust.

“Heaven Mandate and the other two from the neighboring immortal territories had similar reactions. I don’t know what the four immortals sensed, but they all tacitly converged toward the North Star region.

“The four of them engaged in fierce combat with an unknown enemy. I had never seen them so enraged; it was a life-and-death situation. That battle lasted seven full days. During that period, I went to find Lianyi and asked what happened. Like me, she knew nothing.

“Seven days later, Hubby returned severely injured. He said the enemy was mysterious and intractable. To be on the safe side, he wanted both Lianyi and me to use the Play-Dead Technique.

“Lianyi used the Play-Dead Technique, while I insisted on staying awake, demanding my husband to explain. Due to my strong persistence, he explained the reason.

“Only then did I learn that all the previous anomalies were related to your perishing, Everlasting-jiejie.

“The one who killed you also erased your existence. Hubby and the other three were furious about your demise and sought to eliminate the culprit. Unfortunately, they didn’t succeed and had to settle for remolding stars to form the six-sided continent, imprisoning the culprit there.

“We were unable to eradicate the culprit in a short time; in fact, we didn’t even know where the culprit was. After Hubby and the others discussed, they believed the utmost priority was to find a way to resurrect you.

“They said the simplest method to resurrect you was to utter your name. But even they had forgotten your name. They created millions of clones and simultaneously uttered different names, yet they still failed.

“Logically, with so many names spoken simultaneously, at least one should be correct. It’s a matter of probability. Thus, the four of them suspected that one of the clones did utter the correct name, but the culprit had secretly intervened and employed some undetectable names to cause that clone to utter the wrong name.

“Nevertheless, this was mere speculation and couldn’t be verified. After all, once your name was uttered, Hubby and the other three would forget what they had said.”

Lu Yang interjected solemnly. “There’s another possibility.”

“What is it?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Ao Ling both looked at Lu Yang.

“The mastermind only blocked the ancient language version of ‘Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou’ but not the current language.

“Immortal Fairy, I remember you once said that regardless of language system, as long as your honorific title and immortal name are called out, you can be resurrected. But only you knew this; you never told anyone.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recalled this. Shortly after my resurrection, Lu Yang studied the ancient language to learn ‘Clairvoyance.’ He asked me if I could be resurrected with any language system, and this was how I answered him.

“Current language?” Ao Ling didn’t understand what Lu Yang meant. Why does it feel like many things happened after I slumbered?

Exactly how long have I been asleep?

Since awakening, Ao Ling had been speaking the ancient language. Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were fluent, so there were no communication barriers. She wasn’t aware that people in the outside world no longer spoke the ancient language.

“Correct. According to existing evidence, after the Ember Legacy Dynasty fell, the ancient language vanished. The outside world now uses a different language system.”

Lu Yang analyzed seriously, “This way, the problem can be explained. Using the ancient language cannot resurrect you, Immortal Fairy. Be it the four immortals or the mastermind, none of them knew this point, so none of them considered this issue.”

After figuring this out, Lu Yang felt a lingering fear, like he had survived a catastrophe. Fortunately, no one knew this. Otherwise, after the language system changed, if the mastermind continued the blocking, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy might never get to be resurrected.

Come to think of it, I resurrected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy just by randomly speaking. Isn’t my luck too good? Could it be that all the luck I accumulated from saving the world in a past life was used here?

Pah, how does resurrecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy count as good luck?

“Wait, wait. Are you saying the Ember Legacy Dynasty established by Hubby and the other three has been destroyed?”

Ao Ling was astonished. The Ember Legacy Dynasty, established by four immortals, actually disappeared?

“Senior Ao Ling, you know of the Ember Legacy Dynasty?”

Ao Ling nodded. “Of course. I witnessed the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s founding with my own eyes.”

Chapter 783: Yet Another Junior Sister

“Upon realizing they couldn’t resurrect you by calling your name, Hubby and the others sought other methods. After some discussion, they consulted Qing He and attempted to use faith power to resurrect you, Jiejie. Thus, they founded the Ember Legacy Dynasty.”

“Faith power is that useful?” Lu Yang was surprised. He truly didn’t know much about this.

However, considering the Great Qian Dynasty practiced “divine faith,” which could form the basis of a dynasty, faith power must have merits.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. She only accepted worship as an object of faith for fun and hadn’t paid much attention to this aspect.

Ao Ling continued recalling. “On the foundation of the Ember Legacy Dynasty, Hubby and the others established two major faith systems: ‘Heavenly Court’ and ‘Underworld.’

Lu Yang, “...”

Did I just hallucinate? Why did I hear a very familiar term?

“The ‘Heavenly Court’ system was to manage the mortal realm.

“The ‘Underworld’ system was to govern life and death.

Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stared at each other.

Lu Yang saw excitement in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw her excited self reflected in Lu Yang’s eyes.

“Second-in-Command, you truly have clairvoyance to foresee the future—oh no, foresee the past!”

Lu Yang didn’t really want to speak.

The Everlasting Dao Fruit is imperishable, and this method could call it back. If it was unsuccessful, they could also use the Underworld system’s governance over life and death to resurrect you.

“Of course, all this was in theory. No one had practiced it and knew the outcome. But judging from the four’s attitude, the success rate seemed quite high.”

Lu Yang suspected the reason the four immortals were so confident was that they knew the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would be resurrected in the future.

“Meanwhile, Hubby and the others were also trying to analyze the culprit’s identity and abilities. The Epoch Immortal attempted to observe the past, seeking the murder process. Someone suspected a Karma Dao Fruit, someone suspected a Law Follows Words Dao Fruit, and someone suspected a Substitution Dao Fruit... There were all kinds of conjectures. “The only thing they could be certain of was that the culprit was formidable; their strength surpassed that of my husband and the other three.

“The Insight Dao Fruit allows complete vision and insightful comprehension; one can sit and see in all ten directions, perceiving heaven above and earth below with no obstructions—everything is within sight.”

“Sitting and seeing in all ten directions—that’s pretty impressive. It’s much more useful than the Epoch Dao Fruit that observes the future. I never expected a place like the Shi Huang Clan could produce such a genius,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy complimented.

Sitting and seeing in all ten directions means being able to see the past, present, and future. Although the Epoch Immortal could observe the future, he couldn’t do so accurately, only perceiving one possible future.

Ao Ling shook her head. “Jiejie, you think too highly of him. He barely achieved immortality, and his strength was right at the bottom.”

Lu Yang’s eye twitched. Only a half-immortal like Ao Ling, who can sense Dao Fruit suppression, is qualified to say such a thing. And there’s also Senior Lianyi, Big Senior Sister, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the Heaven Mandate Immortal, the Nine-Layers Immortal, the Epoch Immortal, the Qilin Immortal... Counting all of them, there are actually quite a few people who are qualified to say such a thing...

“Hubby and the others invited this ‘Left Historian Immortal’ to observe the murder process. He exerted his Dao Fruit until he sweated profusely, but couldn’t discern any useful results.

“When he was asked to observe the future, he could only see a certain fragment, but he couldn’t control which timeframe it belonged to. For instance, he once observed that there would be a Battle of the Great Era 390,000 years later and that an immortal would perish. Only when observing the present world could he perceive everything in detail.”

Hearing the Left Historian Immortal’s observation, Lu Yang’s heart skipped a beat. Isn’t that now?

An immortal perishing—does that refer to the first Yu Emperor? Or is it another immortal?

“Another ten thousand years passed. Hubby was uncertain when you could be resurrected, so he suggested I slumber. Once you were revived, you would naturally come to wake me. Thus, I slept in my cave abode.” freewebnovel.com

Ao Ling’s lifespan was finite; she couldn’t wait forever.

“The energy in the Dragon-Pattern Bracelet that the Heaven Mandate Immortal forged for you is depleted.” Lu Yang took out the bracelet and respectfully returned it to its owner.

Ao Ling took the bracelet and froze. She was well aware of what the Dragon-Pattern Bracelet’s depleted energy signified.

That immortal is deliberately erasing information about the dynasty, to the point of becoming enemies with the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other three immortals.”

Ao Ling hadn’t expected so many events to occur after her slumber.

Sensing the atmosphere was somewhat awkward, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy kindly comforted her and took charge of the situation. “Alright, alright, don’t dwell on these things. Thinking about it now won’t yield results. Besides, with this immortal here, nothing will go wrong.”

Lu Yang thought, Senior Ao Ling, could you not trust her in such a matter?

“And you, your name is Lu Yang, right?” Ao Ling got up from the bed, her dragon tail swaying.

She bowed deeply to Lu Yang, stating solemnly, “Thank you for resurrecting Everlasting-jiejie. My husband and the other three immortals, Lianyi, Qing He, and I all owe you a great favor!”

Lu Yang was flustered, not daring to accept such a grand bow. However, whether he dared or not wasn’t up to him; he couldn’t even budge a single strand of Ao Ling’s hair.

Seeing this, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy quickly stepped in to alleviate the situation. “Aiya, Second-in-Command, don’t decline. As the Second-in-Command of the Everlasting Lineage, your status is much higher than unofficial disciples like Little Ling and Lianyi. By seniority, Little Ling can even call you senior brother.”

Unfortunately, she didn’t have eyes.

Chapter 784: The Legitimate Heavenly Court

Lu Yang’s heart trembled. Immortal Fairy, you’re really not afraid of matters escalating, huh?

I haven’t done anything, yet I already have two half-immortal level junior sisters.

Am I worthy?

If Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi are my junior sisters, what should their husband, the Qilin Immortal, call me?

Jiang Lianyi was also considered the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s unofficial disciple. If Lianyi hasn’t woken yet, and I’ve called Lu Yang senior brother first, wouldn’t that make me her senior sister?

“Then what about Hubby? Do you know where he is?”

“He’s probably still alive.” Lu Yang didn’t know how to phrase it.

“Probably?” Ao Ling didn’t understand why Lu Yang said that. I can clearly sense the Dao Fruit suppression from above. Otherwise, I would have become an immortal by now.

“Senior Lianyi woke up over half a year ago. Right after waking, she happened to encounter Little Zhu—ah no, Supreme Lord Zhu Tian—establishing the Demon Kingdom. She exchanged blows with him, shocking the world.

“Currently, no immortals are publicly known in the outside world. Hence, news of ancient half-immortals fighting spread swiftly to everyone.

This wasn’t just Lu Yang’s view; Yun Zhi shared the same perspective. Though the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t verbalize it, she likely thought similarly.

Ao Ling’s expression turned off. “Only half a year has passed. Isn’t it normal for my husband not to know?”

“Huh?”

“Senior Brother, don’t you go into seclusion? My husband often went into seclusion for eight to ten years. During the Ember Legacy Dynasty, he once went into seclusion for several centuries.”

Lu Yang, “...”

If you put it that way, it does seem plausible.

Lu Yang recalled his cultivation experiences.

Not long ago, I had gone into seclusion for an hour.

Big Senior Sister appears to be in a state of spontaneous enlightenment and doesn’t need seclusion.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy advocates for comprehending the Dao within the mundane realm and doesn’t want seclusion.

Thinking about it now, cultivators going into seclusion for eight to ten years is normal, let alone immortals with infinite lifespans and vague perceptions of time. They’re peerless powerhouses who could play a single game of Five in a Row for a century.

“But the Epoch Immortal really met with misfortune,” Lu Yang said. “We discovered the Epoch Immortal’s Fusang Tree original form. It was covered in scars, definitely left from an immortal battle. The Fusang Tree was also empty with no immortal soul inside. Whether the soul dissipated into heaven and earth or fled is unknown.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded beside him. Lu Yang had voiced her thoughts.

“To think such a thing happened! Big Brother Epoch met with misfortune?!” Ao Ling grew solemn. This is no minor matter. The immortal governing time actually died? Who was responsible for this terrible deed?!

“According to the intelligence we currently have, Senior, after you fell asleep, the immortal with the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit wanted to kill you, leading to a battle with the Qilin Immortal. The Ember Legacy Dynasty fell for unknown reasons, an immortal deliberately hid the dynasty’s existence, and the Epoch Immortal’s fate remains uncertain.

“This series of events likely occurred within the same period.”

Lu Yang hadn’t expected another immortal to be born during the Ember Legacy Dynasty. This indicated that five immortals existed during the dynasty. Even so, the dynasty was still destroyed. A single immortal with the Silent Annihilation fruit couldn’t have accomplished that alone. Something else major must have happened—something we don’t know.

“By the way, Senior, we’ve also established a Heavenly Court. Would you consider joining us?”

“You also established a Heavenly Court?” Ao Ling was hearing something like this for the first time.

Lu Yang scratched his head, wearing a rare, abashed smile. “It’s a long story. I was the one who set up the Heavenly Court. At the time, I really didn’t know the Ember Legacy Dynasty already had one; otherwise, I would have picked a different name. Now, our Heavenly Court is too famous; I’m afraid changing the name would be difficult.

“You can probably understand it as us having some matters that were inconvenient to handle in person. Hearing the Immortal Fairy talk about the Heavenly Court, I decided to fabricate one too and use that identity for certain tasks.”

Lu Yang recalled the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mentioning that the Five Ancient Immortals fabricated many versions of the Heavenly Court. Now that I think about it, perhaps this was a backup plan prepared by the four other immortals, just that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t aware?

“Then who are the members of your Heavenly Court?”

Lu Yang counted on his fingers. “Let me list them for you. The Heavenly Court’s ruler is the Immortal Fairy. I have a senior sister named Yun Zhi, who is the Heavenly Court Creed Leader. One of the Four Regents is Senior Lianyi. There are also the Nine Heavenly King Protectors, me, who is the Young Creed Leader, and four Holy Sons.”

Ao Ling was puzzled. “The original purpose of establishing the Heavenly Court was to resurrect Everlasting-jiejie. Since you’ve resurrected her, and she is the Heavenly Court’s ruler, then the Heavenly Court you established should be the legitimate one.”

Chapter 785: Conspiracy

Lu Yang hadn’t expected that the Heavenly Court he established later would become the legitimate one.

But upon careful thought, Ao Ling’s words did make sense.

Ao Ling noticed an individual who stood out among the Heavenly Court members. “Senior Brother, may I know who this Yun Zhi is? She actually holds the position of the Heavenly Court Creed Leader, second only to Everlasting-jiejie and even above Lianyi.” freewebnovel.com

Lu Yang was about to explain, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was faster. “Lass Yun is my arch-rival. Our strengths are on par. Once I recover to my peak, along with you, Second-in-Command, and Lianyi, the four of us joining forces will surely defeat Lass Yun and return victorious.”

Lu Yang looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in surprise. Why am I involved in this?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy seemed to have read Lu Yang’s thoughts and explained, “You are the Second-in-Command. We must share hardships and fortunes.”

Is the price of being the Second-in-Command so heavy?

Besides, since I resurrected you, Immortal Fairy, have I ever enjoyed a single day of fortune?!

“To think such a remarkable person exists.” Ao Ling was astonished. To be called an arch-rival by Everlasting-jiejie, people of later generations truly shouldn’t be underestimated.

“Lianyi has already fought her,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said.

“How did it go?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied seriously, “They fought to a draw.”

Ao Ling heaved a sigh of relief. Then this Yun Zhi isn’t as hard to handle as I’d imagined.

“Senior, shall we leave this bead?” Lu Yang felt that although the bead’s environment was beautiful and a favorite for reclusive cultivators, they couldn’t stay here forever.

“We naturally have to leave.” Ao Ling nodded, then asked in bafflement, “But how do we leave?”

The bead’s internal space was refined by the Qilin Immortal. Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Ao Ling didn’t know about it, much less how to exit.

Lu Yang, “...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy volunteered. “Simple. It’s just a broken bead. Smash it, and we’ll be able to leave.”

Forcibly breaking the bead from outside would cause the internal space to teleport randomly, but breaking it from inside wouldn’t pose such a problem.

Lu Yang got a fright. This is an immortal artifact refined from an entire star. It is capable of neutralizing myriad poisons and contains a miniature world inside.

Suggesting to shatter an immortal artifact just like that... Isn’t it a bit too extravagant?

“Then what do you propose?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy only had this idea.

Lu Yang scratched his head; he was all the more clueless. “Come to think of it, when I entered this bead, it continued flying. Where was it flying to?”

~~~

In the inner zone of Penglai Island, at the core location of the ninth-grade spirit vein.

Unbeknownst to everyone, the three great Transcendent Tribulation cultivators of the East Sea’s human race secretly gathered here.

“Big Brother, do we really have to do this?” The speaker looked tense. It was the Yingzhou Island Lord, known as the Sea-Listening Teacher.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest sighed lightly. “We have no other choice. I am deeply mired in the faith quagmire, unable to extricate myself. Although establishing faiths everywhere helped me condense an Incipient Dao Fruit to become a half-immortal, faith power also has drawbacks.

Not to mention, I was worshipped by someone of a higher status to the point of vomiting blood. Actually, that’s still not too bad—such a powerful being wouldn’t worship me daily; it’s an occasional occurrence.

“The worst is that my body isn’t under my control but influenced by faith. Every action is to fulfil the wishes of believers!”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest had repeatedly watched helplessly as his body disobeyed him, performing acts against his will.

“My physical body is almost completely beyond my control. I must salvage the situation while I can still command my physical body.”

The matter of the Three Mountains Daoist Priest becoming a half-immortal was known only to the Fangzhang Island Lord and the Yingzhou Island Lord. If not for the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s dire circumstances, he would have publicly revealed his half-immortal cultivation and unified the East Sea long ago.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest said indignantly, “I once tried letting my daughter commit evil to ruin my reputation. But the East Sea cultivators’ faith in me is deeply rooted; a few evil deeds can’t harm my reputation!”

The Fangzhang Island Lord, also known as the Six Directions Venerable Lord, asked, “Big Brother, the East Sea has many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Why do you want to take over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body? Although he’s the strongest Transcendent Tribulation cultivator in the East Sea, his lifespan is nearing its limit.”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest waved his hand. “No need to worry about that. Half-immortals differ from immortals. An immortal’s cultivation resides in both the immortal soul and the immortal body, while a half-immortal’s cultivation is all in the soul, and the Incipient Dao Fruit binds to my soul.

“As long as I take over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body, I’ll remain a half-immortal. The Old Dragon Emperor’s lifespan can extend from ten thousand to a hundred thousand years. I won’t have to worry about lifespan problems in the future.

“Furthermore, the Old Dragon Emperor controls the entire Dragon Tribe. What is the Dragon Tribe? It’s the place that gave birth to the Dragon Ancient Ancestor, not to mention that this Ancient Ancestor is also the Qilin Immortal’s wife. One can imagine the Dragon Tribe’s wealth, not just in spirit stones—they might possess half-immortal or even immortal-level magical treasures, like that stone pillar he always coils around. That has to be at least a half-immortal magical treasure!

“Once I take over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body, all this will be ours!”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s words made the other two island lords’ blood surge with fervor.

“It’s a pity that the Old Dragon Emperor refuses to leave the stone pillar. We can only act during that old thing’s birthday banquet!” The Three Mountains Daoist Priest sighed. The Dragon Palace’s foundation runs deep. Even as a half-immortal, I dare not directly barge in.

The Fangzhang Island Lord, the Six Directions Venerable Lord, asked further. “But taking over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body in public won’t be simple, right? Putting aside the issue of being seen by everyone, which makes taking over his body pointless, the most important thing is that your Incipient Dao Fruit doesn’t aid in body takeover. Your soul isn’t as strong as the Old Dragon Emperor’s either. How will you take over his body?”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest sneered coldly. He had already prepared for this. “Six Directions, have you forgotten Yingzhou Island’s ‘Longevity Immortal Grass?’”

The Six Directions Venerable Lord was inwardly floored. “You mean the Great Void Immortal Grass?”

The world spread rumors that deep within Yingzhou Island’s eighth-grade spirit vein grew a Longevity Immortal Grass planted by the Evergreen Supreme Lord.

In truth, it wasn’t the Longevity Immortal Grass but the Great Void Immortal Grass, which induced hallucinations. Someone poisoned by it fell into illusions, dreaming they achieved longevity and became undying. That was how the ‘Longevity Immortal Grass’ rumor started.

The Great Void Immortal Grass was quite terrifying, able to affect even a half-immortal.

However, over the long ages, the Yingzhou Island Lord had grasped the method to counteract the Great Void Immortal Grass’ poison. “As long as we release the Great Void Immortal Grass at the birthday banquet under the guise of presenting gifts, we’ll catch the Old Dragon Emperor off guard. That way, everyone will be poisoned and trapped in illusions, including the Old Dragon Emperor. Only we will be unaffected.

“The Great Void poison affects even souls. I’ll seize that chance to take over the Old Dragon Emperor right there and then! Afterward, no one will know what happened at the birthday banquet!”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest had long prepared thoroughly to take over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body.

Chapter 786: The Meticulous, Foolproof Plan

“Then how do we transport the Great Void Immortal Grass?” The Six Directions Venerable Lord continued asking, his brows slightly furrowed with concern. He couldn’t help but feel the preparations this time weren’t sufficient.

“If we don’t set up restrictions around the Great Void Immortal Grass, it will release poison gas the entire journey. All creatures along the way will be poisoned—that would be too conspicuous.

“But if we set up restrictions, a small box probably can’t hold it, right?”

The Sea-Listening Teacher was confident as he took out a small wooden box. “Can you sense the slightest bit of poison gas from this?”

The Six Directions Venerable Lord was startled. “This holds the Great Void Immortal Grass?”

“Indeed.”

The Sea-Listening Teacher opened the box, presenting a tall and straight immortal grass to the three.

The Six Directions Venerable Lord instinctively activated his cultivation technique to resist the poison gas, but discovered the immortal grass emanated no poison gas even at close range. “What array is this?” He noticed that aside from the Great Void Immortal Grass, an array was engraved inside the box.

The Sea-Listening Teacher closed the box and smiled insipidly. “All things mutually engender and restrain one another. Since the Great Void Immortal Grass exists, there exists something that restrains it. This is a detoxifying array that our Yingzhou Island predecessors discovered in an ancient secret domain. It can neutralize all poisons, perfectly countering the Great Void Immortal Grass.

“Regrettably, research indicates that this detoxifying array should have a focal point, but it has never been found.”

The Six Directions Venerable Lord was amazed. I didn’t imagine such a good thing to exist. He wanted to open the box again to see this rarity, but the Sea-Listening Teacher stopped him.

“It can’t be opened again. Another array is set up inside the box. The next time the box is opened, that array will crush the Great Void Immortal Grass, causing its poison gas to be fully released. Even this detoxifying array won’t be able to suppress it.”

Realization dawned upon the Six Directions Venerable Lord. “So we must open it at the Old Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet!”

“Correct.”

The Six Directions Venerable Lord mulled over it. The plan accounts for everything from start to finish; nothing is left out.

“If I must say a flaw, it would be the Juxuan Island Four Thieves failing their task.” The Three Mountains Daoist Priest sighed.

“The Dragon Palace houses a Dragon Pearl, which is said to be an ancient object with a great connection to the Dragon Tribe’s Ancient Ancestor. The Old Dragon Emperor treasures it dearly. That Dragon Pearl also has detoxifying properties and may affect the Great Void Immortal Grass.

“Fortunately, although the Juxuan Island Four Thieves failed to steal the Dragon Pearl, according to intelligence from the Dragon Palace’s sea market, that Dragon Pearl was snatched by a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple. Even the Dragon Palace has no clue about its whereabouts.” freewebnovel.com

“Good that it’s lost. As long as the Dragon Palace can’t find it, anything works.”

The Sea-Listening Teacher handed the box to the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, who solemnly stowed it away. The three smiled at each other and sprang into action.

No one realized a pill-sized bead flying toward Penglai Island at incredible speed, penetrating layer upon layer of restrictions. It passed through the wooden box and landed precisely at the center of the detoxifying array.

Exactly like the focal point of an array.

The Great Void Immortal Grass withered at an extremely rapid pace.

~~~

“Lu Yang, come!”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord activated his Incipient Dao Fruit, lightly pulling at the void.

Nothing.
