“Lu Yang, come!”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord repeated the technique, reaching out to scratch at space multiple times, but he still couldn’t track Lu Yang down.

Meng Jingzhou remained silent, watching the Vast Sea Daoist Lord act as though he was possessed by a malevolent ghost. The latter appeared to have lost command of his body, clawing at empty space.

If even the Founding Ancestor can’t locate that grandson Lu Yang, he has probably gone to some secret domain prepared by an immortal or the likes.

Five days ago, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord used his Space Incipient Dao Fruit to open a spatial passage, directly stepping over to the East Sea and inquiring about the situation from Meng Jingzhou and the others.

Meng Jingzhou and the other two had no idea where Lu Yang had flown to, shaking their heads.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had no choice but to repeatedly use his Space Incipient Dao Fruit, summoning Lu Yang like he would a soul. But he never succeeded.

Later, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord brought Meng Jingzhou’s trio and the Dragon Tribe’s hero, Xiao Xinghai, back to the Kunpeng Tribe. The Black Feather Venerable Lord personally came out to welcome them. Even someone as powerful as the Black Feather Venerable Lord was merely a junior before the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

If records were accurate, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had interacted with the Kunpeng Tribe in his early years. That was fifty thousand years ago. Whether it was in terms of cultivation or seniority, the Black Feather Venerable Lord didn’t dare to act presumptuously.

“Little Meng and the others, rest assured. With me here, no one in the whole of East Sea is my match,” the Vast Sea Daoist Lord declared impassively, his tone exuding unparalleled confidence to step up to the occasion.

He wasn’t wrong. For an East Sea without half-immortals, he was unbeatable.

Five days later, the aftereffects of Tao Yaoye using the Metamorphic Immortal Body faded. The Old Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet was about to commence, so the Vast Sea Daoist Lord led the group to attend.

The Old Dragon Emperor’s nine-thousandth birthday banquet was a major event of paramount importance in the East Sea. All seafolk and humans at the Divine Transfiguration Stage and above received invitations.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord stood on an auspicious cloud with his hands clasped behind his back. The sea’s surface was filled with human cultivators displaying their mighty abilities, crossing the East Sea to attend the birthday banquet. In the sea were countless old ancestors of various races in their original forms—fish, crab, or shellfish—coming in response to the invitation.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord laughed heartily, his visage glowing with vigor. “Of course. Back in the day, I established a great reputation in the East Sea. It’s a pity you young cultivators only know me as the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Resurgence Ancestor but are unaware of my East Sea experiences.”

The era where the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was active in the East Sea was too distant, so distant that even Chieftain Xiao and Xiao Xinghai hadn’t heard of his deeds here.

“The ‘Vast Sea’ in my Daoist title commemorates my active years in the East Sea. At that time, I was still at the Fusion Stage. I was researching the Dao of Space, which triggered spatial turbulence, teleporting me from the Dao-Seeking Sect to the East Sea.

“The spatial turbulence severely injured me, and my strength fell below the Golden Core Stage. Fortunately, the fishermen then saved me.

“In that small fishing village, I met a little princess who had sneaked out from the Dragon Palace, and we hit it off immediately.

“Under the little princess’s care, my injuries gradually healed. The two of us felt an instant bond and became Dao partners, roaming the East Sea together. We searched for immortal grass, encountered rogue cultivators, and ventured into secret domains...”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord gazed up at the sky and let out a long sigh, his tone full of melancholy. “Alas, those who walk different paths cannot make plans together. We ultimately had racial differences and couldn’t be together.”

Meng Jingzhou and the others were immersed in the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s lament, as if they could feel his emotions from that time.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord abruptly turned his head, glaring fixedly at the Black Feather Venerable Lord.

Chapter 787: A Transcendent Tribulation Cultivator Defies and Challenges a Half-Immortal

The battle between a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and a half-immortal was on the verge of erupting. The East Sea hadn’t witnessed a battle of this level in a hundred thousand years.

The Black Feather Venerable Lord lived up to his reputation as a seasoned Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. He acted decisively and showed no hesitation.

While the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was immersed in his sorrowful recollection, the Black Feather Venerable Lord secretly employed the Dao of Time to defy and challenge the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, tracing back through time to pry open a corner of truth buried in history.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord didn’t dare to be careless, countering with his Space Incipient Dao Fruit.

The Black Feather Venerable Lord appeared to have employed some unknown secret art that caused the Vast Sea Daoist Lord to lose one of his five senses—his hearing. Even though the Black Feather Venerable Lord pleaded for mercy multiple times, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord heard none of it.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord narrowly won, while the Black Feather Venerable Lord had lost honorably despite his defeat!

Meng Jingzhou felt that the Kunpeng Tribe truly deserved its place among the Ten Great Sea Tribes. Their survival to this day is undoubtedly tied to their formidable strength.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had held back from striking too viciously. After all, they were above the East Sea waters, with many races coming and going, and the Kunpeng Tribe members were also present. He had to leave a bit of face for the Black Feather Venerable Lord.

Thus, there weren’t many unscathed patches left on the Black Feather Venerable Lord’s face.

Chieftain Xiao and Xiao Xinghai sighed inwardly. The Old Ancestor truly has a death wish, blurting out everything.

Xiao Xinghai almost brought out the coffin again. This way, the Old Ancestor won’t end up with his corpse exposed in the wild, giving outsiders a reason to say the Kunpeng Tribe’s descendants are unfilial.

Since he’s still alive, there’s no need to take it out.

The coffin had been soaked in copious amounts of Dragon blood, staining the originally pure black coffin a deep crimson inside and out, making it look particularly ghastly. Its grade had also risen by half a level.

Hearing the embarrassing dark history the Black Feather Venerable Lord had revealed, Su Yiren became even more determined to make good use of the yang-boosting essence blood in the vial.

“Just what kind of demon beast does this blood belong to? Even Dragon and Phoenix blood don’t seem as potent. Could it be from a hybrid descendant of both Dragon and Phoenix?”

The group entered the waters of the East Sea. No sooner had they descended than they heard a voice calling out.

“Yiren, over here!”

“Gu’er, what are you doing here?” Su Yiren was surprised. It was precisely Ao Gu’er who had invited her to the Old Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet.

Ao Gu’er grabbed Su Yiren’s hand, somewhat displeased. “You’re one to talk! Couldn’t you have come to the Dragon Palace earlier to look for me? You just had to wait until the day of the banquet.”

Not forgetting her main task, she gracefully bowed to the Vast Sea Daoist Lord. “You must be Senior Vast Sea. Emperor Father instructed me to wait for you all here.”

Hearing Ao Gu’er’s name, Meng Jingzhou and the others wore odd expressions. Back then, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had stolen the Dragon Pearl from this very person before them, even shamelessly calling her ‘mommy’ in the process.

Fortunately, Lu Yang hadn’t come along. Otherwise, this situation would have been extremely awkward.

It’s a pity Old Lu isn’t here.

Ao Gu’er led the group all the way down to the seabed until they reached the end of the winding sea market shaped like a true dragon, where the Dragon Palace stood.

The Dragon Palace was surrounded by clusters of millennium-old coral. Undulating seaweeds swayed gently like curtains. The palace complex was majestic and presented a dazzling sight. The interior walls were embedded with various resplendent gems and pearls, emitting a soft yet radiant glow. Numerous shrimp soldiers and crab generals stood guard, along with patrolling members of the Yaksha Tribe.

A portion of the guests had already arrived at the Dragon Palace. They were leaders of major factions, paying much attention to the activities of the cultivation world’s top experts. The Vast Sea Daoist Lord was no mysterious figure. As the Resurgence Ancestor, he was highly active fifty thousand years ago, and many portraits of him were passed down.

“Look! That’s the Vast Sea Daoist Lord!” freewebnovel.com

Ao Gu’er led the group through the Dragon Palace to its deepest part. Pushing open a large, heavy door, they saw an old azure dragon coiled around an impossibly thick stone pillar.

Facing the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, the Old Dragon Emperor didn’t dare to put on airs. He climbed down from the pillar with a thud and transformed into human form.

The Old Dragon Emperor was truly old. After he assumed human form, he resembled an old man with one foot already in the grave. He walked unsteadily, as if a mere wave could knock him over. Ao Gu’er hurriedly went to support him.

I just don’t know what went wrong afterward; I couldn’t locate him at all. What exactly is the origin of this Dragon Pearl of yours?”

The Old Dragon Emperor shook his head. “I have no idea either. I only know that it’s an item from antiquity. It is indestructible and has detoxifying properties. I wasn’t even aware that there was a smaller bead inside the Dragon Pearl.”

The Dragon Pearl was among that pile and not particularly conspicuous.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord huffed and puffed. When have I ever experienced such wealth? If the Dao-Seeking Sect had been this rich, would I have ended up with the title of “Resurgence Ancestor?”

Isn’t it precisely because I appeared during the Dao-Seeking Sect’s poorest period that I’m called the Resurgence Ancestor? Even after I made the sect prosperous later on, it didn’t reach the Dragon Palace’s level of extravagance.

Of course, the Dao-Seeking Sect is definitely richer than the Dragon Tribe now. After all, we have raided the lairs of several half-immortals.

Without even a single lead, where am I supposed to find that kid Lu Yang?

I promised I’d protect him. This is a terrible start.

A female dragon with an enchanting figure stepped out from behind the pillar. Her eyes twinkled with a captivating gaze, and the three dragon scales on her forehead added to her charm, exuding an irresistible temptation.

It’s been fifty thousand years. Can a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator live for fifty thousand years?

Before Ao Ya, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord appeared flustered and uneasy, his hands fidgeting with nowhere to put them.

Ao Ya shot the Vast Sea Daoist Lord a glare. “I’m not as capable as you. I’m merely a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. However, before I went into slumber, I instructed my descendants to wake me either if the Dragon Tribe faces a crisis or when you emerge in the world again!”

She smiled brightly as she grabbed the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s hand, dragging him toward a room at the side before he could say anything. “What a coincidence! I’ve only been awake for a few days and haven’t recovered my former strength yet. Perfect timing for you to accompany me in dual cultivation! And you can also explain why you ran away back then!”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s face paled instantly. I came to the East Sea but failed to protect Lu Yang, and now I’m about to lose my chastity first?

Once again, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator defied and challenged a half-immortal.

Chapter 788: The Transcendent Tribulation Cultivator’s Sweeping Victory

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord looked at everyone helplessly, hoping someone could help him.

The only thing that separated a half-immortal from a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator was the Incipient Dao Fruit they possessed, which offered no enhancement to one’s physical constitution. Meeting Ao Ya once again after fifty thousand years, he feared he would end up suffering the same fate as last time.

Unfortunately, when faced with this situation, even the highest-ranking half-immortal Li Haoran couldn’t provide any assistance, much less anyone else.

Although Meng Jingzhou’s blood had yang-boosting properties, his cultivation was limited. Its efficacy extended to Divine Transfiguration cultivators at best, rendering it useless in this scenario.

But dragging an old flame into a room the moment you meet again...isn’t that a bit too hasty?

However, such words could only be muttered within his mind.

The Old Dragon Emperor could understand Ao Ya’s impatience. After all, as a member of the Dragon Tribe, he also possessed the dragon’s inherently lascivious nature. It was merely that age had caught up to him, and he could no longer act on it.

Everyone readily agreed.

The Dragon Palace’s main hall was a colossal complex constructed from iridescent coral reefs. Mothers-of-pearl emitted a moonlight glow, forming shimmering walls, while seaweeds swayed gently like jadeite curtains.

I heard the Second Imperial Prince’s search for longevity-extending items hadn’t gone smoothly.

Meng Jingzhou suddenly remembered that extending the Xia Emperor’s lifespan didn’t necessarily require longevity items. Something like the Metamorphic Immortal Grass, which forcibly raised one’s cultivation realm, could also extend lifespans. Once the relevant cultivation realm is achieved, lifespan naturally won’t be a problem.

However, he didn’t plan to tell this to the Second Imperial Prince, who was deliberately trying to befriend him. He didn’t exactly like this imperial prince.

Noticing Meng Jingzhou, the Second Imperial Prince’s eyes lit up, and he stepped forward to greet him. “Young Master Meng, you came after all.”

Ever since Lu Yang’s group was abducted by that mysterious Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, he had been gripped with constant anxiety. Fortunately, he later heard that Lu Yang and the others were at the Dragon Palace’s sea market and temporarily staying with the Kunpeng Tribe. Only then did he relax.

If something had happened to Lu Yang and the others on the ship, whether he could return to Great Xia alive was up in the air. With the Dao-Seeking Sect’s and the Meng Family’s foundations, if they were truly bent on seeking revenge, I’m afraid these ten Fusion cultivators and one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator on our three ships wouldn’t withstand it.

“I am deeply regretful about the matter of Fellow Daoist Lu Yang’s disappearance. I’d also dispatched people to inquire about his whereabouts, but unfortunately, nothing came up.” The Second Imperial Prince shook his head and sighed with genuine regret.

If I had managed to find Lu Yang, he would be indebted to me for this favor. That way, he would be on my side in the future struggle for the throne.

“It’s fine. Old Lu has nine lives; nothing will happen to him,” Meng Jingzhou said dismissively.

If anyone present was the least worried about Lu Yang’s safety, it would definitely be Meng Jingzhou.

Even if something happens to the Old Dragon Emperor, nothing will happen to Old Lu.

“Did Senior Vast Sea not come?” The Second Imperial Prince wanted to meet this legendary Resurgence Ancestor.

“The Founding Ancestor is currently discussing the Dao with his good friend from the Dragon Tribe.”

“I see.”

Meng Jingzhou and the others sat with the Kunpeng Tribe, idly nibbling on the fruits on the table.

A commotion arose in the Dragon Palace, mainly from the human cultivators’ side. The Black Feather Venerable Lord looked over and exclaimed softly, “Heh, I didn’t expect the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s trio to arrive so early. They’re really showing the Old Dragon Emperor face.”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest, the Sea-Listening Teacher, and the Six Directions Venerable Lord were the mainstay of the East Sea's human cultivators and wielded immense influence, especially the Three Mountains Daoist Priest. Most human cultivators had paid respects to his statues to some degree, praying for a smooth cultivation journey.

Man Gu noticed the Three Mountains Daoist Priest holding a small wooden box and suddenly remembered that their group seemed to have come empty-handed. “Shouldn’t we prepare a gift too?” He felt a bit embarrassed about coming to the East Sea for a free feast.

Meng Jingzhou waved his hand. “The Old Dragon Emperor is a senior elder. If anyone should prepare gifts, it’s cultivators at the Void Refinement or Fusion stages. We juniors just need to eat and drink.”

Only then did Man Gu feel reassured and continued burying his head in the fruits.

“Black Feather.” A seafolk of an imposing bearing walked over to greet them. His race wasn’t apparent.

The Black Feather Venerable Lord smiled. “Mystic Water, it’s been ten years since we last met. I heard that you were bedridden a while ago. How are you so lively now?”

“Don’t mention it. If I hadn’t made up an excuse, my descendants would have kept pestering me to remain as the tribe chieftain. It was too annoying, so I said I was old, frail, and bedridden, and that it was time to change the chieftain.”

“I told you long ago that being the tribe chieftain isn’t a good job. Look at me—I retired ages ago.” The Black Feather Venerable Lord preened. This is called foresight.

Seeing the two converse happily, Meng Jingzhou quietly asked Xiao Xinghai who this person was.

“That’s Mystic Water Venerable Lord of the Xuanwu Tribe, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. He’s known the Black Feather Old Ancestor since they were young. The two of them are very close, often acting together. Since both their bodies are black, they’re called the ‘East Sea Twin Blacks.’”

“East Sea Twin Blacks?”

“As you know, my tribe excels in speed, while the Xuanwu Tribe excels in defense. When the two old ancestors were young, they couldn’t stay idle, always going out to stir up trouble. “Now that they’ve reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, they rarely act together.”

“Grown old and settled down?”

“It’s because the Old Ancestor’s speed has reached the peak. No one can catch up to him anymore, so he no longer needs the Mystic Water Venerable Lord’s protection.

Apart from the Mystic Water Venerable Lord, the Transcendent Tribulation cultivators from the remaining seven major sea tribes had also taken their seats. Those seven seafolk Transcendent Tribulation cultivators all sat far away from the Black Feather Venerable Lord and the Mystic Water Venerable Lord, afraid the duo might air their dirty laundry.

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Chapter 789: Grand Gift

Although the Vast Sea Daoist Lord possessed a Space Incipient Dao Fruit and could be considered formidable among half-immortals, Meng Jingzhou felt that once he cultivated to the half-immortal stage, he might very well be able to challenge the Vast Sea Daoist Lord in combat. In particular, when he saw Ao Ya and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord exchanging flirtatious glances, he was certain the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was enjoying himself.

Meng Jingzhou was convinced that when the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was dragged into the side chamber to be “exploited” under the demands and pressure, it was voluntary. Otherwise, he would have used his Space Incipient Dao Fruit to escape long ago!

So you envy my Single’s Spirit Root, huh? Wait till I become a half-immortal—I’ll show you what a half-immortal’s Single’s Spirit Root is like!

Finally, the Old Dragon Emperor made his entrance.

With the appearance of the birthday star, the entire hall rose in unison, congratulating the Old Dragon Emperor on his grand birthday. Their voices were thunderous, like mountains and seas roaring. All the East Sea’s high-level cultivators had gathered here to offer their congratulations. In the East Sea, only the Dragon Emperor could command such a treatment.

Ao Ya and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord were exceptions. Their seniority was higher than the Old Dragon Emperor’s, so they did not need to follow the crowd.

“Alright, that’s enough. No need to be so reverent to this old man.” The Old Dragon Emperor sat on the palace leader’s seat with a benevolent smile on his face, gesturing for everyone not to stand on formality. The most important thing when celebrating a birthday was to be at ease.

Clam maidens and members of the Jiao-Folk Tribe danced gracefully in the center of the main hall, their beautiful movements enchanting the audience.

Dancing was also a form of cultivation. There were quite a few cultivators who entered the Dao through dance, though few chose this particular cultivation method. To date, the individual with the highest attainment on this path was Zhu Tian. Since Zhu Tian emerged and established the Demon Kingdom, the number of cultivators entering the Dao through dance had begun to increase.

~~~

“I can’t find any other way to leave this damn bead. We might as well just break it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy laughed triumphantly. It seems that we still have to rely on the method I’d thought of from the start.

Lu Yang had no other choice but to agree to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s idea.

~~~

The birthday banquet proceeded smoothly. Aside from the underwater dances, Conch tribesmen were playing immortal-like music, while aquatic scholarly talents composed and recited poems extolling the Old Dragon Emperor’s majesty and benevolence. Dragon Tribe elders transformed into their original forms to showcase magical arts and theatrical performances depicting the glorious achievements of the Old Dragon Emperor in his youth.

Seeing this, the Old Dragon Emperor raised his wine cup high, laughing heartily as if he had become two thousand years younger.

The Black Feather Venerable Lord was suffocating below. Behind each of these glorious achievements hid stories known to few. He yearned to reveal them, but considering this was a birthday banquet, he figured it wouldn’t be appropriate to stage a performance of the birthday star brandishing a cane to beat someone.

The Mystic Water Daoist Lord was similarly suffocating.

After the theatrical performances concluded, the gift-presenting segment commenced.

In the Old Dragon Emperor’s youth, he had been a rake, unrestrained and licentious, fathering over thirty children.

One must know that the higher a cultivator’s cultivation, the more difficult it was to produce offspring. The Dragon Tribe was not an exception to this. With Ao Ya as an example, back when Ao Ya and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord were like lovers inseparably joined at the hip and not leaving their room for a full month, Ao Ya still did not get pregnant.

“Emperor Father, this is a Nine-Cycle Spirit Pill I commissioned a Great Xia pill-concocting grandmaster to refine. It can regulate the body and nurture vital energy.” The Dragon Palace’s First Prince opened a box, revealing a spirit pill with nine pill marks. The moment it was opened, a rich fragrance assailed the nostrils. It was clearly a marvelous pill. freewebnovel.com

“Emperor Father, this is a Five-Colored Evergreen Flower I retrieved from the depths of the Netherworld Abyss. It will never wither.”

The Five-Colored Evergreen Flower symbolized longevity, for it never withered—a fitting gift. However, this flower grew in the Netherworld Abyss, which teemed with countless Fusion stage demon beasts and was fraught with danger. The fact that the Second Prince could pluck it under such circumstances demonstrated his filial piety.

Over thirty princes and princesses presented their gifts in succession. Some emphasized efficacy, others sincerity, but the commonality was that all these items were extremely difficult to obtain. Every reveal elicited gasps from the crowd. It was truly befitting of the tremendously wealthy Dragon Palace; even the gifts were so precious. Most of the gifts from the Fusion cultivators couldn’t compare.

“The Five-Colored Evergreen Flower is quite pretty,” the Vast Sea Daoist Lord muttered, chewing on a Nine-Cycle Spirit Pill to restore his yang energy.

Meng Jingzhou cast a strange look at the Vast Sea Daoist Lord. Founding Ancestor, why are you carrying that thing around?

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord was inwardly annoyed and transmitted an auditory message to explain. “I just used my Space Incipient Dao Fruit to retrieve this from our sect a moment ago!”

Meng Jingzhou simply uttered, “Oh.”

Then, he saw the Vast Sea Daoist Lord reach under the table, secretly activating his Space Incipient Dao Fruit to open a small spatial portal directly to the Netherworld Abyss and pluck a Five-Colored Evergreen Flower.

“I’ll give this to Little Ya after the banquet is over,” the Vast Sea Daoist Lord murmured cheerfully.

After the princes, princesses, Dragon Tribe elders, and Fusion cultivators presented their gifts, it was the Transcendent Tribulation cultivators’ turn to showcase their sincerity.

Among all the gifts presented so far, the one the Old Dragon Emperor liked most was the Ancestral Dragon Grass given by Ao Ran. He directly beckoned Ao Ran to bring it up for closer inspection.

The Old Dragon Emperor greatly revered the Dragon Ancient Ancestor—Ancient Ancestor Ao Ling, who could be termed the strongest half-immortal. As such, he also liked anything related to Ao Ling.

He carefully examined the dragon-claw-shaped Ancestral Dragon Grass, and a scene from ancient times seemed to unfold before his eyes—the Dragon Ancient Ancestor tenderly caring for the Ancestral Dragon Grass and watching it grow robustly.

“Senior Dragon Emperor, this junior has an item here that is also related to the Dragon Ancient Ancestor.” The Three Mountains Daoist Priest held a wooden box aloft with both hands, displaying respect to the Old Dragon Emperor.

Although the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s arrival had made him nervous for a while, he felt relieved upon remembering that the Great Void Immortal Grass would also be effective against a half-immortal.

“Oh, something related to the Dragon Ancient Ancestor? What is inside the box?” The Old Dragon Emperor grew interested. Although seafolk and humans often clashed in the East Sea, as the leader of the sea tribes, he still admired the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, who was the leader of the humans.

The Dragon Ancient Ancestor was a legendary figure in the East Sea, her influence no less than that of Jiang Lianyi in the Demon Region.

Everyone’s gaze converged on the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, curious to know what the box contained.

The Sea-Listening Teacher and the Six Directions Venerable Lord still lacked experience. As soon as they thought of what was about to happen, they broke out in a slight cold sweat.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest smiled faintly, appearing calm and composed as he said unhurriedly, “The most important aspect of a gift is the element of surprise. Why don’t you open it personally, Senior Dragon Emperor?”

“That works too.”

Ao Gu’er, who stood by the side, took the wooden box and delivered it to the Old Dragon Emperor’s hands.

Seeing this, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest was assured that his plan was more than halfway to success.

In truth, the wooden box didn’t contain anything related to the Dragon Ancient Ancestor. This was merely a pretext to trick the Old Dragon Emperor into opening the box himself and coming into close contact with the Great Void Immortal Grass’ poison.

The Old Dragon Emperor eagerly opened the wooden box.

A loud sound pierced the air, as if something had shattered. Thick smoke billowed from the wooden box, obscuring one’s view.

Two figures suddenly appeared. When the Old Dragon Emperor saw one of them, he was tongue-tied, his eyes visibly widening in shock. He was so overwhelmed with emotions that he couldn’t speak for a long time. Clutching his chest, his eyes rolled back, and he nearly fainted.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest circulated his cultivation technique to resist the Great Void Immortal Grass’ poison. I didn’t expect it to be so potent, dense enough to block even spiritual consciousness and line of vision.

The corner of his lips curled into a cold smile as he casually stepped forward. “Senior Dragon Emperor, how do you like this grand gift I’ve presented?”

“I...I like it.”

“Do you currently feel your senses blurring and your soul unstable, as if you’re experiencing hallucinations?”

“Yes.”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest wore a smug expression of someone whose scheme had succeeded. When he walked over to the Old Dragon Emperor and saw the two figures within the smoke, he froze.

The smoke dispersed, revealing the figures of Ao Ling and Lu Yang.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest stood rooted to the spot, dumbstruck.

Why is the Dragon Ancient Ancestor here?

Did I get poisoned too?

Chapter 790: Ao Ling Appears

“The Dragon Ancient Ancestor?!”

The banquet attendees saw the peerlessly beautiful woman in a black dress standing calmly before the Old Dragon Emperor. They rose to their feet abruptly, their eyes bulging and faces filled with disbelief.

Several seafolk dignitaries were so flabbergasted that they couldn’t maintain their human forms. With a loud sound, they reverted to their original forms, which were enormous, instantly throwing the entire Dragon Palace into chaos.

Ao Ling was renowned throughout the East Sea, and her portraits were also widely circulated. Those qualified to attend this birthday banquet were all prominent figures in the East Sea and had seen her portraits before.

The sea tribes with deep heritage and ancestors who were half-immortals had records of those half-immortal ancestors being defeated by Ao Ling.

The Phoenix Ancient Ancestor had also publicly declared at the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony that she and the Dragon Ancient Ancestor were both wives of the Qilin Immortal.

The crowd couldn’t help but be astounded by the layer upon layer of identities.

“Heavens, she’s identical to the ancient paintings—she really is the Dragon Ancient Ancestor!”

“Why would the Dragon Ancient Ancestor appear here?!”

“Is this what the Three Mountains Daoist Priest meant by an item related to the Dragon Ancient Ancestor?!”

“This is more than just related!”

“As expected of our East Sea’s human leader! To think he found the Dragon Ancient Ancestor, who has been missing for three hundred thousand years!”

“Ancient cultivators have been emerging one after another. The Great Era has arrived, huh?”

Hearing these exclamations and praises, the Sea-Listening Teacher and the Six Directions Venerable Lord were bewildered. They each slapped their own faces and turned to see the Dragon Ancient Ancestor still standing there.

Is the Great Void Immortal Grass’ poison this potent? Did we get affected despite circulating our cultivation technique?

Before opening the wooden box, the Old Dragon Emperor had exhausted his imagination pondering what relic of the Dragon Ancient Ancestor could possibly be inside such a small box.

Never in my wildest dreams did I imagine that the box contained the Ancient Ancestor herself.

“Where have we ended up this time?” Not only were the people present dumbfounded, but even one of the parties involved, Lu Yang, was also dumbfounded.

Why are there so many people here? And who is this old dragon man who’s so excited that he’s about to faint?

Wait a moment. This can’t be the Old Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet, right?

The timing seems to match up.

“Hmm? Why is there a withered Great Void Immortal Grass here?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s voice sounded in the mental space.

“What is the Great Void Immortal Grass?”

“A type of grass that tempers one’s mental state by creating illusions. Its effects aren’t up to par, though. When I cooked and plated dishes, this stuff could only serve as a garnish.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s cooking emphasized the impeccable combination of color, aroma, and taste.

Hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy speak so casually, Lu Yang assumed it was just an immortal grass with a fancy name but little substance.

Pft—

The old horse, who was representing the Dragon-Horse Tribe at the banquet, spat out his spirit wine and looked at Lu Yang as if he’d seen a ghost.

Just what happened during this time I wasn’t with you?

It’s only been a month since you all left the Dragon-Horse Tribe. How did this kid Lu Yang end up standing next to the Dragon Ancient Ancestor?

Ao Ling was someone who had weathered countless storms after all. She reacted swiftly, cupping her fists toward Lu Yang. “Many thanks, little Fellow Daoist, for awakening me from slumber. May I know if you would be willing to join my Heavenly Court?”

Lu Yang returned the salute, his manners perfect but his tone resolute. “Senior Ao Ling, this junior appreciates your kind offer, but as a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect, I absolutely cannot join another faction!”

“That is most regrettable.”

The context of their casual exchange sparked endless speculation among the listeners.

“So the Dragon Ancient Ancestor is also a member of the Heavenly Court, just like the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor.”

“Both the Dragon and Phoenix ancestors are in the Heavenly Court. I’ve heard they possessed the talent to become immortals, though for unknown reasons, they never did. Just how powerful is this Heavenly Court?”

“The Dragon Ancient Ancestor was sleeping all this time, and Lu Yang awakened her?”

If the Vast Sea Daoist Lord was greatly surprised to see Ao Ling, then seeing Lu Yang standing beside her was downright shocking.

He used his Space Incipient Dao Fruit and grabbed Lu Yang by the scruff of his neck, yanking him to his side in an instant. “What exactly is going on with you, kid?”

Lu Yang explained with an innocent expression. “I don’t know. The Dragon Pearl sucked me in. I saw the Dragon Ancient Ancestor lying inside, so I woke her up.”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord poked Lu Yang’s forehead. “You’ve got guts, kid! Lucky for you, the Dragon Ancient Ancestor doesn’t have morning grumpiness, else a single sneeze from her could have finished you off!”

“I won’t dare next time, I won’t dare next time,” Lu Yang apologized profusely with a smile.

“Ao Cang of the Dragon Tribe pays respects to the Ancient Ancestor!” The Old Dragon Emperor rose to his feet shakily and kowtowed to Ao Ling.

Ao Ya also kowtowed.

There was another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator named Ao Fan in the Dragon Tribe. He was at the Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation Stage. He was at the Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation Stage and served as the Dragon Palace’s Vice Palace Leader. It was he who had led Ao Li and the others to attend the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony.

I hadn’t expected that after seeing the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor at the Demon Kingdom, I’d see our tribe’s ancient ancestor at the Palace Lord’s birthday banquet half a year later.

“Ao Fan of the Dragon Tribe pays respects to the Ancient Ancestor!”

Noticing the Dragon Tribe had only three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, Ao Ling knitted her brows slightly. “Does the current Dragon Tribe not even have a single half-immortal?”

The Old Dragon Emperor was ashamed by her words and didn’t know how to respond. Incipient Dao Fruits aren’t that easy to form.

Be it seafolk or humans, their wills united in this moment, and they respectfully bowed in unison, their voices as thunderous as the mountains and seas.

“We pay our respects to Senior Ao Ling!”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest remained composed. Kneeling on the ground like everyone else, he also loudly greeted Ao Ling.

Suddenly, a pair of elegant shoes entered his field of vision.

He looked up, unsure how long Ao Ling had been standing before him.

Ao Ling stared at the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, her eyes narrowing slightly and her pupils transforming into vertical golden dragon eyes. An extremely dangerous smile curved her lips. “If my eyes weren’t mistaken just now, the moment I appeared, your soul showed signs of leaving the body. Were you intending to take over the body of this descendant of my tribe?”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s body takeover method was subtle, and he had immediately retracted it upon seeing Ao Ling, confident no one would notice.

However, while he could deceive others, he could never hope to fool Ao Ling, who had gained much experience from countless battles in ancient times. The ancient era was far more chaotic than the present, and body takeover was a frequent occurrence.

“What?!”

Ao Ling’s words caused an uproar. The crowd looked at her and the Three Mountains Daoist Priest incredulously. Those whose minds worked a bit slower hadn’t even grasped the situation.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest wore a blank look of confusion, as if he didn’t know what Ao Ling was talking about. “Senior Ao Ling, do you perhaps have some misunderstanding about this junior?

Ao Ling sneered, seeing through the Three Mountains Daoist Priest situation at a glance. “Misunderstanding? Then why don’t you explain—where did this Incipient Dao Fruit condensed from faith power on you come from?”

Hearing that the Three Mountains Daoist Priest possessed an Incipient Dao Fruit, both seafolk and humans revealed astonished expressions.

“What did the Dragon Ancient Ancestor just say? The Three Mountains Daoist Priest has an Incipient Dao Fruit? Doesn’t that mean he’s become a half-immortal?!”

“The first half-immortal in the East Sea in a hundred thousand years!”

Ao Ling continued, “I don’t know where you learned his half-baked method of condensing an Incipient Dao Fruit with faith power. You didn’t even filter it and simply let the faith power pour into your body.

“I presume your body is no longer under your control most of the time. Under such circumstances, if you don’t choose body takeover, I’d be very curious to know what other method you could have to save yourself.”

Originally, Ao Ling didn’t understand much about faith power. However, the foundation of the Ember Legacy Dynasty was faith. Having spent twenty thousand years there, she had long since become familiar with the usage of faith power.

“I didn’t expect the Dragon Ancient Ancestor to be so knowledgeable about faith power.” The Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s gaze turned fearsome, his face dark enough that water could drip out.

Hearing Ao Ling dissect his situation word by word, he was aware he couldn’t bluff his way through, so he simply stopped pretending. “My original plan was to secretly take over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body, thereby gaining control of the entire East Sea. Since you won’t give me that opportunity, don’t blame me for resorting to force!”

He initially didn’t want the matter of his taking over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body to be exposed, fearing complications. But that doesn’t mean I can’t fight!

Lu Yang sat beside the Vast Sea Daoist Lord obediently. Three Mountains Daoist Priest, with how strong you are, I wonder if you’d vomit blood if I bow to you.

Chapter 791: A Nascent Soul Old Monster Defies A Half-Immortal

“Old Ancestor, help me out.” Lu Yang stealthily transmitted an auditory message to the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

Everyone’s gaze converged on Ao Ling and the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, so no one noticed this Nascent Soul old monster here.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had learned about the Heavenly Court from Yun Zhi. “Since I said I’d protect you once, you can act as you please. I’ll be your backup.”

Lu Yang requested the Vast Sea Daoist Lord to open a portal to teleport him away secretly.

Upon reaching his destination, Lu Yang used the Tree-Planting Mantra to create a clone and made it wear a mask, preparing to make an appearance as Young Creed Leader Lu.

Back then, the Dijiang Tribe’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivator had given him this monk when he impersonated Young Creed Leader Lu. Without a half-immortal with the Insight Incipient Dao Fruit, no one could see through the identity beneath the mask.

~~~

An ethereal voice resounded throughout the Dragon Palace.

“Heh, a mere half-immortal dares to provoke the Four Regents of the Heavenly Court? Do you really think our Heavenly Court can be trifled with?”

Under the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s assistance, Lu Yang’s voice had passed through several spatial transfers before echoing in the Dragon Palace. This was a half-immortal technique. The voice was also processed, preventing anyone from detecting its source.

“The Heavenly Court!”

“It’s someone from the Heavenly Court!”

Humans and seafolk alike were flabbergasted and grew restless. They hadn’t expected someone from the Heavenly Court to come so soon after Ao Ling had awakened. What reaction speed! They must have left some contingency on the Dragon Ancient Ancestor, detectable once she awakens.

Accompanied by the opening of a spatial rift, a figure emerged from the other side.

It was none other than Young Creed Leader Lu, who had been away from the public eye for a long time.

A sword hung at Young Creed Leader Lu’s waist, and his smile was as gentle as a spring breeze, his demeanor as elegant as ever. He cupped his fists toward the figure behind the door. “Many thanks for your assistance, Junior Uncle. You need not accompany me further.”

Then the door closed, with no guardian dispatched, as if Young Creed Leader Lu’s safety was not a concern... Or perhaps, it was a display of absolute confidence in Young Creed Leader Lu.

“Penglai Island Lord, Three Mountains Daoist Priest?” The corners of Young Creed Leader Lu’s mouth curved into a smile, though it carried a hint of coldness.

He narrowed his eyes. “It’s merely an Incipient Dao Fruit condensed from faith power, yet you have the audacity to shout and clamor here. Why trouble my junior sister to deal with a vermin like you? I can handle it on her behalf.” As he spoke, he deliberately glanced in a certain direction.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s face darkened. The legendary Heavenly Court has two immortals presiding over it—Dou Heavenly Sovereign and Creed Leader Yun. I’m absolutely no match for them.

But I am a dignified half-immortal! So what if the other party is Young Creed Leader Lu? He’s only at the Nascent Soul Stage, yet he has the nerve to talk big and claim he could deal with me?

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest was so angry that he burst out laughing. “In that case, I should indeed seek to learn about the ancient Heavenly Court’s methods—” Before the Three Mountains Daoist Priest could finish, Young Creed Leader Lu pressed his palms together and gave the Three Mountains Daoist Priest a sincere bow.

In an instant, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s face turned deathly pale, and a mouthful of heart’s blood surged to his throat. freewebnovel.com

Cough! The Three Mountains Daoist Priest directly vomited a gout of old blood, staining the nearby sea waters crimson.

He staggered back two steps. The look he gave Lu Yang was no longer one of scorn or rage, but of terror.

A Nascent Soul cultivator bowed, and a half-immortal spat blood!

Witnessing this, the crowd was flabbergasted. This overturned all cultivation theories. “What technique is this?!”

Even the Vast Sea Daoist Lord wore a peculiar expression. What kind of technique is this, making someone spit blood with a bow?

~~~

“How is this possible? A Nascent Soul cultivator could make a half-immortal vomit blood? How did he do it?”

“The fact is right before your eyes. Do you still not believe it?”

“Perhaps the ancient Heavenly Court has another expert here.”

“No, there should be another reason. I think I’ve seen records about this somewhere before...

“I remember! I recall reading it in an ancient text from the Great Qian era. Cultivators who cultivate with faith power most fear encountering opponents whose fate profile is superior to their own.”

That person mumbled to himself excitedly, speaking rapidly. “That’s it! The Heavenly Court ruled antiquity. Young Creed Leader Lu is the future leader of the Heavenly Court and has taken an immortal as his shifu. His fate profile naturally far surpasses the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s!”

“Young Creed Leader Lu is so terrifying!”

“No, what’s truly terrifying is the Heavenly Court!”

Everyone discussed in hushed tones, growing increasingly alarmed as they gradually approached the truth.

~~~

Ao Ling cupped her fists and bowed to Young Creed Leader Lu. “Senior Brother Lu, there was no need for you to intervene. Your junior sister could have dealt with him.”

Young Creed Leader Lu returned the salute, his genuine smile as warm as a spring breeze. “Junior Sister Little Ling, it’s been three hundred thousand years since we last met. Has everything been well?”

“Thank you for your concern, Senior Brother Lu. Everything is well. It’s just that after slumbering so long, I didn’t expect the world to have forgotten the Heavenly Court and the Underworld.”

~~~

“What is the Underworld?”

The crowd noted the other term that Ao Ling mentioned.

“Never heard of it.”

~~~

“The river of time is long and can erase the memories of all beings. When I first awoke, I also didn’t expect that the Heavenly Court, which once ruled for eons, would have faded from fame.”

Young Creed Leader Lu appeared deeply rueful and shook his head with a wry smile. “The mark left by Shifu was triggered. I thought something had gone wrong there. I didn’t expect you to have truly awakened. My original plan was to awaken you in another ten years. I never thought Lu Yang would beat me to it.

“Never mind. This is an internal matter of your Dragon Tribe after all. It’s not my place to interfere.

“Speaking of which, Lu Yang and I are quite fated. We once sparred and actually fought to a draw.”

“A draw?” Ao Ling was astounded. “Senior Brother, your talent was even praised by Shifu and the Creed Leader, who said your future could rival theirs. Is Lu Yang actually that strong?”

~~~

“Young Creed Leader Lu is the Dragon Ancient Ancestor’s senior brother?”

The crowd remembered that Jiang Lianyi had also addressed Young Creed Leader Lu as “senior brother.”

To think this Young Creed Leader Lu is actually the senior brother of both the Dragon and Phoenix ancient ancestors!

Just this fact alone means he could roam the ancient world unimpeded!

Young Creed Leader Lu spotted the Three Mountains Daoist Priest glaring fixedly at him. The latter was extremely nervous, his muscles tensed, as if he was ready to flee at the slightest sign of trouble.

Young Creed Leader Lu chuckled. “Relax. The matter between you and Junior Sister Little Ling has nothing to do with the Heavenly Court. If I meddle further, I’m afraid Junior Sister Little Ling will get angry with me.

“I came here simply to check on Junior Sister Little Ling’s condition. Since she is fine, I can rest assured. Whether you defeat Little Ling or she defeats you, the Heavenly Court will not intervene. My promise represents the Heavenly Court’s stance.” With that said, Young Creed Leader Lu walked to the side.

Just when everyone thought Young Creed Leader Lu was going to observe from the sidelines, he walked up to Lu Yang.

“Sect Leader Lu, it’s been a long time. I see your cultivation has advanced. Why don’t you and I spar?”

Lu Yang was taken aback. He was sitting here peacefully and avoiding the spotlight, yet the other party had come to him.

Though he didn’t go looking for trouble, he wasn’t afraid of trouble either. He turned to seek the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s opinion with a glance.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord huffed and puffed, almost slamming the table. “Why do you have to ask me? You should let him properly understand the strength of our Dao-Seeking Sect’s prodigy, of course!”

Having obtained the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s consent, Lu Yang heaved a sigh of relief that there were no qualms about him acting boldly.

Nearby, Meng Jingzhou watched coldly as the two people staged an act for three characters, regretting that he hadn’t thought of doing something similar!

Chapter 792: Battle Between Ancient and Present-Day Prodigies!

The ancient youth prodigy and the present-day youth prodigy stood facing each other, both brimming with fighting spirit, their battle intent soaring skyward.

“Sect Leader Lu’s talent is the highest I’ve witnessed in my lifetime. Although the Dao-Seeking Sect has the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, a half-immortal, the pond is ultimately a bit too small to nurture a true dragon.

“My Heavenly Court welcomes all virtuous talents. If you are willing, why not join us? A position as a Holy Son would surely be reserved for you.”

Sect Leader Lu countered, “Oh? Aren’t you afraid I might snatch your position as Young Creed Leader?”

Young Creed Leader Lu laughed out loud. “The strong reigns supreme—that is an unchanging principle since time immemorial. If you can defeat me and lead the Heavenly Court to its former glory, what harm is there in giving you this position of young creed leader?”

The crowd inwardly praised him. As expected of someone who could become the Young Creed Leader, his magnanimity far surpasses that of his peers.

Lu Yang shook his head. “I appreciate your kind offer, Young Creed Leader Lu, but I’m indebted to the Dao-Seeking Sect for nurturing me. If I were to abandon them, that would make me a vile person.”

“Is that so? What a pity then.” Young Creed Leader Lu had sincerely invited Lu Yang to join the Heavenly Court. With Lu Yang becoming part of their ranks, their odds of victory in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era would increase.

It was a shame. The only option left was to fight.

Even the incomparably talented Young Creed Leader Lu dared not hold back against Lu Yang. Seven swords hovered vertically around him, protecting him. The characters such as “Tianshu (Dubhe),” “Tianxuan (Merak),” and “Tianji (Phecda)” engraved on their hilts indicated the swords’ origins.

“That’s the legendary Seven-Star Sword Set!” The Divine Ao-Turtle Tribe Chieftain involuntarily cried out upon recognizing the seven swords.

“What is the Seven-Star Sword Set?” Most had not heard of it.

The Divine Ao-Turtle Tribe Chieftain said solemnly, “In the ancient era, there was a sword cultivator named Liu Ningxuan. He was peerless in both the qin and sword and was the strongest sword cultivator of that era. His talent could rival that of the Sword Tower Supreme Lord in Great Xia.

“My tribe once had an old ancestor who cultivated until the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage. However, even he was slain by Liu Ningxuan with a single slash of the sword!”

The crowd gasped. The Divine Ao-Turtle Tribe was famed for defense. A Divine Ao-Turtle at the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage has undoubtedly formidable defense, yet he was still cut down by Liu Ningxuan?

“Liu Ningxuan was adept as Human and Sword as One. At its peak, a single sword strike would lead to inevitable death for anyone below immortals!

“Everyone thought he could become a half-immortal or even an immortal. Unfortunately, after a certain battle, he vanished. Some say he was trapped in an immortal domain, while others say he died.

“This Seven-Star Sword Set belongs to Liu Ningxuan!”

Lu Yang hadn’t expected the Seven-Star Sword Set to have such a history.

Liu Ningxuan, peerless in both qin and sword—I know him. He’s the one who performed Human and Sword as One too well.

“Immortal Fairy, did you know about this?”

This stumped the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. She tried hard to recall, then shook her head. “I have no impression of that. When that kid fought with this immortal, he had a lot of flashy swords with no substance. I didn’t pay much attention to what they looked like. Anyway, they all looked pretty similar.”

Young Creed Leader Lu smiled, gripping the Tianshu Sword. “Come to think of it, our last fight was at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage. Who would have thought that over a year would pass in the blink of an eye? The two of us have already advanced to the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage.”

Lu Yang didn’t speak, silently drawing the Qingfeng Sword.

Shing—

Sword light shot skyward, slicing through the waters and creating a vacuum in the area.

Two types of true fires attached themselves to the Qingfeng Sword. Sword qi transformed into numerous golden divine birds. The birds flapped their crimson wings, completely unaffected by the East Sea’s waters!

The Tianshu Sword’s brilliant aura carried the arrogance of antiquity, purer and sharper. The other six flying swords were like six jiao-dragons breaking free from a cage, cleaving the golden divine birds in two.

After being split, each golden bird turned into two smaller golden birds, their scorching heat undiminished!

“What true fire is this?”

Even with the East Sea cultivators’ knowledge, they had never seen such a true fire.

“It looks like the Golden Jinwu Crow True Flame, but the problem is, I’ve never heard of a Golden Crow with two legs.”

Even children who had never cultivated had heard of the Three-Legged Golden Crow.

The two fought from the water to the sky, then from the sky to an island, exchanging blows a hundred times. Wherever they passed was reduced to ruins. The combat prowess they displayed left everyone present awestruck.

Is this what Intermediate Nascent Soul cultivators are capable of?

These East Sea dignitaries had been prodigies of their territory when they were young, their cultivation and combat power far surpassing that of their peers. But not a single one of them had reached the level of Lu Yang and Young Creed Leader Lu.

The Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors mentally weighed themselves against the two and felt they could barely achieve such a level.

“Wasn’t Lu Yang said to be a spell cultivator? How is his proficiency in the Sword Dao also this impressive? He’s somewhat able to keep up with Young Creed Leader Lu.” A Fusion old ancestor was puzzled.

In terms of Sword Dao alone, Lu Yang was no match for Young Creed Leader Lu. It was by supplementing with spell attacks that he managed to hold himself against Young Creed Leader Lu.

Another Fusion old ancestor shook his head. “No, he’s not just a spell cultivator. When I was seeking pills in Great Xia, I heard that Lu Yang has a Sword Spirit Root. That’s why the Taciturn Daoist Priest took him as a disciple!”

“He actually has a Sword Spirit Root?!” Those nearby were shocked, their pupils quaking.

Since ancient times, no one had heard of a sword cultivator possessing phenomenal talent in spells.

“Good, good, good! Truly worthy of being the opponent I approve of. To think that you can still fight me on equal footing even after advancing to the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage!” Young Creed Leader Lu laughed heartily. He hadn’t experienced such an exhilarating fight in a long time. Those who could fight him to an impasse were minimally at the Advanced Divine Transfiguration Stage.

The Tianshu Sword left his hand, returning to the Seven-Star Sword Set. Young Creed Leader Lu pointed skyward, and the seven swords formed a great array.

“Sect Leader Lu, try this move!”

Young Creed Leader Lu extended two fingers, gently swaying them. The ringing of the swords reverberated through the air continuously as the Seven-Star Sword Set appeared above Lu Yang’s head, their gleaming tips aimed downward.

“Be careful, Sect Leader Lu. This array is called ‘Immortal Kneels With One Sword.’ Even the Qilin Immortal had to kneel before this sword array!”

Upon hearing this piece of ancient secret, the spectators instantly became restless, unable to control their voices.

“Immortal Kneels With One Sword—what a domineering name for an array!”

“The Qilin Immortal was once defeated by this sword array?!”

“Who created this sword array? I’ve never heard of any ancient immortal skilled in both swords and arrays.”

Everyone discussed fervently. They had read countless ancient and modern texts, yet they hadn’t come across one that recorded this event.

“Right. For the Qilin Immortal, this would be a scandal. How could he allow it to be passed down to later generations?”

“Array, activate!”

As the words left Young Creed Leader Lu’s lips, the sword array activated. It crushed down with overwhelming force and annihilated everything, seemingly capable of destroying heaven and earth.

Thud! Even Lu Yang couldn’t withstand the sword array’s oppressive pressure and knelt on the ground.

He raised his head and stared fixedly at the array, showing no signs of submission as he took out the Sword-Cleansing Pond.

“One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!”

Using sword intent, Lu Yang manifested innumerable Sword-Cleansing Ponds that blotted out the sky. They formed a dark mass, like storm clouds gathering, and seemed to contain the majestic power of heaven and earth.

Just when everyone thought Lu Yang was about to lose, they froze upon witnessing this move from him.

“What move is this?!”

“Didn’t he say it? ‘One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords.’”

“But there are no swords, though.”

“Perhaps Lu Yang’s comprehension of the Sword Dao has reached a realm where ‘the sword is in the heart, and all things can be swords!’ I heard that after Lu Yang came to the East Sea, he defeated over a dozen Divine Transfiguration cultivators by relying on this very move!”

“Yes, yes, yes! I also heard that this move can materialize a sword into human form, which can then manifest three heads and six arms.”

Lu Yang was completely focused, ignoring the commentary from the outside world. He concentrated solely on the battle before him and softly uttered, “Go!”

The Sword-Cleansing Ponds descended like a downpour. The sight of this scene alone was terrifying.

Two torrents of Sword Dao collided, erupting in an unprecedented radiance that shook heaven and earth, boiled the sea of clouds, and shot straight into the nine heavens.

“Who won?”

The Sword-Cleansing Ponds and the Seven-Star Sword Set were scattered across the ground. Both Lu Yang and Young Creed Leader Lu used their swords to prop themselves up, half-kneeling on the ground as they glared at each other. Although their spirit power was totally depleted, their eyes still blazed with fighting spirit.

“Alright, that’s enough. Let’s not fight anymore.” Suddenly, Young Creed Leader Lu chuckled. “If we continue fighting, we’d have to rely on consuming pills. That wouldn’t be fair to you. Let’s end this battle here.”

“Let’s end it here then.” Lu Yang agreed readily. As Young Creed Leader Lu said, continuing the battle would be meaningless, regardless of the outcome.

The two exchanged a glance and smiled, an unspoken sense of mutual admiration passing between them.

A veteran Transcendent Tribulation cultivator saw this and sighed. “True. As peerless prodigies, they rarely meet equals. Encountering an evenly matched opponent is greatly beneficial for their future cultivation.”

Tao Yaoye felt that Lu Yang’s acting was even more convincing than the acting in Dreamlike Bubble Mirages.

Man Gu was astounded after witnessing the entire process, feeling he’d probably never master such acting skills in this lifetime.

Li Haoran thought that if Qin Haoran had possessed Lu Yang’s brains back then, he would probably have led the Nine-Netherworlds Creed to immense wealth long ago.

Meng Jingzhou was considering whether he could finish off both the utterly exhausted Lu Yang and Lu Yang in one go if he suddenly attacked now, usurping the position of young creed leader.

Chapter 793: The Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s Incipient Dao Fruit

Meanwhile, at the main battlefield at the Dragon Palace.

Compared to the battle between Lu Yang and Young Creed Leader Lu, the battle here was at a higher level, drawing even more attention.

“Nine-Tier Demon-Suppressing Pagoda!” The Three Mountains Daoist Priest seized the initiative, producing a pristinely white nine-tiered miniature pagoda.

The East Sea Cultivators Alliance headquarters was a nine-tiered pagoda, but few knew it was actually the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s life-bound magical treasure.

As the Three Mountains Daoist Priest chanted incantations, the pagoda radiated a brilliant light, turning into a dawn-breaking golden ray that shot straight toward Ao Ling.

Ao Ling transformed into a black true dragon that was ten thousand zhang long. Her entire body was covered in shimmering, jet-black scales that glistened with a profound, mysterious luster.

Witnessing the half-immortal battle about to break out, the crowd frantically scrambled to flee the Dragon Palace.

Meng Jingzhou appeared abnormally calm. It’s merely a half-immortal battle. I’ve seen two already.

This isn’t as entertaining as that grandson Lu Yang performing a double act.

“Transform!”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest shouted. The pagoda swelled to the size of a mountain, intending to suppress Ao Ling. With a light flick of her tail, Ao Ling effortlessly overturned it.

The pressure of facing a formidable opponent weighed on the Three Mountains Daoist Priest. Ao Ling hadn’t even activated her Incipient Dao Fruit, simply relying on her physical strength to easily topple his prized life-bound treasure.

Ao Ling then charged with her dragon horns, stirring up a tsunami from the seabed that roared like the wind. The Three Mountains Daoist Priest was so frightened that he hastily shifted the pagoda to shield himself. reewebnovel.com

The dragon horns were the hardest part of Ao Ling’s original form. Even though the pagoda was the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s life-bound magical treasure and had been refined over many years, it still couldn’t withstand Ao Ling’s strike.

Boom!

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest was sent flying alongside the pagoda. Stone pillars collapsed, and an enormous hole appeared in the Dragon Palace’s wall—he had been blasted right out of the Dragon Palace!

Lu Yang and Young Creed Leader Lu seized the chance to slip out through the hole and continued their battle on the sea surface.

“Who do you think will win?”

“Probably the Dragon Ancient Ancestor. I heard she was an absolute powerhouse even during the era where prodigies were as ubiquitous as rain, rarely losing in half-immortal battles.”

“I think so too. And don’t forget, dragons’ physical bodies are innately tough. The Dragon Ancient Ancestor’s physical strength has likely reached a pinnacle. The Three Mountains Daoist Priest definitely won’t dare engage her at melee range.”

“Don’t be so quick to judge. I’ve heard half-immortals aren’t absolutely stronger or weaker; they restrain one another. If the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s Incipient Dao Fruit happens to counter the Dragon Ancient Ancestor, the outcome could be reversed.”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest ignored the crowd’s discussions, silently reciting in his heart. “I hereby wish: Strengthen my physical body, strengthen the pagoda, and grant me the ability to subdue dragons!”

After making the wish, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest felt his entire being undergo a drastic transformation. His physical strength reached the limits of the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, and the pagoda became indestructible and almost indistinguishable from an immortal artifact. The parts damaged earlier were now perfectly repaired. The weaknesses of dragons flashed before his eyes one by one—in his eyes, Ao Ling’s true dragon form was riddled with flaws and openings!

“I recall the Three Mountains Daoist Priest wasn’t known for physical strength. How can he brawl with the Dragon Ancient Ancestor up close?”

The strength of Ao Ling’s physical body was considered the pinnacle, the ultimate goal of all physique cultivators in the world. No one expected the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, who excelled in spells, to attain this realm.

This was the Incipient Dao Fruit the Three Mountains Daoist Priest had obtained through faith power—the Wish-Fulfilling Incipient Dao Fruit. It allowed him to make three wishes using the Incipient Dao Fruit, but the scope of the wishes had to be related to the wishes of his believers. For example, since few believers made wishes regarding the soul, he couldn’t use the Wish-Fulfilling Incipient Dao Fruit to strengthen his soul.

“The Wish-Fulfilling Incipient Dao Fruit? How utterly predictable.” Ao Ling detected the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s change and smirked scornfully. She had seen this type of Incipient Dao Fruit during the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

The biggest issue with this Incipient Dao Fruit was the limitation of wishes. Most wishes were made by mortals, and mortals wouldn’t make outrageous wishes like controlling time and space.

Infuriated by Ao Ling’s derisive laugh, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest activated his dragon-subduing technique. The pagoda immediately emitted dazzling rays. Gray chains shot from its base, rapidly coiling around Ao Ling in an attempt to bind her. Regardless of whether Ao Ling grew larger or smaller, she couldn’t break free.

“Ancient Ancestor, we are here to aid you!”

The Old Dragon Emperor and the other two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators from the Dragon Tribe wanted to step forward to assist Ao Ling. To their surprise, Ao Ling suddenly extended two claws and grabbed the gray chains. With a forceful pull, she ripped the chains apart.

“Alright, alright. Why would I need your help when dealing with a mere half-immortal inflated by faith power?”

If a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator intervened in a half-immortal battle and failed to coordinate well, they could easily become a casualty, causing them to become a hindrance instead.

Accompanied by a dragon roar, the seawater began to boil as if an undersea volcano had erupted. The water throughout the Dragon Palace area churned violently, and even seaweeds ignited.

This was the Dragon Tribe’s life-bound true fire, capable of burning even in water. It was difficult to extinguish, and its searing heat surpassed even the Nirvana True Flame. Otherwise, it wouldn’t have forced Jiang Lianyi out of her Play-Dead Technique state back then.

Of course, that was partly because Jiang Lianyi’s skills weren’t polished then. The current Jiang Lianyi wouldn’t fear the flames.

Dragons were born with the ability to command the wind and rain. Coupled with their life-bound true fire, they could be said to master both yin and yang, proficient in water and fire.

Ao Ling and the Three Mountains Daoist Priest clashed again. The Three Mountains Daoist Priest felt immense pressure from the combat. Ao Ling’s dragon claws seemed impervious to all spells, and any spell could be shattered by her claws.

Worse, he felt each of Ao Ling’s strikes was stronger than the last. Even with the pagoda, he couldn’t withstand the relentless assault.

“You think having a pagoda blocking makes you safe? Utterly naive! Striking Through Mountains!”

Ao Ling applied a subtle force that penetrated the pagoda, striking the Three Mountains Daoist Priest directly in the chest. Instantly, three bloody claw marks appeared on his chest. Blood flowed out, mixing with seawater to form a dense crimson mist.

“I hereby wish: Cease strengthening the pagoda and heal my injuries!”

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s injuries healed at a visible rate.

His recovery was swift, but Ao Ling’s attacks were more swift.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest inwardly cursed. I overestimated myself. I should have just run away. Why did I insist on making those grand statements? Now I can’t win, and running away will be too embarrassing.

He had already tried wishing for the “ability to control the sea,” “ability to command the wind and rain,” “increase luck,” and so on, but none enabled him to become a match for Ao Ling. He even sensed that Ao Ling was gradually growing stronger. At first, he could hold his ground, but later, it became a one-sided rout.

Boom!

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest attempted to flee the battlefield multiple times, only to be yanked back by Ao Ling each time. Finally, his lower body was shredded by dragon claws, and he plummeted into the sea, stirring humongous waves.

Ao Ling assumed human form and stepped on the Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s face, her expression cold.

The outcome was finalized.

“If I say I just wanted to take over the body for fun and planned to give the body back afterward, would you believe me?”

Ao Ling sneered repeatedly. “Why don’t you guess?”

Seeing that Ao Ling had no intention of letting him go, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest hollered at the top of his lungs. “If you don’t help me now, I’m going to be beaten to death!”

After a moment of deathly silence, an aged, dark-faced elder appeared.

If possible, he naturally didn’t wish to intervene. The original plan hadn’t involved fighting a legendary figure like Ao Ling, much less the appearance of Young Creed Leader Lu. This signified the Heavenly Court had noticed this place.

Although he was confident he could defeat Ao Ling, he knew he stood no chance against the Heavenly Court. That Young Creed Leader Lu had glanced toward my hiding spot and likely detected me. Escaping is useless now.

Young Creed Leader Lu was in the middle of performing his double act when he glanced at the dark-faced elder who had abruptly appeared. It was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy who had informed him that another half-immortal was hiding in the Dragon Palace, probably the Three Mountain Daoist Priest’s ally.

Lu Yang surmised that this person was a half-immortal from Great Qian, and that the method the Three Mountain Daoist Priest employed to condense his Incipient Dao Fruit through faith power had originated from him.

Chapter 794: Ao Ling’s Strength

Faith and the Divine Dao built the foundation of the Great Qian Dynasty. Lu Yang deduced that there might be some connection between the Great Qian and the Ember Legacy dynasties.

Otherwise, how could it be so coincidental that two successive great dynasties were both related to faith?

“Greetings, Fellow Daoist Ao Ling. I am Great Qian’s Mountain-River Lord—” Before the dark-faced elder could finish, he was abruptly sent flying by a kick from Ao Ling.

You’re an accomplice of the Three Mountains Daoist Priest. How could you be a good person?

I don’t care what nonsense you say. I’ll just beat you up first. Explanations can come later!

“Fine, fine! Fellow Daoist Ao Ling, since you’re unwilling to give me face, don’t blame me for being impolite!” The Mountain-River Lord had assumed that an ancient legendary figure like Ao Ling would be someone of decorum. He never expected her to not play by the book and beat him right from the outset.

You want to fight? Then I’ll fight you!

He had given the Three Mountains Daoist Priest an incomplete faith cultivation method, hinting to the latter that he could take over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body. His aim was to use the Three Mountains Daoist Priest to obtain the incense offerings dedicated to the Great Venerable Dragon Mandate. He never expected matters to develop to this point.

“He said he’s the Mountain-River Lord? That grand general who campaigned across all eight directions for the Great Qian Dynasty?”

“After the campaign ended, the first Qian Emperor conferred him as the Mountain-River Lord to eternally enjoy the incense offerings of the mountains and rivers!”

A Transcendent Tribulation old ancestor who heard the dark-faced elder’s title was visibly moved. This was a figure akin to a war god of the Great Qian Dynasty, one who wielded command over the military forces, excelled in warfare, and was victorious in all his battles.

The Mountain-River Lord swung his arm, and a white-bone spear appeared in his hand.

Ao Ling transformed into her true dragon form once more, her body wreathed in purple-gold dragon flames and lightning. The spirit energy of the entire sea region grew turbulent, erupting in a deafening roar that shook heaven and earth.

The Mountain-River Lord’s figure did not waver in the slightest from the impact. With a twist of his body, his spear shot forth like a stunning swan, thrusting toward Ao Ling with lightning speed.

A sense of danger twirled around Ao Ling’s mind. She violently twisted her dragon form, evading the spear tip.

The space where she had been just a moment ago had turned into nothingness, and seawater rushed in to fill the void.

“Be careful, Ancient Ancestor! According to records, the Mountain-River Lord wields the Devouring Incipient Dao Fruit!” Ao Ya anxiously transmitted an auditory message. Historical accounts recorded that those who fought the Mountain-River Lord were often reduced to a fate where not even their bones remained, completely devoured.

“Devouring Incipient Dao Fruit?” Ao Ling narrowed her eyes. This is indeed a little troublesome.

Her dragon head tilted, dodging an attack from a streak of light.

It was the Three Mountains Daoist Priest!

Taking advantage of Ao Ling and the Mountain-River Lord’s brief clash, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest had used all his wishes on his recovery. In the blink of an eye, his injuries healed, and even his depleted spirit energy was restored in full.

“I’m here to aid you!”

It was now two half-immortals against Ao Ling!

The Nine-Tier Demon-Suppressing Pagoda and the white-bone spear were unleashed simultaneously.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest continued wishing. “Strengthen my physical body, strengthen my pagoda, and grant me the power to overturn mountains and seas.”

The Mountain-River Lord brandished his white-bone spear and donned an armor tempered by incense worship, as if he had returned to his glorious days of campaigning across the lands three hundred thousand years ago. Although he was old now, his battle prowess remained at its zenith.

With three half-immortals attacking, the entire Dragon Palace sea area became unstable and tumultuous. Onlookers watched from afar as darkness enveloped the skies above the Dragon Palace. Three figures clashed fiercely, their every move capable of altering heaven and earth.

“Third Chan Heavenly Wind!”

Ao Ling summoned the wind and rain, stirring up boundless hurricanes over the East Sea. This terrifying wind specifically targeted souls and brimmed with yang energy. It could blow the souls out of their bodies, causing them to dissolve within the gusts of wind silently.

“Under the Bodhi Tree, boundless wondrous methods!” The Three Mountains Daoist Priest had secretly studied a Buddhist method to stabilize the heart and mind. It could anchor the soul within the body, preventing it from being affected by external influences.

However, all he could achieve was merely maintaining his sense of self within the wind; he was unable to retaliate.

On the other hand, the Mountain-River Lord’s soul had been tempered and stabilized, unafraid of the Third Chan Heavenly Wind.

“World-Ending Crimson Lotus!”

A crimson lotus exuding the power of karmic fire appeared above the East Sea. The black clouds were stained a blood-red, as if heralding the arrival of doomsday.

“Innate Ren Water.”[1]

Ao Ling stood upon the crest of a wave. Every drop of seawater beneath her feet could transform into vast oceans and lakes. Innate Ren Water was formed by mixing three types of Innate Divine Water from the sun, moon, and stars. In this age where stars were absent, it had long since vanished without a trace.

Light from fire and water interwove like the collision of two worlds, forming a bizarre and kaleidoscopic tapestry of light and shadow. The Innate Ren Water overwhelmed the World-Ending Crimson Lotus and pressed down to crush the Mountain-River Lord.

The Mountain-River Lord remained unperturbed, allowing the Innate Ren Water to surge toward him. Before the Ren Water could even touch him, it was completely devoured by his Devouring Incipient Dao Fruit, not a single drop of seawater reaching him.

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest chanted inwardly. “I make a wish upon this place: This is my Dao field, gathering the power of Pengshan Mountain, Fangzhang Mountain, and Yingzhou Mountain!”

This required the use of three wishes, leaving him utterly vulnerable during the process. That was why he hadn’t dared to make such wishes when fighting Ao Ling one-on-one earlier. Now, with the Mountain-River Lord keeping Ao Ling occupied in battle, he finished charging up the power in one go.

“Three Mountains Suppress Demons!” This was the reason for his Daoist title “Three Mountains.” He could mobilize the power of the East Sea’s three mountains!

Three mountain apparitions appeared. Although they were phantom images, they were not at all inferior to the actual mountains descending. These apparitions contained the spirit vein power of those three mountains!

Penglai Island had a ninth-grade spirit vein, while Yingzhou Island had an eighth-grade spirit vein, but after the Great Void Immortal Grass was removed, it was restored to the ninth-grade.

As the three mountains descended, they suppressed all foes.

Ao Ling was struck consecutively by the three mountains, coughing up blood. The Mountain-River Lord pressed his advantage, clinging to her like gangrene to bones. Gripping his spear, he leveraged the momentum to leap, deftly maneuvering across the dragon’s body. His spear tip manifested the power of the Devouring Incipient Dao Fruit, and crimson dragon blood rained down, staining the night sky.

The three immortal mountains rose and fell, stirring up waves ten thousand zhang high and a bloody mist. Ao Ling’s black dragon form was battered until it dripped with blood.

“Kill!” The Mountain-River Lord’s eyes reddened with bloodlust. This was an old habit of his—once he struck, it would be a fight to the death. It was how he had carved out his fearsome reputation across the world during the Great Qian era.

~~~

“Immortal Fairy, is Senior Ao Ling really alright?” Lu Yang’s eyelid twitched as he witnessed this scene. It looks like she is about to lose.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wore an intrigued smile, looking like she was enjoying the show. “Do you actually think that Little Ling is at a disadvantage?”

“Is she not?” Lu Yang thought, Can Senior Ao Ling still turn the tables despite being beaten to such a state?

“Hehe, have you forgotten her Incipient Dao Fruit?”

Lu Yang suddenly remembered that Ao Ling possessed the Natural Selection Incipient Dao Fruit!

~~~

While the Young Creed Leader and the Heavenly Court Ruler were talking, the scales of victory began to shift.

It was unclear whether it was an illusion, but the Three Mountains Daoist Priest couldn’t help but feel that Ao Ling’s aura wasn’t weakening despite her severe injuries; on the contrary, it seemed to be intensifying.

“Power of Three Mountains!”

The three mountains pressed down on Ao Ling, rendering her immobile. Only then did the Three Mountains Daoist Priest feel slightly reassured.

Suddenly, Ao Ling seemed to have been infused with new strength, arching her dragon spine and tossing away the three mountains crushing her!

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest’s eyes widened. Isn’t Ao Ling gravely injured? How does she still possess such strength?!

A hint of a smile flickered in her huge dragon eyes, reflecting the astonished and bewildered expressions of the two half-immortals.

“Are you done attacking?”

The black dragon flipped over, her body emanating a sacred radiance as her injuries healed at a rapid rate.
