“This is impossible!” The Mountain-River Lord cried out involuntarily. Most of Ao Ling’s wounds were sustained from being devoured by my Incipient Dao Fruit. This kind of devouring occurs at the soul level—it isn’t something that can be easily repaired!

Ao Ling paid him no heed. An enormous dragon claw descended, seeking to suppress both of them beneath it.

“If you’re done attacking, then it’s my turn!”

“Oh no! Devouring Vortex!” The Mountain-River Lord activated his Incipient Dao Fruit, attempting to devour Ao Ling’s dragon claw.

However, the colossal claw simply shattered the Devouring Vortex and suppressed the two half-immortals with undiminished momentum.

The Mountain-River Lord crossed his white-bone spear before his chest, but it was still ripped to pieces by the dragon claw. This spear had accompanied him through countless half-immortals and had never suffered significant damage. Who would have thought it would be so easily broken by a dragon claw?

“This is an immortal’s body!”

The Mountain-River Lord wore an expression of utter disbelief. The dragon claw’s ability to crush the devouring vortex and shatter the bone spear wasn’t due to any technique but pure, overwhelming physical dominance!

Ao Ling possessed the Natural Selection Incipient Dao Fruit. As long as she survived an attack, she would grow stronger. In other words, the longer the fight dragged on, the stronger she would become! But since they were all half-immortals, how could anyone defeat her right from the start?

The Three Mountains Daoist Priest could strengthen his body to the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

But Ao Ling could break through the limits of the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and attain an immortal’s body!

If Ao Ling could elevate to an immortal’s body, even the Qilin Immortal in his half-immortal days would have been unable to defeat her!

1. Ren water represents yang water and is symbolized by expansive bodies of water. ☜

Chapter 795: Those in the Know Must Die

An insurmountable chasm lay between a half-immortal and a true immortal. This was not merely reflected in the completeness and perfection of the Dao Fruit. Possessing either an immortal body or immortal soul alone was enough to crush a half-immortal utterly.

“Get off me!” The Mountain-River Lord’s essence blood burned as he struggled to break free from the dragon claw pinning him. With a shout, he unleashed Heaven-Earth Dharma Manifestation.

“I hereby wish: Let the three mountains become one!”

The three mountains merged into a single pitch-black immortal mountain with the power of restriction. Anyone who approached this dark mountain would be unable to employ spells or divine abilities, and their physical bodies would be severely weakened.

A young divine individual shouldering the black immortal mountain stood tall between heaven and earth. Despite the East Sea’s depth of two hundred thousand meters, this youthful divine individual’s feet rested on the seabed, while his head extended beyond the ocean’s surface.

This was the Mountain-River Lord’s appearance in his youth.

Space collapsed around the dharma body, and even the waters of the East Sea could not approach, forming a vacuum zone where everything was devoured.

Ao Ling sneered, her gaze full of contempt. Although she appeared as minuscule as dust before the youthful divine being, the aura she radiated far surpassed that of his.

Charging with her dragon horns, she closed in on the youthful divine being. Even the Incipient Dao Fruit couldn’t devour her dragon scales.

The youthful divine being hefted the black immortal mountain and brought it crashing down upon the terrifying black dragon.

Ao Ling remained unruffled. As if she was piercing a mere pane of window paper, she effortlessly tore through the immortal mountain, then bored into the youthful divine being’s glabella, bursting out from the back of his skull and penetrating his spirit platform.

“Gah—!” The technique fueled by burning essence blood was broken. The Mountain-River Lord and the Three Mountains Daoist Lord suffered a backlash, vomiting large mouthfuls of blood as their auras rapidly plummeted.

The spectators were completely taken aback. The Dragon Ancient Ancestor, who had seemingly been at a disadvantage, easily turned the tide and suppressed two half-immortals. This was a victory of absolute domination.

The majestic black dragon returned triumphant, like a sovereign returning from a crushing victory over foreign tribes. Its overwhelming aura made heaven and earth hold their breath.

Despite facing two opponents alone, she captured both half-immortals alive—a result no one had anticipated!

Meanwhile, the battle between Lu Yang and Young Creed Leader Lu was drawing to a close, ending in a tie.

“See? I told you Little Ling could win,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said with a proud smile. After all, she is my unofficial disciple.

“Congratulations on your grand victory, Senior Ao Ling!” The East Sea crowd was practically showing as they bowed in unison, causing the sea surface to shake.

Unlike the previous bow given out of respect for her seniority and legendary status, this time, it was a bow of genuine submission born from witnessing Ao Ling’s combat prowess.

The Dragon Tribe was the most thrilled. Their Ancient Ancestor had displayed her divine might and an unbeatable bearing, filling them with pride.

Ao Ling’s dragon claw pressed down on the two half-immortals, her icy dragon pupils fixed intently upon them.

“Move aside!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly transmitted an auditory message to Ao Ling.

Something unexpected occurred. Ao Ling felt a chill run down her spine, as if she had been plunged into an ice cellar. It seemed as though some great terror was unfolding. She didn’t even bother with the Mountain-River Lord and the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, hastily shifting away from her position.

A saber light imbued with an aura of finality and death descended from the sky. Without even a chance to scream, the Mountain-River Lord and the Three Mountains Daoist Priest were bisected by this sudden attack, their physical body and souls utterly annihilated. Not a trace of them remained in the world!

Ao Ling inhaled sharply. Had she not dodged, she would have been grievously wounded even if she survived.

“It’s quite unexpected that you managed to evade this esteemed one’s casual strike.” A deep voice reverberated between heaven and earth, carrying an aura so heavy like one had reached the end of the world.

Be it seafolk or humans, their spirit platforms seemed to be shrouded in dust, the pressure making it hard for them to breathe. Even the earlier battle between the three half-immortals had not given them this feeling.

No, there was simply no comparison between the two!

A murky figure streaked across the horizon, appearing above the East Sea. An aura of death permeated every inch of space. Under its influence, the East Sea froze into ice.

The figure was obscured by dense mist, his features indiscernible.

An immortal!

Never in their wildest dreams had the East Sea crowd imagined that an immortal would suddenly make an entrance, much less one who bore killing intent toward Ao Ling.

“I thought your soul was shattered and you had long since died. This esteemed one didn’t expect you to be still alive. Never mind, since I could kill you once, I can kill you a second time.”

The murky figure’s tone was placid, as if he was speaking about a trivial matter, casually dictating the life and death of a half-immortal.

Lu Yang felt his blood run cold. This murky figure is the immortal who once battled the Qilin Immortal and shattered Ao Ling’s immortal soul!

Moreover, he is likely the one who has been deliberately erasing the existence of the Ember Legacy Dynasty!

“Oh, right, and you. Since you know this esteemed one’s identity, you must also die.” The murky figure glanced sidelong at Lu Yang. He flicked a finger, and a black lightning bolt shot forth.

Lu Yang was stupefied. Who are you? What have I done to know your identity?

“How dare you!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord blazed with fury, positioning himself in front of Lu Yang and activating the Space Incipient Dao Fruit to divert the black lightning.

“Cough—!” The energy contained within the black lightning bolt was so terrifying that even space was affected. The Vast Sea Daoist Lord could barely redirect the attack. Forcefully activating his Incipient Dao Fruit caused him to cough up a mouthful of clotted blood.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s eyelid twitched. Recalling his high spirits when he just arrived in the East Sea, he felt like slapping himself twice.

Teach you to claim you’d protect this kid Lu Yang!

A half-immortal battle is still fine—that’s within my capabilities.

But how did an immortal just pop out of nowhere? Who the hell can protect against that?

The murky figure hadn’t expected the Vast Sea Daoist Lord to deflect his attack. He expressed slight surprise before quickly figuring out the reason. “So it’s the Space Incipient Dao Fruit. Somewhat interesting. Pity it’s only somewhat interesting. Ultimately, you are a mere mortal, incapable of defying an immortal.” He didn’t bother about the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s actions.

“Founding Ancestor, are you alright?” Lu Yang asked gingerly.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord rolled his eyes. “Not really. But I said I would protect you, so I definitely will protect you!”

Lu Yang was utterly astonished. To think the Founding Ancestor is still saying he can protect me even in such a situation! Just what kind of trump card could that be?

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord stealthily slipped a hand into the front of his robe and tore a talisman.

A spatial channel opened, and a graceful figure emerged. Her countenance was impassive, devoid of joy and arrow, as if nothing could shake her Dao heart.

Everyone held their breath, their bodies trembling uncontrollably.

That graceful figure had displayed her immense divine might in Chunjiang City and hadn’t concealed her appearance. Every high-level cultivator possessed a portrait of her.

The graceful figure’s gaze swept across the surroundings, passing over Lu Yang, Young Creed Leader Lu, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, and Ao Ling, before finally resting upon the murky figure in the sky.

The murky figure furrowed his brows. He seldom paid attention to the affairs of the outside world and had never seen this graceful figure before. But sensing her composed demeanor and her aura that was concealed to resemble a mortal’s, he knew this graceful figure was like himself—an immortal.

Looks like she’s an immortal from later generations.

Nothing to fear.

When I want to kill someone, no one can stop me!

The murky immortal ignored Yun Zhi and activated his Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit, launching a bolt of Silent Annihilation Immortal Lightning as thick as a bucket toward Lu Yang and Young Creed Leader Lu.

Yun Zhi took a light step forward and extended a jade-white hand, revealing a section of her fair wrist. Without so much as a glance, she casually caught the Silent Annihilation Immortal Lightning, seemingly unaffected by its Silent Annihilation intent, and flung it back at the murky immortal.

An immortal naturally wouldn’t be harmed by their own attacks. However, when he caught the returned Immortal Lightning with confidence, he let out a muffled grunt.

Caught off guard, he got wounded by Yun Zhi!

He could sense that another power was intermingled within the returned Immortal Lightning.

How many hundreds of thousands of years has it been since I was last injured?

“Who are you?!” The murky immortal no longer looked down on Yun Zhi, treating her as an immortal of equal standing to himself and engaging with her seriously.

“Yun Mengmeng, Creed Leader of the Heavenly Court Creed,” Yun Zhi introduced herself insipidly.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord secretly breathed a sigh of relief. Fortunately, Yun Zhi was worried and told him to give her a spatial talisman. If something went wrong, he could tear the talisman, and she would rush over immediately.

“Hmm?”

The murky immortal was dumbfounded. Since when did a “Heavenly Court Creed” pop up?

Chapter 796: The Gray-Mist Immortal

“Who are you?” Yun Zhi observed her opponent and sighed inwardly.

My premonition is indeed correct. Little Junior Brother truly has a knack for attracting unexpected prominent figures.

Although I don’t know what happened, since the Dragon Tribe’s Ancient Ancestor is here, it’s likely linked to Little Junior Brother. The same probably applies to this murky gray-mist immortal before me.

Fortunately, before leaving, I’d told the Founding Ancestor to seek me out if he ran into any problem he couldn’t deal with.

My premonition has come true.

The murky immortal seldom moved about in the outside world. The only ones who could draw his attention were ancient immortals like the Heaven Mandate Immortal and fishes that slipped through the net like Ao Ling.

Now there is one more called Lu Yang. It was likely Ao Ling who informed him.

A half-immortal and a Nascent Soul cultivator—I thought I’d have them in the bag. I didn’t expect a female cultivator with remarkable cultivation to suddenly pop up, claiming herself to be the Creed Leader of the Heavenly Court Creed.

What is the Heavenly Court Creed?

Didn’t I destroy the Ember Legacy Dynasty? How could anyone still know of the Heavenly Court?

And if they know of the Heavenly Court, how could they not know of my existence?

Within the gray mist, the immortal frowned. I don’t sense any karmic connection with this Heavenly Court Creed Leader.

The gray-mist immortal had no intention of answering Yun Zhi’s question. All he wanted now was to kill Lu Yang and Ao Ling. As for this self-proclaimed Heavenly Court Creed Leader, there’s nothing to fear. Not to mention, I stand above immortals like the Heaven Mandate Immortal; I am the undisputed number one of the Immortal Dao!

“Die!”

The gray-mist immortal struck brazenly. Space collapsed as an aura of annihilation intensified, condensing into a light of a heavenly saber representing death and finality. The Silent Annihilation Immortal Lightning coiled around this Heavenly Saber Light as it slashed violently toward Ao Ling.

The Heavenly Saber Light annihilated everything it touched, reducing all to nothingness. It was far beyond anything a mere Devouring Dao Fruit could compare to. Let alone Ao Ling, who merely had an immortal’s body, even a true immortal wouldn’t dare to bear the brunt of this attack directly.

As if she possessed foreknowledge, Yun Zhi took a step forward, appearing before Ao Ling in advance. She gently thrust out a palm, stirring ripples in space.

The spatial ripples clashed with the Heavenly Saber Light. At the same time, Yun Zhi’s gaze met the gray-mist immortal’s, setting off a silent shockwave that seemed poised to sweep through and flatten the entire East Sea.

The East Sea quaked like mountains roaring and oceans howling. Living beings at the far borders of the East Sea didn’t know what was happening but felt an inexplicable panic, as if a great calamity was imminent.

The birthday banquet attendees shuddered with fear. A battle between immortals was something that had only occurred in ancient times. To think it’d be reenacted here!

Even Meng Jingzhou, who had weathered through countless storms by following Lu Yang, got a huge fright. I didn’t expect events to escalate to the point where Big Senior Sister has to fight with an immortal.

The one who felt the most complicated was undoubtedly the Old Dragon Emperor.

It’s my nine-thousandth birthday today, but... First, the Three Mountains Daoist Priest had tried to take over my body, then Ancient Ancestor Ao Ling appeared, followed by the Great Qian half-immortal making an entrance, leading to a battle between the three half-immortals, and now, it has escalated into a battle between immortals.

Even if a birthday should have surprises, there is no need for so many layers of surprises. I’m old and can’t take it.

“It seems you are unwilling to yield?” The gray-mist immortal sneered. If you continue blocking me like this, I wouldn’t mind killing you as well!

As he spoke, the power of the Heavenly Saber Light in the gray-mist immortal’s hand increased by another thirty percent.

Yun Zhi softly uttered four words like a lofty immortal fairy aloof from worldly affairs. “Inverting Yin and Yang.”

The Heavenly Saber Light that originally carried annihilation intent suddenly brimmed with vitality. It emitted a soft radiance and was devoid of any offensive intent.

A rock bathed in this gentle light grew a layer of moss in the blink of an eye.

A school of fish shrouded by this soft glow aged at an incredible rate.

Unlike the “Inverting Yin and Yang” that Lu Yang had learned, this was a bona fide divine ability. It was capable of transforming the exceedingly destructive Heavenly Saber Light into a power of creation.

“What’s your relationship with the Nine-Layers Immortal?!” The gray-mist immortal was stupefied. He had seen the Nine-Layers Immortal employ this move.

“None. That was simply an ordinary spell attack,” Yun Zhi replied in a placid tone, as if she had just performed a minor task.

“Heaven above and heaven below, only I reign supreme!” The gray-mist immortal pointed one hand to the sky and the other to the earth, uttering an incantation. “This world shall be annihilated!”

Raging flames suddenly erupted from another part of the sky. The red fire clouds were like gates to the underworld opening, and a blazing rain of fire descended from the heavens. Wherever it touched, all things turned to ash. The night sky was illuminated by the firelight, bright as day yet more bleak than day.

Three hundred years ago, it was with this move that the gray-mist immortal had brought about the downfall of the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

Let’s see how this Creed Leader Yun handles this!

A Fusion old ancestor was dumbfounded, murmuring to himself, “Heavenly fire descends upon the world—this is the Three Calamities Fire from the Buddhist legend, said to bring the world to its end.”

Other Fusion old ancestors wore expressions of despair. Even with their cultivation, the slightest bit of contact with the water would cause them to die in the blazing inferno, burned to charcoal. If this rain of fire fell, the entire East Sea would be plunged into a conflagration capable of boiling its waters dry!

“Returning Wind and Fire.” As if she was oblivious to the terror of the heavenly fire, Yun Zhi gently uttered another four words, her hand gestures shifting to form a cryptic seal.

The heavenly fire vanished as if it had never appeared. The crowd wore blank looks of confusion, seeming to have forgotten what had just transpired.

Only Lu Yang had witnessed the entire process with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s aid.

After Yun Zhi uttered “Returning Wind and Fire,” the heavenly fire about to touch the sea surface retreated into the sky, while the ancestors fleeing in a panic reversed their movements backward to their original positions.

It was like an old film being rewound in Lu Yang’s previous lifetime, the scenes playing backward to the starting point.

Returning Wind and Fire was a temporal divine ability.

“You do have a bit of substance!” After witnessing Yun Zhi’s methods, the gray-mist immortal was still overflowing with confidence, thinking Yun Zhi was nothing special. freewebnovel.com

Yun Zhi couldn’t be bothered to speak. With each step, a golden lotus bloomed in the air. The light of these golden lotuses pierced through the overcast skies full of dark clouds.

Yun Zhi delivered a punch just by turning her hand over, and a crack could be heard. Before the gray-mist immortal’s stupefied eyes, the fist closed in from afar, filling his vision.

Bang!

Yun Zhi’s fist hammered into the gray-mist immortal’s face!

The speed of the punch was so fast that the gray-mist immortal had no time to react.

Yun Zhi continued dishing out a series of consecutive punches, all aimed at the face. She wanted to know what the gray-mist immortal actually looked like.

The gray-mist immortal finally understood the gulf between himself and Yun Zhi. These fists carried immense force, as if they encompassed the power of the stars in the sky. Each punch felt like the universe crashing down upon him, causing him unbearable agony.

He began to consider retreating. If this goes on, forget about killing Lu Yang and Ao Ling, even my life will be at risk!

Under the relentless barrage of attacks, the gray mist became extremely unstable, showing signs of dispersing at any moment, no longer able to protect the gray-mist immortal.

Finally, with another heavy punch from Yun Zhi, the gray mist protecting his face dissipated, revealing the gray-mist immortal’s appearance.

Lu Yang was standing below and borrowing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal consciousness to watch the battle when he froze.

He felt a rare sense of absurdity and fear.

This face was none other than the Everlasting Immortal Fairy!

Chapter 797: What Exactly Did You Four Ancient Immortals Resurrect?

“Ah? Why does this person look exactly like this immortal?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was also stunned, utterly bewildered.

Staring at that familiar peerlessly beautiful face, Lu Yang looked up at the sky, his face contorting into a helpless, bitter smile.

What exactly did you Four Ancient Immortals resurrect?

Back when Ao Ling stated the goal of founding the Ember Legacy Dynasty was to revive the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang had formed a rough conjecture.

Since the four immortals established the Ember Legacy Dynasty with great fanfare and spent a hundred thousand years on it, it must have stirred at least a ripple. Taking the Three Mountains Daoist Priest as an example, how many half-immortals could be produced in a hundred thousand years?

If there was a result, what could it be?

According to Ao Ling, the purpose of establishing the Underworld was to replicate the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Dao Fruit. That definitely did not succeed; otherwise, it wouldn’t have fallen to him to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

He then connected it to the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit that belonged to the immortal who fought the Qilin Immortal. It was the very Dao Fruit the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had once attempted to condense. Furthermore, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had mentioned that the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit was exceedingly difficult to condense, and that no one in the ancient era had succeeded.

Therefore, the possibility of an immortal suddenly emerging from the Ember Legacy Dynasty and attaining the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit wasn’t high. It was likely that the Underworld had condensed the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit through a twist of fate. In fact, the objective of establishing the Heavenly Court was to create an immortal’s body using the power of faith.

In that case, that immortal body would undoubtedly be a spitting image of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

In other words, if establishing the Ember Legacy Dynasty had a result, it was highly likely the birth of an immortal bearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s appearance, their Dao Fruit being the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit.

The gray-mist immortal, or rather, Hui (gray) Doudou, had corroborated Lu Yang’s conjecture with her actions.

Lu Yang had guessed accurately enough, which was why Hui Doudou wanted to kill him.

The latter’s action also allowed Lu Yang to figure out another matter.

Hui Doudou’s aim in erasing the Ember Legacy Dynasty wasn’t to make the dynasty vanish but to prevent the world from knowing of her existence. After all, Hui Doudou was the Heavenly Court’s ruler during the Ember Legacy Dynasty, and everyone then knew of her.

However, Lu Yang still couldn’t make sense of what Hui Doudou was after.

“Could she be controlled by faith power like the Three Mountains Daoist Priest, so she wants to snuff out the source of that faith power?” Lu Yang deduced a reasonable theory.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “Not sure. But it’s possible. If the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others are still alive, they and Little Ling would be the only sources of faith power remaining.

“Their cultivation realms are sufficiently high, and they wield immense influence. There’s indeed a possibility that she’s killing to free herself from such shackles. But why kill you?”

Lu Yang felt she made a valid point. He didn’t believe in Hui Doudou.

I can’t possibly believe in her just because I know of her existence. This thinking would mean Hui Doudou is far too narcissistic.

After all, I have the bona fide Heavenly Court Ruler, Huang Doudou, inside me.

Wait, judging from Hui Doudou’s previous behavior, it resembles the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s personality. She might actually be narcissistic.

Besides, from Hui Doudou’s perspective, my cultivation is merely at the Nascent Soul Stage. It’s possible for a Nascent Soul cultivator to believe in an immortal as an object of faith.

However, Lu Yang still couldn’t help but feel something was off.

For instance, Hui Doudou had said to me, “Since you know this esteemed one’s identity, you must die.”

How did she know I’d guessed her identity? Could she sense it?

Lu Yang tossed the question to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, hoping for an answer, but it only resulted in two faces staring blankly at each other.

“Oh, right, you don’t believe in her. How did she detect you?”

Lu Yang nodded. As I thought, I can’t count on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. It’s best to use my brain more.

Seeing the gray-mist immortal’s face, Ao Ling felt a sense of absurdity, just like Lu Yang.

No wonder Hubby couldn’t defeat this gray-mist immortal.

Hui Doudou was unwilling to let the world learn of her. The gray mist quickly enveloped her face once more, restoring her mysterious aura.

“Did any of you clearly see that immortal’s face?” The Black Feather Venerable Lord was most curious about this. Unfortunately, asking around yielded the same reply—no one had seen clearly.

Everything had happened too fast, beyond the reaction speed of Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Only Yun Zhi, Lu Yang, who borrowed immortal consciousness to watch the battle, and Ao Ling, who temporarily possessed an immortal’s vision, had seen Hui Doudou’s appearance.

Even the Vast Sea Daoist Lord hadn’t seen Hui Doudou’s face properly.

“Falling Cloud Palm.”

Yun Zhi’s fist turned into a palm, resembling a white cloud. It was ever-changing and contained a wondrous power. A single palm strike made Hui Doudou vomit blood, all of it splattering within the mist.

Hui Doudou’s visage was one of incredulity. I am the almighty number one of the Immortal Dao. Since the ancient era, I’ve never met a rival, and even the Nine-Layers Immortal and the others weren’t my match. How could I be so beaten so badly?

“Immortal Dao Killing Fist!” Hui Doudou possessed her own set of fist techniques. When her fists struck, they were unparalleled, causing heaven and earth to change color. The power encompassed within the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit surged like a raging river, vast and boundless. An intangible pressure as heavy as mountains pressed down, causing the air to solidify.

She had once used this fist technique to make the Nine-Layers Immortal vomit blood!

Yun Zhi remained unruffled, striking out with another palm.

Fist and palm collided. In an instant, the spirit energy in the sea region above the Dragon Palace began to boil, triggering a spirit energy explosion. The spirit energy of the spectating cultivators also grew restless, forcing them to sit down cross-legged on the spot and meditate to regulate their chaotic spirit energy and meridians.

Boom!

A figure was sent flying backward from the spirit energy explosion. It was Hui Doudou, and she coughed up blood incessantly.

Seeing that she had put distance between herself and Yun Zhi, Hui Doudou seized the opportunity to flee.

Her attacks had been neutralized one after another by Yun Zhi, and she couldn’t defeat the latter in close combat either; even her true appearance had been seen. Accepting that she couldn’t kill her targets, she decided that escaping was the best option.

Anyway, she hadn’t planned on defeating Yun Zhi. Unleashing the Immortal Dao Killing Fist was merely to create a chance to run away.

If I don’t flee now, I’ll lose my life in the East Sea!

Where exactly did this Heavenly Court Creed come from? And who is this Heavenly Court Creed Leader, Yun Mengmeng?!

But how could Yun Zhi easily let Hui Doudou off? She employed “Flying Body Veiled Traces,” a mighty ability more advanced than Shrinking Earth To Inches. It allowed one to hide between heaven and earth while performing spatial leaps.

Hui Doudou used her immortal consciousness and detected Yun Zhi close on her heels. Her face distorted malevolently, and she steeled her resolve.

“Heavenly Court Creed Leader, you forced my hand!

“Heavenly Devil Dissolution Great Spell!”

“Five-Elements Great Escape!”

At the cost of grievous injury, Hui Doudou performed the Heavenly Devil Dissolution Great Spell. For caution’s sake, she also made use of a five-elements escape technique, transforming into one of the five elements and merging with the world to flee to a distant place.

“Returning Wind and Fire.” Yun Zhi reversed time once again, returning to the moment before Hui Doudou had executed the Heavenly Devil Dissolution Great Spell.

Hui Doudou refused to give up, performing the Heavenly Devil Dissolution Great Spell once more. Unfortunately, it was still futile.

Time reversed again.

Hui Doudou gritted her teeth, activating the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit. “Destroy the concept of ‘time!’”

She could temporarily destroy a specific concept. By destroying the concept of time, the time-reversal spell would be nullified.

“Heavenly Devil Dissolution Great Spell! Five-Elements Great Escape!”

Only then did she finally escape Yun Zhi’s grasp.

She felt no relief, only humiliation. I’m the almighty Heavenly Court Ruler, yet I was chased all over by the Heavenly Court Creed Leader.

In terms of position, the Heavenly Court Creed Leader should be subordinate to the Heavenly Court Ruler!

Chapter 798: Vast Sea Daoist Lord: What Exactly Did I Come to the East Sea For?

Watching the two immortals vanish from sight one after another, the East Sea crowd collectively let out a long sigh of relief.

It’s good that they’re gone, good that they’re gone. The pressure from the immortal battle was too immense; even the aftershocks could have shattered them to dust.

The gulf between immortals and mortals was apparent.

“This is probably the first time an immortal battle has occurred since ancient times, right?” Even the Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors felt relieved at having survived a calamity. Beyond that relief, they recognized the historical significance of this battle.

What kind of cursed luck is this? This is an event that hasn’t happened in three hundred thousand years, yet we ran into it.

Ao Ling secretly rejoiced that Yun Zhi was on her side. Such combat prowess would have been unbeatable even in the ancient era, capable of rivaling Everlasting-jiejie. freewebnovel.com

Man Gu let out an emotional sigh. Traveling with Brother Lu and Brother Meng can truly broaden my horizons.

True Lord Horse felt he shouldn’t have come to the birthday banquet. Or rather, the moment I saw Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou at the banquet, I should have turned tail and fled.

The East Sea has been calm for tens of thousands of years. As soon as Lu Yang and the others arrived, they turned the entire place upside down—first with Ancient Ancestor Ao Ling’s resurrection, then with an immortal making an appearance.

“Looking at things now, it appears that it doesn’t matter whether I cultivate or not.” Originally, True Lord Horse felt that he needed to cultivate diligently, reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage as soon as possible, and become a qualified guardian.

But now, I’m afraid that even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator isn’t qualified to be a guardian.

The birthday star, the Old Dragon Emperor, stepped forward and cupped his fists toward the crowd. “Dear guests, due to the unforeseen events today, we are unable to continue hosting everyone. We ask for your understanding.”

The Dragon Tribe truly couldn’t host the crowd anymore. Having undergone a battle between three immortals and a clash between two immortals, the Dragon Palace had been flattened and reduced to rubble. Gold, silver, and jewels were scattered across the trenches at the bottom of the sea. Who knew how long it would take to rebuild the Dragon Palace?

However, this wouldn’t affect the Dragon Tribe’s status as the hegemon of the East Sea. With Ao Ling’s return, their standing would only be greater than before.

Originally, the crowd wanted to pay their respects to Ao Ling. But since the Old Dragon Emperor had personally stepped forward to chase them away, staying on shamelessly would likely yield no results, so they reluctantly abandoned the idea. Even the Black Feather Venerable Lord, who was enjoying the show, was dragged away by Chieftain Xiao.

As the crowd departed, only the Dragon Tribe, the Dao-Seeking Sect members, and Young Creed Leader Lu remained.

“Ancient Ancestor, I didn’t expect you to also be part of the Heavenly Court,” Ao Ya said excitedly, displaying much admiration for Ao Ling.

This is the number one in combat prowess among half-immortals, the pride of our Dragon Tribe!

“Ao Ya pays respects to the Ancient Ancestor and Senior Lu.

“Allow me to introduce—this is my Dao partner, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, Fang Wuya.” Ao Ya was open-minded and wasn’t particular about wedding rituals. Since the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had dual-cultivated with her, he was her Dao partner.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had no choice but to cup his fists. “Junior Fang Wuya pays respects to the Dragon Ancient Ancestor.”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord and Ao Ling were both half-immortals and could address each other as fellow Daoists. Although he referred to himself as a junior, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord felt pleased inwardly.

Meng Jingzhou shot a disdainful glance at the Vast Sea Daoist Lord. Founding Ancestor, you can barely keep that smile off your face, yet you still say you envy my Single’s Spirit Root?

“Wuya, you haven’t finished paying your respects,” Ao Ya whispered to the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord wore a puzzled expression. Who else do I need to bow to?

Ao Ya subtly nudged her chin toward Young Creed Leader Lu. This is the Ancient Ancestor’s senior brother. In terms of seniority, he is also our senior.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s face darkened.

Me, bow to him?

Ao Ya kept urging him. Succumbing to her pressure, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had no choice but to force a stiff smile and bow to Young Creed Leader Lu. “Junior Fang Wuya pays respects to Young Creed Leader Lu.”

Lu Yang felt that he would have interesting times ahead once he returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Ancient Ancestor, our tribe still has two Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Would it be convenient for you to meet them?” the Old Dragon Emperor asked cautiously, observing Ao Ling’s expression.

An opportunity to have an audience with Ao Ling was rare. If those two old ancestors missed this chance due to slumber, the Old Dragon Emperor would feel regret on their behalf.

“There are more Transcendent Tribulation cultivators? Seems like you’ve been doing alright in the East Sea,” Ao Ling remarked with slight surprise. Although the Dragon Tribe lacked half-immortals, having five Transcendent Tribulation cultivators already placed them among the top-tier factions.

In Lu Yang’s impression, only Great Xia’s imperial court had more Transcendent Tribulation cultivators than the Dragon Tribe.

Oh, wait, now there’s also the Demon Kingdom.

Having obtained Ao Ling’s consent, the Old Dragon Emperor hurried to the depths of the Dragon Palace to awaken the two slumbering old ancestors. They were from twenty thousand and thirty thousand years ago respectively, and were part of the Dragon Tribe’s most pivotal foundations.

The Old Dragon Emperor cleared away the debris from the ruins and entered an undersea chamber. Inside were three crystal casings. One of them was empty; this was where Ao Ya had resided. Within the other two crystal casings lay two Dragon tribesmen in human form.

The Old Dragon Emperor activated a secret spell, producing resonance with the patterns on the crystals.

Hummm—

As the resonance synchronized, the crystals bloomed like flowers. The two Dragon old ancestors slowly stirred awake.

“Who awakened us? Has the Dragon Tribe encountered a life-and-death crisis?”

According to ancestral rules, they were only to be awakened when the Dragon Tribe faced an existential threat.

The Old Dragon Emperor replied respectfully, “Old ancestors, the Dragon Tribe currently faces no crisis. It is simply that someone wishes to meet you both, and hence we have awakened you two.”

The two old ancestors flared up in anger. “Preposterous! What is our status? How could we be summoned for an audience with anyone?!”

“It’s me.” Ao Ling gazed calmly at the two Transcendent Tribulation true dragons.

“Who are you...” The two old ancestors instinctively began to reprimand, but when they turned and saw Ao Ling, they looked as if they had seen a ghost, their hearts nearly stopping from fright.

“Ao—Ao—Ao—Ao—Ao—Ao Ling Ancient Ancestor?!”

To be honest, if Lu Yang hadn’t heard the latter part, he would have thought they were just howling “ow-ow.”

“Do you have any objections?”

The two old ancestors hastily clambered out of their crystals, offering apologetic smiles. “Ancient Ancestor, it is our great honor that you wish to meet with us juniors. If anyone has any objections, your juniors will beat them to death!”

Seeing her descendants so lively and vigorous put Ao Ling in a good mood.

The Old Dragon Emperor turned to the two old ancestors with a beaming smile. “Old ancestors, the Ancient Ancestor simply wished to see you both, nothing more. You two can go back to sleep now.”

The two old ancestors glared furiously at the Old Dragon Emperor. Having learned that the Ancient Ancestor has awakened, who the hell could sleep after that?

“I will be returning to the Heavenly Court for a while. After I’ve met with some acquaintances, I will come back,” Ao Ling informed them.

She didn’t linger long in the Dragon Tribe, departing with Young Creed Leader Lu.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord bid goodbye to Ao Ya reluctantly and led the Dao-Seeking Sect members back.

The two parties separated at the Dragon Palace. After they left the palace grounds, they reconvened, and Lu Yang retrieved his clone.

Ao Ling had heard much from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, most of it related to the Dao-Seeking Sect, so she very much wanted to see this sect that her Everlasting-jiejie praised so effusively.

A graceful figure returned. Noticing her, Lu Yang promptly stepped forth and bowed. “Big Senior Sister, you’re back. That person...”

Yun Zhi’s tone was calm. “Severely wounded, then fled.”

“Little Junior Brother, Senior Ao Ling, you two come with me for a moment. Tell me more about the person I fought with.”

I want to know where this “Huang Doudou” popped out from.

Watching the receding backs of the three, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord felt somewhat dazed.

He recalled his trip to the East Sea carefully. First, I had helped Lu Yang stage an act, then I suffered a blow from an immortal, and in the end, I became Lu Yang’s junior for no reason?

Shouldn’t I have been able to swagger through the East Sea unimpeded?

Chapter 799: Dai Bufan: Didn’t You All Say You Went to the East Sea Just to Have Fun?

On a deserted island, four figures formed a circle, each sitting on a throne.

These four figures possessed terrifying strength, their average power verging infinitely close to that of an immortal.

Yun Zhi listened quietly to the accounts of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Ao Ling, and Lu Yang, then calmly summarized. “In other words, the Four Ancient Immortals originally intended to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, but through some twist of fate, they somehow ended up creating a ‘Senior Immortal Fairy’ who possessed the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit? And this person is highly likely the very immortal who deliberately concealed information about the Ember Legacy Dynasty?”

A strange expression crossed Yun Zhi’s face. Little Junior Brother had promised earnestly back then that he would absolutely not involve himself in matters of the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

Only a month has passed. How has he even managed to find the immortal who hid information about the Ember Legacy Dynasty?

“Lass Yun, this really can’t be blamed on me. The fog suddenly enveloped us. This immortal had no idea that the Dragon-Patterned Bracelet we stumbled upon was the key to opening the Dragon Pearl. I just saw that it belonged to Xiao Ling and asked the Second-in-Command to pick it up.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke up for Lu Yang in the name of justice. She didn’t mention a word about her and Lu Yang exploring the remnant immortal background a second time at night.

Yun Zhi showed no surprise at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s answer. “Who taught you to say that?”

“Second-in-Command.”

Yun Zhi shot a frosty glance at Lu Yang but said nothing.

Lu Yang felt that he could no longer collude with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy on alibis. It’s far too easy for her to give me away.

Ao Ling had been sitting all this time quietly. She glanced at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy on her left, then at Yun Zhi on her right, and let out a puzzled sound. “Hmm? Strange. Why do I feel like the two of you are somewhat alike?”

Lu Yang felt that Ao Ling’s eyesight might be failing. Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Big Senior Sister are peerless beauties in their own right, one is rather dim-witted, while the other is brilliantly clever. Just what similarity could you see?

“It’s not about looks. Aiya, I can’t put a finger on it. Anyway, I just have this feeling you two are somewhat alike.” Ao Ling didn’t know how to explain it either.

Yun Zhi said calmly, “Perhaps you are mistaken, Senior Ao Ling. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy and I share no similarities.”

“Is that so?” Ao Ling couldn’t help but feel her intuition was correct.

“You’re just mistaken.”

“Alright then.”

The four of them returned to discussing the main topic.

“Judging by Hui Doudou’s methods, anyone aware of her existence becomes her target for elimination,” Lu Yang mused.

“Wait, wait! Why are you calling her Hui Doudou?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was displeased with Lu Yang’s naming choice.

Yun Zhi also felt that the name lacked a sense of intimidation. It doesn’t sound like a powerful being’s name at all.

“Then what should we call her? Silent Annihilation Immortal?” Lu Yang felt troubled. We need a codename for discussion.

“No way, no way! How could you give her such an imposing name?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy objected again. This honorific title of “Silent Annihilation Immortal” overshadows my own honorific title.

Lu Yang turned to Ao Ling. “Senior, did Hui Doudou have a name during the Ember Legacy Dynasty?”

Ao Ling replied seriously, “In the Ember Legacy Dynasty, she was the ruler of the Heavenly Court and had no name. But from a functional standpoint, since her existence was for the purpose of resurrecting Everlasting-jiejie, calling her ‘Huang Doudou’ would also be acceptable.”

“Then let’s just call her Hui Doudou then.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hurriedly concluded the matter.

Yun Zhi appeared pensive. “That is to say that I’ve also become one of her targets for elimination.”

Lu Yang analyzed it carefully. It seems all four of us here are in danger... Wait, that isn’t right. Big Senior Sister could defeat Hui Doudou, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could resurrect, and Senior Ao Ling has the Dragon-Pattern Bracelet as defense—doesn’t that mean I’m in the most danger?!

Lu Yang prayed that Hui Doudou’s temperament was like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s, preferring to challenge the strong. Please don’t be like me and only like to fight those who are weaker than myself.

“Senior Ao Ling, if you trust me, you could hand the Dragon-Patterned Bracelet to me. I know someone who can replenish its energy.”

“Here.” Ao Ling naturally trusted Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi stowed the bracelet away properly.

“Speaking of which, my husband never told me that you are from the Jiao-Folk Tribe, Everlasting-jiejie.” Ao Ling smiled as she watched the half-fish, half-human Everlasting Immortal Fairy lounging on the throne.

Since the start of their East Sea journey, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had maintained her mermaid form.

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, why don’t you just change back? While you’re at it, please also discharge the seawater from my mind.

~~~

Originally, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord could have directly led everyone back to the Dao-Seeking Sect. However, considering that Lu Yang and the others only had records of leaving Great Xia but none of returning, he figured it would be hard to explain, so he instead set them down to let them register.

Yun Zhi and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had been teleported back through the Space Incipient Dao Fruit, leaving no exit records, so they naturally didn’t need to go through entry procedures.

As for Ao Ling, her special identity made it inconvenient for her to appear in public.

After Lu Yang and the other four completed the procedures, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord crossed the border and opened a spatial channel. On the other end lay the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Yun Zhi instructed, “Quite a few events transpired in the East Sea. Junior Brother Dai is in charge of intelligence; he likely isn’t aware of the affairs in the East Sea yet. Little Junior Brother, since the five of you experienced them firsthand, do go and inform Junior Brother Dai.”

“Alright!”

Yun Zhi invited Ao Ling to have a seat at Heaven’s Gate Peak, while Lu Yang and the others excitedly headed straight for the Great Mission Hall.

~~~

As the five frequented the Great Mission Hall, they easily found Dai Bufan’s room.

“Senior Brother Dai, are you in?” Lu Yang knocked on the door lightly.

“Come in.”

Seeing all five of them enter, Dai Bufan smiled. “Didn’t you guys follow the old horse to the East Sea to have fun? Back so soon? Did the Vast Sea Daoist Lord bring you back?” He had heard that Lu Yang was kidnapped by a Dragon Pearl and that the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had gone to the East Sea to find him.

Lu Yang nodded. It was indeed the Vast Sea Daoist Lord who had brought them back.

Noticing Lu Yang’s hesitant behavior, Dai Bufan teased, “Could it be you encountered something in the East Sea and want to tell me about it?”

“Yes.” Lu Yang was deliberating over his choice of words, trying his best to ensure Dai Bufan could accept the information smoothly.

Based on past experience, although Senior Brother Dai’s cultivation is high, his Dao heart can’t make it. He’s prone to being startled.

“Senior Brother Dai, here’s what happened. Originally, we went to the East Sea to have fun, and we experienced the culture and quite a few local specialties, like brawling and such. But rest assured, we were acting under the identities of Five-Elements Sect disciples at the time. We definitely didn’t tarnish the sect’s reputation.”

Lu Yang rubbed the back of his head, feeling rather embarrassed. “Later on...something unexpected happened. I accidentally awakened the Dragon Ancient Ancestor, Ao Ling. Senior Ao Ling insisted on calling me ‘senior brother,’ and even the Vast Sea Daoist Lord ended up calling me ‘senior.’

“The Three Mountains Daoist Priest of Penglai Island wanted to take over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body, but fortunately, Senior Ao Ling stopped him. Afterward, the Mountain-River Lord of Great Qian showed up. Senior Ao Ling fought both of them alone and gave them a beating.

“After that, an immortal suddenly appeared and attacked Ao Ling. The attack didn’t kill Ao Ling but instead killed the Three Mountains Daoist Priest and the Mountain-River Lord. freewebnovel.com

“Seeing that no one could defeat this immortal, Big Senior Sister stepped in to help and engaged in a great battle with that immortal.”

Lu Yang sighed. “It’s just that we didn’t manage to capture that immortal. She was left severely injured, but we let her escape. It’s a real pity.”

After listening, Dai Bufan laughed heartily. “Junior Brother Lu, you really know how to joke. Your imagination is truly vivid.”

“Senior Brother Dai, if you don’t believe me, Senior Ao Ling is right here in our sect and having tea with Big Senior Sister. She can attest to what I’m saying.”

Dai Bufan wore a smile, but his eyes were vacant, as if his expression had frozen in that moment.

“Senior Brother Dai? Senior Brother Dai?” Lu Yang called twice but received no response. Curious, he waved his hand in front of Dai Bufan’s face.

Still no reaction.

Lu Yang gingerly poked Dai Bufan’s shoulder. The latter’s upper body swayed a couple of times before he slumped forward onto the table with a thud, giving Lu Yang a huge fright.

Lu Yang hissed. I thought I’d been subtle enough. Why does Senior Brother Dai still have such a dramatic reaction?

Chapter 800: Junior Brother Gu, What Insights Have You Gained From This?

“Senior Brother Dai, wake up, wake up.”

Dai Bufan faintly heard someone calling him.

Who’s calling me? So noisy.

Struggling to open his eyes, he saw Lu Yang’s large face extremely close to his, gazing at him earnestly.

Seeing that he had regained consciousness, Lu Yang’s large face moved slightly away.

Dai Bufan shook his head. I can’t help but feel like I’ve forgotten something. What happened before this? Why did I pass out?

“Ah, it’s Junior Brother Lu. What brings you here?”

Lu Yang gestured to the row of people behind him, each trussed up like zongzi rice dumplings.

Lu Yang boasted to Dai Bufan, smiling somewhat sheepishly. “Senior Brother Dai, I just went out to have some fun, and I accidentally captured the Four Ancient Immortals, all the slumbering immortals from antiquity, the founding Qian emperor, the founding Yu Emperor, the first Imperial Preceptor, the founding Xia Emperor... With this, victory will definitely belong to our Dao-Seeking Sect in the Battle of the Great Era!”

“What?!”

Dai Bufan’s eyes flew open. He bolted upright, eyes wide and round, staring at Lu Yang’s detestable, large face.

He looked at Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and the others in bewilderment. The row of ancient immortals trussed up like zongzi had all vanished.

“So it was a dream, just a dream...” A chill ran down Dai Bufan’s spine as he recalled the scenes in the dream. He was relieved that it had been a false alarm.

First Elder excelled in dreamscapes, and Dai Bufan himself knew some dreamscape spells. It had been centuries since he last had a nightmare.

“Senior Brother Dai, are you alright?” Lu Yang asked with concern. Senior Brother Dai, your Dao heart really can’t make it. This is hardly anything. If I weren’t worried about putting you on the hit list, I would have told you about Hui Doudou’s identity.

As Dai Bufan’s memories gradually returned, he recalled what Lu Yang had said before he fainted.

Lu Yang, you kid really have a knack for stirring things up. It’s said that the East Sea has no half-immortals. Yet as soon as you went there, not only did you give the East Sea a half-immortal, but you also got two half-immortals killed there.

As for the immortal battle, it’s something that hasn’t occurred in three hundred thousand years.

“Any single one of the events that transpired in the East Sea could earn a place in the annals of history. And you’re now telling me that all of these incidents are related to you?”

Lu Yang felt rather bashful, not expecting Dai Bufan’s compliment. “It’s not quite as impressive as you make it sound...”

Dai Bufan forcibly stabilized his Dao heart. “All of you, tell me properly. How did you go from a leisurely two-day trip to the East Sea to triggering a great immortal battle in the East Sea?”

Lu Yang recounted most of the events as the primary firsthand witness who personally experienced everything, while Meng Jingzhou and the others provided supplementary details.

Only then did Dai Bufan straighten out the sequence of events. According to the accounts of the five, the East Sea affairs truly can’t be blamed on Lu Yang. It was simply a problem of luck.

From an intelligence standpoint, this was priceless information. Dai Bufan dared say the East Sea matters would shock the entire cultivation world, but only Lu Yang and his companions knew the full story behind them; others only saw the surface.

From the standpoint of the supervisor of the Great Mission Hall, Dai Bufan simply wanted Lu Yang to take over his position.

Dai Bufan held his forehead, feeling a headache coming on. He shooed the five away as though he was swatting flies. “Alright, alright, I know what happened. Let me have some peace and quiet.”

I need to properly digest the intelligence about the East Sea.

After Lu Yang and the other four left, Dai Bufan sat cross-legged, steadying his breathing. He replayed the East Sea events repeatedly in his mind, finally erupting with a furious roar.

“Even if it was just luck, isn’t this whole thing just too damn outrageous?!”

Boom!

In his rage, Dai Bufan’s aura shot skyward. In one go, he advanced to the Intermediate Fusion Stage!

~~~

A month had passed since the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance trials. The four newly recruited disciples had each become disciples under various elders.

The Innate Daoist Priest became the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s disciple; Gu Junye became First Elder’s disciple; Zhou Xing’er became Grandpa Ba’s disciple; Zhuang Ping became Fourth Elder’s disciple.

First Elder was currently lying in some random coffin, so Dai Bufan had no choice but to take on the role of his shifu, instructing Gu Junye in a certain clearing on the back mountain.

Perfect for a change of mood, he thought.

“Our lineage oversees both the Great Mission Hall and the enforcement of sect discipline. The most important thing is to avoid stirring up trouble. Since you have joined our lineage, you must abide by the rules. Remember: Do not stir up trouble.”

“Understood, Senior Brother,” Gu Junye replied, obediently sitting across from him and listening to him teach.

“As for a prime example of what not to do, it’s that kid, Lu Yang. Whenever he goes out on a mission, he’s bound to stir up something. At the start, it wasn’t so bad—he just joined the Everlasting Creed and such. Later, he attended the Qing Province Grand Ceremony and encountered two archaic Fusion cultivators and one archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. After that, he went to the Wilderness Province and encountered three archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivators... Not long ago, he returned from the East Sea. The events there are inextricably linked to him as well.”

Dai Bufan enumerated Lu Yang’s inexplicable connections with high-level cultivators. Every time Lu Yang returned, his harvest was enough to scare Dai Bufan half to death.

“Junior Brother Gu, tell me, what insight have you gained from this?”

Gu Junye’s eyes shone brightly. “Such is how a true man ought to be!”

Dai Bufan, “...”

Is it too late to get a different junior brother now?

~~~

When Lu Yang returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak, he saw Yun Zhi and Ao Ling having tea. Ao Ling had one leg crossed over the other, appearing quite unrestrained.

“Our sect already has two guest elders: Senior Immortal Fairy and Senior Lianyi. I wonder if you might be interested in becoming a guest elder of our sect, Senior Ao Ling.”

“Damn it! Lianyi got ahead of me again,” Ao Ling grumbled with regret. Why is it Jiang Lianyi who woke first and not me?

Falling a single step behind means falling behind everywhere. Even if I become a guest elder now, there would still be a Jiang Lianyi standing between me and Everlasting-jiejie.

“Then what benefits do I get for becoming a guest elder?”

“There are naturally many benefits to being a guest elder. For example, if there is anything in our sect that catches your eye, you may feel free to take it, Senior.”

“Oh? There are such perks?” Ao Ling gaze fell upon Lu Yang, who had just arrived, and a smile of keen interest spread across her face.

Lu Yang felt an ominous feeling well up within him.

“Little Junior Brother is not a thing,” Yun Zhi reminded. “However, our sect has captured several half-immortals and confiscated their assets. These are all stored in the treasury now. You may choose one item you like from among them.”

With Lu Yang acting as bait to hook a whole bunch of half-immortals, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s wealth and foundation now surpassed even that of the Dragon Tribe.

Yun Zhi continued, “Alternatively, you can make contributions to the sect, earn contributions, and use these points to exchange for the ‘Dao-Seeking Sect Leader One-Day Experience,’ temporarily becoming the sect leader. Everyone in the sect must obey the acting sect leader’s commands.”

“Even guest elders are no exception?”

“Guest elders are no exception.”

Ao Ling slapped her thigh. “I’ll do it!”

“Then can I also earn contribution points?” Hearing Yun Zhi’s words, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly remembered she hadn’t received any contribution points in a long while.

Yun Zhi replied, “Senior Immortal Fairy, you have made indelible contributions to the sect. Naturally, you have earned contribution points.”

“Then I want to redeem the ‘Dao-Seeking Sect Leader One-Day Experience!’” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes gleamed.

Yun Zhi was not surprised. “What is the duration you wish to redeem, Immortal Fairy? One or two years...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had contributed greatly to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s capture of half-immortals, which meant her contribution points were as vast as the ocean.

“One year will do.”

Yun Zhi nodded. “In that case, starting from today...”

“Wait! This immortal is just redeeming it in advance. I don’t want to be the acting sect leader yet.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recalled the previous two times she immediately became the acting sect leader. One involved organizing the exchange with the Five-Elements Sect, and the other involved organizing the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000th anniversary celebration.

Both were fraught with difficulties. If I hadn’t had Lu Yang as my golden finger cheat, I might not have made it through those two challenges.

This time, I must pick a favorable time to become the acting sect leader.

It was Yun Zhi’s turn to be stunned. She didn’t expect the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s intelligence to have improved by leaps and bounds without her noticing.

Chapter 801: Fierce Contention for the Position of Acting Sect Leader

For the past three hundred thousand years, battles between immortals were not unheard of, but one that occurred before the public was unprecedented.

The events of the East Sea swept through like a hurricane, reaching every street and alley in the shortest possible time. freewebnovel.com

“Who would have thought! It hasn’t been long since the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor awakened, and now even the Dragon Ancient Ancestor has revived!”

“Doesn’t this mean that both of the Qilin Immortal’s wives have appeared?”

“I heard it was the Three Mountains Daoist Priest who tracked down the Dragon Ancient Ancestor’s whereabouts. He presented her as a gift at the birthday banquet to surprise the Old Dragon Emperor.”

“Strange. Why did I hear that the Three Mountains Daoist Priest wanted to take over the Old Dragon Emperor’s body, but something went wrong in the middle? The ambush failed, stopped by the Dragon Ancient Ancestor.”

“That’s what I heard too. Otherwise, how did they end up fighting later?”

“The Dragon Ancient Ancestor fought one against two, suppressing two half-immortals. Truly unbelievable.”

“Didn’t Supreme Lord Zhu Tian proclaim himself to be the number one below immortals? Could he have achieved that?”

“Not sure.”

“Who was that immortal who appeared later and tried to kill the Dragon Ancient Ancestor? They even fought with the Heavenly Court Creed Leader.”

“I heard the ancient Heavenly Court and the Four Ancient Immortals were opposing factions. Could that immortal have been one of the Four Ancient Immortals?”

“That doesn’t sound right. If it were one of the Four Ancient Immortals, would the Qilin Immortal have just stood by and watched?”

“Then who do you think it was?”

“It could be the founding Qian Emperor, the Midheaven Emperor-Lord.”

“That can’t be, right? Didn’t that immortal even cut down the Mountain-River Lord?”

“Maybe he had long found the Mountain-River Lord an eyesore. Cutting him down with one slash would be normal.”

“If you put it that way, it does make sense.”

Qiongqi Tribe.

Upon hearing the news of the Dragon Tribe’s appearance in the East Sea, Chieftain Jin immediately requested leave from the Taciturn Daoist Priest and hurried back to the Demon Region.

Before he entered the ancient tomb, he heard the furious voice of the Little Ancestor, Jin Caiwei.

“Damn it! Why are they popping out one after another?”

Chieftain Jin entered the tomb and saw the Little Ancestor so angry that her hair was standing on end, like a bristling kitten that no one could touch. The Qiongqi Tribe’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivator standing beside her didn’t know how to comfort her.

Even if he wanted to, there was no way he could comfort her. When Jiang Lianyi appeared, the Little Ancestor had lowered her goal from ranking among the top ten in the Battle of the Great Era to the top eleven. With Ao Ling’s appearance, she would have to lower it from the top eleven to the top twelve.

If a few more of the Little Ancestor’s acquaintances popped out, there would be no point in contending for the Great Era anymore.

Furthermore, he surmised there was another important reason for the Little Ancestor’s anger. Now that the Qilin Immortal’s two wives are awake, what place does that leave for her?

“Little Qu, why have you returned?” Jin Caiwei noticed Chieftain Jin Que.[1]

Chieftain Jin thought to himself, Isn’t it because I was worried you’d be enraged, Little Ancestor?

Of course, such words could not be spoken aloud.

“I’ve befriended a big brother in Great Xia. He is truly remarkable and has an extensive network of friends. You could say his connections span the entire cultivation world. All Fusion cultivators greet him warmly when they see him, and he enjoys great relations with people.” Chieftain Jin gave a thumbs-up, full of praise for his big brother, the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“Relying on his connections, I can establish contact with the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect has the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, a half-immortal who wields the Space Incipient Dao Fruit. His prowess is first-rate even among half-immortals. Little Ancestor, what do you think about forming an alliance with the Dao-Seeking Sect? A union of two powerful forces would allow us to carve out a place in the Battle of the Great Era!

“Moreover, one more friend means one less enemy. Having one less enemy in the future is always good.” This was an insight that Chieftain Jin had inferred through backward induction.

Jin Caiwei fell silent. Little Que’s proposal is not without merit.

But she was used to acting alone and was reluctant to collaborate with others. “Allow me to think it over carefully.”

~~~

Zhu Tian sat upon the monarch chair, his face twisted with conflict.

“How has even Big Sister Ao Ling come back to life? Is it really so difficult for me to become the overlord?”

He began seriously contemplating the feasibility of simply going back to sleep for another long stretch.

“Or should I try harder to curry favor with Big Brother Lu?

“I wonder what Big Brother Lu lacks. Should I try sending him a couple of beauties?”

~~~

While the world was abuzz with speculation about Ao Ling’s whereabouts and the identities of the immortals from the battle, a figure quietly arrived at the Dao-Seeking Sect’s mountain gate.

That figure stepped through the gate, frightening away the River Spirit with a mere glance, and successfully entered the Dao-Seeking Sect’s interior.

That figure ascended to the summit of Heaven’s Gate Peak with practiced ease and saw Lu Yang cultivating and Ao Ling lying on the ground, asleep while hugging her own tail.

That figure raised a hand, terrifying spirit power accumulating in their palm.

Ao Ling sensed someone attempting an ambush, and her eyes flew open. With a kip-up, she rose and delivered a palm strike toward that figure.

Their palms collided, stirring up a gust of wind that blew back the figure’s cloak, revealing a face extremely familiar to Lu Yang.

“Senior Lianyi!”

“Jiang Lianyi, I knew it was you! No one else would sneak up so stealthily to ambush me!” Ao Ling laughed and scolded.

Jiang Lianyi pretended as if she hadn’t seen Ao Ling and bowed to Lu Yang. “Greetings, Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

Jiang Lianyi had guessed that Ao Ling would certainly be at the Dao-Seeking Sect at this time. She turned to Ao Ling, an ambiguous smile playing on her lips. “Junior Sister Little Ling, how dare you address your senior sister by her name? That’s highly improper.”

Ao Ling was unmoved. “You and I are both unofficial disciples. Why bother distinguishing between senior and junior sister?”

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you be the judge! I became your junior sister first, so I should be Little Ling’s senior sister!”

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you tell her! Neither Lianyi nor I am qualified to be Everlasting-jiejie’s disciple. Calling you ‘senior brother’ is already reaching above our station. We shouldn’t be distinguishing between senior and junior brother in the first place, right?!”

Lu Yang felt a headache coming on. Senior Ao Ling, please don’t say things like that. I’m scared.

He desperately wished Yun Zhi would return, but unfortunately, she had gone to repair the Dragon-Patterned Bracelet and wouldn’t be back for a while.

Fortunately, although Yun Zhi wasn’t present, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was around to mediate.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy drifted out from the mental space to act as a peacemaker. “Since ancient times, the strong have reigned supreme. How about you two fight it out? Whoever wins becomes the senior sister. How’s that?”

Lu Yang broke out in a cold sweat. Immortal Fairy, it would have been better if you hadn’t come out.

“Our Everlasting Lineage values harmony above all. There’s no need to resort to violence,” Lu Yang hastily persuaded them. If these two ancestors start fighting within the Dao-Seeking Sect, even Founding Ancestor Vast Sea wouldn’t be able to stop them when he arrives. He might even get caught in a dragon-phoenix combo beating.

As their “senior brother,” Lu Yang held considerable weight in the hearts of the Dragon and Phoenix ancient ancestors. Since he advised against fighting, they would not fight.

Jiang Lianyi still had a trump card. She reckoned Ao Ling must also have become a guest elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect. “Guest Elder Ao, I became a guest elder before you. According to sect custom, you should address me as senior sister.”

Ao Ling had long anticipated that Jiang Lianyi would pull this move. She sneered. “You don’t know yet, do you? I can become the acting sect leader through exchanging contribution points. Even you, Guest Elder Jiang, would have to obey this acting sect leader’s commands!”

Jiang Lianyi was taken aback. She truly hadn’t known that one could exchange contribution points for becoming the acting sect leader. “Everlasting-jiejie, how do I earn contribution points?” She turned to ask the expert.

“Contribution points, as the name implies, are earned by contributing to our sect. For example, this immortal once eliminated a wicked Fusion cultivator and served as acting sect leader for three days.”

Jiang Lianyi’s eyes lit up at this. That doesn’t sound difficult. “When I return, I’ll have Zhu Tian go capture a couple of wicked Fusion cultivators and present them to Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

Ao Ling snorted coldly. As if I can’t do the same. “I’ll go to the East Sea and have the Dragon Tribe capture a couple of archaic Fusion cultivators to present to Senior Brother Lu Yang!”

“I can also have Zhu Tian go capture ten Fusion cultivators!”

“I can also capture ten Fusion cultivators!”

“I can capture archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivators!”

“I can also capture archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivators—and a pair at that!”

“I can have Zhu Tian present the entire Demon Region to Senior Brother Lu Yang!”

“I can also unify the East Sea and present it to Senior Brother Lu Yang!”

Lu Yang listened to them, utterly dumbfounded. How did I suddenly become the ruler of both the Demon Region and the East Sea just from this conversation?

Chapter 802: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Forest of Formidable Subordinates and Troops

Lu Yang felt that he was a mere Intermediate Nascent Soul cultivator and truly could not shoulder the responsibilities of being the ruler of both the Demon Region and the East Sea.

“Aiya, they’re just tokens of Little Ling’s and Lianyi’s heartfelt sentiments. It’s merely the Demon Region and the East Sea; just accept them.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved it off breezily. “If you really don’t dare to take them, this immortal can accept them on your behalf.”

Clearly, while Lu Yang dared not accept them, there were plenty of others who would dare to.

Lu Yang ruminated over it. The Everlasting is the ruler of the Heavenly Court and the founding emperor of the Great Dou Dynasty, now concurrently the ruler of both the Demon Region and the East Sea—the authority she wields is unrivalled.

“Immortal Fairy, even if you accept them, would you actually manage them?” Lu Yang recalled that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had only been in charge of the North Star due to her dislike for management in ancient times. Even that had been forced upon her by the Four Ancient Immortals.

Lu Yang suspected that forcing the North Star upon the Everlasting Immortal Fairy might have simply been to prevent her from running everywhere aimlessly and to provide her a stable residence.

“What’s so difficult about management? I can have Little Ling and Lianyi manage the East Sea and the Demon Region.”

Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t know how to manage, she was brilliant at putting the right people to use.

“Everlasting-jiejie, could you let us see where you usually live?” Jiang Lianyi asked.

“Sure, sure!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy naturally agreed.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi each projected a wisp of spiritual consciousness, which darted into Lu Yang’s mental space.

“Come, come, treat this place like your own home. Sit wherever you like.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy enthusiastically hosted the two half-immortals.

She had long since drained the seawater from the mental space. Now, Lu Yang’s mental space had reverted to its original pink and tender appearance. Against a wall lay a bed, along with other furniture like tables, chairs, and benches.

Lu Yang watched all this silently.

Exactly whose mental space is this?

Only after sitting down did Jiang Lianyi remember that her purpose for coming wasn’t simply to meet Ao Ling. “Little Ling, just what happened with the immortal battle in the East Sea? Who is targeting you?”

Ao Ling frowned, pondering for a moment. “It’s quite complicated to explain this matter. If I tell you everything, you’ll be in danger too. Here’s what. I’ll tell you only the parts I can.

“Back then, after Hubby and the other three immortals fought the murderer, you entered a play-dead state, while I followed Hubby to establish the Ember Legacy Dynasty...”

“Hold on a moment.” Jiang Lianyi interrupted Ao Ling after just one sentence. “Didn’t we agree back then that we would both use the Play-Dead Technique?”

~~~

Great Xia Imperial Palace.

After Jiang Ping’an finished plowing with a hoe, he sat on a small stool to wipe his sweat and look up at the visitor. “Fellow Daoist Yun, what brings you here?”

Yun Zhi took out a palm-sized red package from her sleeve. Unwrapping the red cloth, she revealed an exquisitely crafted Dragon-Patterned Bracelet.

Jiang Ping’an was drawn to the bracelet’s design. “Hmm? What exquisite craftsmanship. Who refined this?”

“This is an immortal artifact refined by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. When its energy is fully charged, it can withstand several attacks from an immortal.”

“Ho, that’s an extraordinary item.” For an immortal artifact to reach this level, it could be considered the pinnacle. “I see the bracelet’s energy is depleted. You want me to recharge it?”

“That is my intention.”

Jiang Ping’an turned the Dragon-Patterned Bracelet over in his hands a couple of times. “Sure. Then allow me to study it.”

While examining it, Jiang Ping’an recalled the recent intelligence he had received and initiated a casual conversation. “Fellow Daoist Yun, who did you fight in the East Sea? Was it one of the Four Ancient Immortals?”

Due to the immortal trait of oblivion, the world could only remember that an immortal battle occurred in the East Sea but not recall the specifics.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “It was an ancient immortal, but not one of the Four Ancient Immortals. Her origins are not something that’s convenient to elaborate on. If you know too much, she will kill you too.”

“Oh? Do you think I am inferior to that immortal?” Jiang Ping’an’s tone carried a faint trace of pride.

As the founding emperor, his contributions to Great Xia’s stability over a hundred thousand years were immense. This was due to both his wise strategies and his profound cultivation.

Yun Zhi nodded. “It’s true that you can’t defeat her.”

“Alright then, if you say so.” Jiang Ping’an was like a wilted eggplant, lowering his head and accepting reality.

~~~

When Yun Zhi returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect with the fully recharged Dragon-Patterned Bracelet, she saw Lu Yang, Ao Ling, and Jiang Lianyi lying neatly on the ground in a row.

Yun Zhi knocked on Lu Yang’s forehead, knocking everyone out of his mental space.

“Big Senior Sister, you’re finally back!” Lu Yang was overjoyed to see Yun Zhi. Finally, there’s someone reliable to take charge. I really can’t handle the two ancestors alone, much less with the troublemaking Huang Doudou added to the mix.

Earlier, in the mental space, things had nearly come to blows twice.

Yun Zhi handed the Dragon-Patterned Bracelet to Ao Ling, then turned to Jiang Lianyi. “Senior Lianyi, did you come to see Senior Ao Ling?”

Jiang Lianyi snorted coldly. “Who cares about seeing her? I came to ask about intelligence regarding the East Sea.”

Yun Zhi simply uttered “oh” and didn’t comment further.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy excitedly emerged from Lu Yang’s body and began counting heads. “Me, Second-in-Command, Little Ling, Lianyi—mmm, everyone’s here!”

“What do you mean by ‘everyone’s here?’” Lu Yang’s mind hadn’t caught up.

“Our team to challenge Lass Yun is all here, obviously!”

Lu Yang, “...”

No, wait. Immortal Fairy, if you’re going to court death, could you please not drag me along?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy raised her hand. Although I haven’t yet recovered to my prime and can’t contend with Lass Yun alone, I now have Ao Ling and Lianyi assisting me, plus the Second-in-Command as my strategist. I can somewhat be considered to possess the means to fight Lass Yun.

Seeing this, Lu Yang hastily stopped the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who was about to swing her hand. “No, no, no! Immortal Fairy, calm down.”

“I am very calm, though,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy refuted loudly.

“No, no, no! Think about it, Immortal Fairy. We—uh—you all want to fight Big Senior Sister, but not everyone’s here yet.”

“Not everyone’s here? Who else is there?”

Lu Yang kindly reminded her. “The Third-in-Command! As a half-immortal, he’s an integral combat firepower!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy slapped her forehead. “Oh right, I forgot about him.”

Heaven’s Gate Peak wasn’t far from the commercial district’s barbeque shop. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy could remotely control the Everlasting Immortal.

While the Everlasting Immortal was counting money at the barbeque shop, he sensed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s summons. It felt as though someone had grabbed the back of his clothes, and his body bent like a shrimp as he flew backward to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

Taking in the grand lineup at Heaven’s Gate Peak, the Everlasting Immortal was visibly stunned.

What’s going on here?

“Greetings, First-in-Command, Second-in-Command. First-in-Command, you called for me?” the Everlasting Immortal asked cautiously, a sense of foreboding welling up within him.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, stating with confidence. “This immortal has decided to crusade against Lass Yun today. A strategy has already been devised. As a member of our Everlasting Lineage, you must contribute.”

As the big boss, I naturally must reward and punish fairly. “How about this? This immortal will give you a chance to earn merit. You shall be the vanguard to test Lass Yun’s level. If you can defeat Lass Yun, the position of first-in-command will be yours!”

“Ah?”
